2. 现行治疗路径图 — CURRENT TREATMENT ALGORITHM (BMI ≥ 28) Treatment-Pathway Diagram

三级路径：① Lifestyle Intervention（生活方式干预：饮食与运动，一线治疗，适用于所有患者）→ ② Drug Therapy（药物治疗：满足条件时使用GLP-1 RA）→ ③ Bariatric Surgery（代谢手术：BMI≥37.5，或BMI≥32.5+合并症，用于难治性患者）。标题标注范围为“CHINA ADULT OBESITY (BMI ≥28)”。

为什么是“三级阶梯(step-care)”结构：这是慢性病管理里最标准的“阶梯式治疗(step therapy)”范式——先用风险最低、成本最低的干预(生活方式)，效果不足再升级到药物，药物仍不足再升级到手术。这个范式本身“无可指摘”，因为它符合医学伦理(优先选择风险收益比最好的方案)和大多数国家的临床指南通用逻辑。把这个图放在“四大障碍”之前，相当于先告诉读者：“GLP-1在这个体系里的位置是清楚的、有共识的——第二级、满足条件时使用”，为后面“问题不在于GLP-1该不该用，而在于‘满足条件’之后会发生什么”做铺垫。

“GLP-1 RA when criteria met” — 这句话里“criteria”指向哪里：这里的“criteria(标准)”直接回指Slide 4“INDUSTRY DEFINITION”大方框里的BMI门槛说明(“Wegovy≥ 30/≥27+; Mufengda/Feisumei≥28/≥24+”)——也就是说，“criteria met”不是一个抽象描述，而是Slide 4已经精确定义过的、“产品specific”的处方门槛。这一页用“criteria met”这个简洁的表达，是因为详细定义已经在Slide 4“用过一次”，这里不需要重复——体现了报告内部“定义只在第一次出现的地方详细展开，后续引用“的设计原则。

为什么手术门槛是“≥37.5或≥32.5+合并症”，而不是和药物门槛(≥28/≥24+)一致：这暴露了一个“空白区间”——BMI在28到37.5之间(或24/32.5之间)的患者，理论上“符合药物使用条件，但不符合手术条件”，这部分人群正是“Drug Therapy”这一级覆盖的核心人群，也是Slide 9流行病学漏斗里“~2亿肥胖人群(BMI≥28)”的主体。手术门槛设置得更高(37.5/32.5)，是因为手术属于“不可逆的侵入性治疗”，临床指南通常要求“更严重、且对其他治疗无效(refractory)”才考虑手术——这是医学伦理上的“风险匹配”，不是任意设定的数字。

Three-tier pathway: ① Lifestyle Intervention (diet & exercise, first-line, all patients) → ② Drug Therapy (GLP-1 RA when criteria met) → ③ Bariatric Surgery (BMI≥37.5, or BMI≥32.5+comorbidity, for refractory patients). Header scope: ‘CHINA ADULT OBESITY (BMI ≥28).’

Why a 3-tier ‘step-care’ structure: This is the most standard chronic-disease-management paradigm — ‘step therapy’: start with the lowest-risk, lowest-cost intervention (lifestyle), escalate to drugs if insufficient, then to surgery if still insufficient. The paradigm itself is ‘unimpeachable’ because it follows medical ethics (best risk-benefit ratio first) and the common logic of most national clinical guidelines. Placing this diagram BEFORE the ‘four barriers’ tells the reader upfront: ‘GLP-1’s position in this system is clear and consensus-based — tier 2, used when criteria are met’ — setting up the point that ‘the problem isn’t whether GLP-1 SHOULD be used, but what happens AFTER criteria are met.’

‘GLP-1 RA when criteria met’ — where do these ‘criteria’ point: ‘Criteria’ here refers directly back to Slide 4’s ‘INDUSTRY DEFINITION’ box (‘Wegovy ≥30/≥27+; Mufengda/Feisumei ≥28/≥24+’) — i.e., ‘criteria met’ isn’t an abstract phrase but the precise, product-specific prescribing thresholds already defined on Slide 4. This page uses the shorthand ‘criteria met’ because the detailed definition was already ‘used once’ on Slide 4 — reflecting the report’s internal design principle: define in full only at first occurrence, refer to it concisely thereafter.

Why is the surgery threshold (≥37.5 or ≥32.5+comorbidity) different from — and higher than — the drug threshold (≥28/≥24+): This exposes a ‘gap zone’ — patients with BMI between 28–37.5 (or 24–32.5) theoretically ‘meet drug criteria but not surgery criteria.’ This group is precisely the core population covered by ‘Drug Therapy,’ and the bulk of Slide 9’s ~200M BMI≥28 epidemiology-funnel population. The higher surgical threshold reflects medical ethics — surgery is irreversible/invasive, so guidelines typically require ‘more severe AND refractory to other treatments’ — a risk-matching principle, not an arbitrary number.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK“BMI在28-37.5之间是‘符合药物条件但不符合手术条件’的区间——这个区间的人群数量有多大？这是否就是你Slide 9市场模型分母的来源？两页之间有没有明确的数字对应关系？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER是的，这正是两页之间的一个重要‘接口’。Slide 9流行病学漏斗的起点是‘BMI≥28的中国成年人口(约2亿)’，这个分母在临床意义上对应的就是这一页‘Drug Therapy’这一级理论上覆盖的人群——也就是‘BMI≥28但尚未达到≥37.5手术标准(或没有合并症达到≥32.5手术标准)’的人群构成了这个分母的主体，加上一小部分‘BMI已经达到手术标准、但出于个人选择优先尝试药物治疗’的患者。我没有把这两页的数字做逐一交叉引用(比如‘Slide 6第②级=Slide 9分母’的明确标注)，这是这份报告在‘页面间数字一致性标注’上可以加强的一点——但概念上两者是同一个人群的不同描述角度：Slide 6描述的是‘这个人群在治疗路径中的位置’，Slide 9描述的是‘这个人群的规模和向下渗透的漏斗’。

EN： Yes — this is exactly an important 'interface' between the two pages. The starting point of Slide 9's epidemiology funnel is 'China's adult population with BMI≥28 (~200 million),' and clinically this denominator corresponds to the population that this page's 'Drug Therapy' tier theoretically covers — i.e., the bulk of that denominator is people with BMI≥28 who haven't yet reached the ≥37.5 surgical threshold (or ≥32.5 with comorbidity), plus a small group who DO meet the surgical threshold but choose to try drug therapy first. I haven't drawn an explicit cross-reference between the two pages' numbers (e.g., labeling 'Slide 6 tier ② = Slide 9 denominator'), which is an area where the report's cross-page numerical consistency could be tightened — but conceptually the two are different lenses on the same population: Slide 6 describes WHERE this population sits in the treatment pathway, while Slide 9 describes the SIZE of this population and how it narrows through the funnel.

3. 四大障碍总览 — 为什么是这4个、为什么是这个严重程度顺序 Four Barriers — Why These 4, Why This Severity Order

四大障碍及严重程度：① High Cost & No Reimbursement (CRITICAL) ② Injection Burden & Adherence (HIGH) ③ Weight Regain After Discontinuation (HIGH) ④ GI Side Effects & Tolerability (MODERATE)。

为什么是“4个”、且正好和Slide 4的“4个机制分类”“4层产业链子项”在数量上呼应：和Slide 4一样，“4”在视觉节奏上形成统一感，但更重要的是，这4个障碍在内容上构成一个MECE(互斥且完全穷尽)的‘患者旅程(patient journey)’切片：①发生在‘决定开始用药之前’(能不能负担)；②④发生在‘用药过程中’(打针频率、副作用)；③发生在‘停药之后’(体重反弹)。三个时间节点(用药前/用药中/用药后)，刚好用4个障碍覆盖——②和④都属于‘用药中’，但分别对应‘行为负担(注射)’和‘生理负担(副作用)’两个不同维度。

严重程度CRITICAL/HIGH/HIGH/MODERATE是怎么定的——这是这一页最容易被问‘方法论’的地方：这一页没有给出一个量化的‘评分公式’，严重程度更可能是基于‘对2025-2026年中国市场渗透率(0.8-1.2%)的解释力大小’来排序的：①(成本/医保)被定为CRITICAL，因为它直接决定了‘绝大多数潜在患者在第一步就被筛掉’——这是‘漏斗最上游、收窄幅度最大’的一环，直接对应Slide 3 Model假设里‘诊断就医率17-23%’和‘渗透率0.8-1.2%’这两个最关键乘数背后的现实原因。②③被定为HIGH，因为它们影响的是‘已经进入治疗的患者能否持续产生收入(LTV Lifetime Value，客户生命周期价值。这个患者作为一个长期治疗用户，整个治疗周期带来的收入价值。)’——但前提是患者已经跨过了①这道门槛，所以影响范围比①小。④被定为MODERATE，因为GI副作用‘可管理’(剂量滴定可以缓解)，且并非‘决定要不要开始用药’的首要考量。

Four barriers and severities: ① High Cost & No Reimbursement (CRITICAL) ② Injection Burden & Adherence (HIGH) ③ Weight Regain After Discontinuation (HIGH) ④ GI Side Effects & Tolerability (MODERATE).

Why ‘4’, echoing Slide 4’s ‘4 mechanism categories’ and ‘4 sub-items per value-chain layer’: As with Slide 4, ‘4’ creates visual rhythm consistency, but more importantly these 4 barriers form a MECE slice of the ‘patient journey’: ① occurs ‘before starting treatment’ (can they afford it); ②④ occur ‘during treatment’ (injection frequency, side effects); ③ occurs ‘after stopping’ (weight regain). Three time-points (before/during/after) are covered by 4 barriers — ② and ④ are both ‘during,’ but correspond to different dimensions: ‘behavioral burden (injection)’ vs. ‘physiological burden (side effects).’

How CRITICAL/HIGH/HIGH/MODERATE were determined — the most likely methodology-question on this page: No quantitative scoring formula is given. Severity is most plausibly ranked by ‘how much each barrier explains the 0.8–1.2% China penetration rate (Slide 3’s Model assumption).’ ① (cost/reimbursement) is CRITICAL because it determines whether ‘most potential patients are filtered out at the very first step’ — the largest narrowing point in the funnel, directly underlying the ‘17–23% diagnosis-seeking rate’ and ‘0.8–1.2% penetration’ multipliers in Slide 3. ②③ are HIGH because they affect whether patients ALREADY in treatment continue generating revenue (LTV Lifetime Value, Customer lifetime value. The revenue generated by this patient as a long-term treatment recipient over the entire course of treatment.— but only AFTER clearing barrier ①, so their scope is narrower. ④ is MODERATE because GI effects are ‘manageable’ (dose titration mitigates them) and aren’t typically the PRIMARY consideration in deciding whether to start treatment.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK“严重程度的排序看起来是分析师主观判断，没有一个可验证的打分体系——这会不会被认为是‘拍脑袋’？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER这是一个公允的问题，我想坦诚回答。这4个标签确实不是来自一个外部发布的量化评分体系，而是分析师基于‘该障碍对当前渗透率的解释力’做出的定性判断——这一点应该被明确承认，不应该伪装成‘有客观公式’。但这个判断不是完全主观的，它有间接证据支持：①CRITICAL有Slide 9模型里‘渗透率仅0.8-1.2%’这个结果作为‘结果证据’——如果成本不是最大障碍，很难解释渗透率为何如此之低；②③HIGH有具体的量化数据支撑(52%停药率、>60%体重反弹)；④MODERATE虽然发生率不低(恶心44%)，但FDA标签数据本身也显示这是‘可通过剂量滴定管理’的不良反应，临床上很少单独导致‘完全不考虑用药’。所以严重程度是‘定性判断+间接量化证据的组合’，不是凭空打分——但我认同，如果要让这个分级更严谨，应该补充一个明确的评分维度说明(比如‘影响的患者比例 x 对该障碍的可解决程度’)。

EN： That's a fair question, and I'll answer honestly. These four severity labels don't come from an externally published quantitative scoring system — they're an analyst's qualitative judgment based on how much each barrier explains the current penetration rate, and that should be stated plainly rather than dressed up as an objective formula. But the judgment isn't purely subjective either — it's backed by indirect evidence: ① CRITICAL is supported by Slide 9's model output of 'penetration of only 0.8–1.2%' as outcome evidence — it's hard to explain such a low penetration rate if cost isn't the biggest barrier; ②③ HIGH are backed by specific quantitative data (52% discontinuation, >60% weight regain); ④ MODERATE, despite a non-trivial incidence rate (44% nausea), is — per the FDA label itself — an adverse effect that's manageable through dose titration and rarely on its own causes patients to rule out treatment entirely. So the severity ranking is a combination of qualitative judgment and indirect quantitative evidence, not an arbitrary score — though I'd agree that, to make this ranking more rigorous, it would help to add an explicit scoring dimension, such as 'share of patients affected × how solvable the barrier is.'

4. 障碍① High Cost & No Reimbursement (CRITICAL)

内容：Wegovy中国：高自费成本(起始剂量约CNY1,400，2024年11月上市价；截至2026年市场价格竞争仍在进行)。无肥胖适应症专属NRDL医保报销。准入受限(自费使用占主导)。解决方向：→国产生物类似药/同类药(2026+)、医保谈判、商业保险扩展。

“起始剂量约CNY1,400”与Slide 3 Model假设“年治疗费用CNY16,800起始剂量(Yicai 2024)”的关系——一个隐藏的内部一致性检验：CNY1,400 × 12(月) = CNY16,800。这两个数字在不同页面上分别出现，但彼此吻合——Slide 3的‘年治疗费用’假设，其实就是这一页‘月度自费成本’乘以12个月得到的。这是一个值得主动指出的‘内部一致性证据’：它说明Slide 3的Model假设不是凭空设定的，而是和Slide 6这里引用的‘真实市场价格(2024年11月Wegovy中国上市价)’是同一个数据源的不同呈现方式。如果面试官分别在两页问到这两个数字，能够主动指出‘这两个数字其实是同一个价格点的月度/年度表达，1400×12≈16,800’，会显得整份报告的数字体系是‘咬合的(internally consistent)’，而不是‘东拼西凑的’。

“market price competition ongoing as of 2026” — 为什么要加这句“价格竞争仍在进行”：这句话承认了‘价格不是静态的’——随着Slide 1时间线里‘6款产品在33个月内集中获批’，供给侧的竞争会对价格产生下行压力。这句话的作用是‘为Slide 3的416M模型里‘年治疗费用’这个乘数提供时间敏感性的预警’——如果未来价格下降(比如降到CNY10,000/年)，模型的市场规模(USD金额)会随之变化，即使‘渗透人数’不变。这是一个‘价格×数量=市场规模’公式里，‘价格’这一项本身是动态的、需要持续更新的提示。

“No obesity-specific NRDL reimbursement” — 和你之前讨论过的“Mufengda 2025年进入NRDL但仅限糖尿病适应症”是什么关系：这句话是‘行业层面的概括性陈述’——目前没有任何一款GLP-1产品的‘肥胖适应症’被纳入NRDL(国家医保药品目录)。Mufengda(穆峰达/替尔泊肽)虽然在2025年因糖尿病适应症进入NRDL，但这是‘同一分子、不同适应症’的医保状态——糖尿病适应症的处方可以报销，但如果医生开具的是‘肥胖/体重管理’适应症，仍然是自费。这构成了一个有意思的‘监管套利/灰色地带’讨论点：理论上，如果患者同时有2型糖尿病(适应症在NRDL内)和肥胖问题，处方时标注的适应症会直接影响是否能报销——这也是‘行为经济学’层面的一个潜在影响因素，但这一页没有展开讨论。

Content: Wegovy China — high out-of-pocket cost (starter-dose ~CNY1,400 at Nov 2024 launch; price competition ongoing as of 2026). No obesity-specific NRDL reimbursement. Access limits (out-of-pocket dominates). Solutions → domestic biosimilars (2026+), NRDL negotiation, commercial insurance expansion.

‘~CNY1,400 starter dose’ vs. Slide 3’s Model assumption ‘CNY16,800 annual cost, starter-dose (Yicai 2024)’ — a hidden internal-consistency check: CNY1,400 × 12 (months) = CNY16,800. These two numbers appear on different pages but reconcile — Slide 3’s ‘annual cost’ assumption is simply this page’s ‘monthly out-of-pocket cost’ × 12. This is worth proactively pointing out as evidence of internal consistency: Slide 3’s Model assumption isn’t arbitrary — it’s the same data point (Wegovy’s November 2024 China launch price) expressed monthly vs. annually. If asked about either number separately, noting ‘1,400×12≈16,800 — same price point, monthly vs. annual’ demonstrates the report’s numbers are internally coherent, not assembled piecemeal.

Why add ‘market price competition ongoing as of 2026’: This acknowledges price isn’t static — as Slide 1’s timeline shows 6 products approved within 33 months, supply-side competition will push prices down. This sentence pre-warns that Slide 3’s $416M model’s ‘annual cost’ multiplier is time-sensitive and needs updating — if future prices drop (e.g., to CNY10,000/year), the market-size figure (in USD) shifts even if the number of penetrated patients stays the same. A reminder that in ‘price × volume = market size,’ the ‘price’ term itself is dynamic.

‘No obesity-specific NRDL reimbursement’ vs. Mufengda’s 2025 NRDL entry for diabetes only: This is an industry-level generalization — no GLP-1 product’s OBESITY indication is currently in the NRDL. Mufengda (tirzepatide) entered the NRDL in 2025 for its diabetes indication, but that’s the reimbursement status of ‘the same molecule, a different indication’ — a diabetes prescription is reimbursable, but if a doctor prescribes it for ‘obesity/weight management,’ it remains self-pay. This raises an interesting ‘regulatory gray-zone’ discussion point: for a patient with both type-2 diabetes (NRDL-covered) and obesity, the INDICATION recorded on the prescription directly affects reimbursement — a behavioral-economics angle this page doesn’t elaborate on.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK“‘domestic biosimilars (2026+)’这个解决方向——国产‘生物类似药’对于GLP-1这种多肽药物来说，技术上现实吗？和Slide 1里提到的国产创新药(信尔美/Ecnoglutide)是同一概念吗？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER这里需要澄清一个术语问题——严格来说，‘biosimilar(生物类似药)’通常指‘原研生物药专利到期后，其他厂商生产的、与原研在质量/安全性/有效性上高度相似的版本’(比如司美格鲁肽专利到期后的仿制版本)。而Slide 1里的Mazdutide(信尔美)/Ecnoglutide属于‘国产创新药(domestically-developed novel molecules)’，是‘全新分子’，不是‘已上市分子的生物类似药’——这是两个不同的概念。这一页用‘domestic biosimilars’这个词，指的是‘未来(2026年后)，当司美格鲁肽等早期分子的专利逐步到期后，国产仿制/类似药将进入市场，进一步加剧价格竞争’——这是‘供给侧降价’的一个长期来源，和Slide 1的‘国产创新分子’是互补但不同的两条路径(创新药走‘差异化’，biosimilar走‘价格竞争’)。这一页没有区分这两者，是用词上可以更精确的地方——但‘通过更多供给(无论是创新药还是biosimilar)压低价格’这个逻辑本身是合理的。

EN： There's a terminology distinction worth clarifying first. Strictly speaking, a 'biosimilar' refers to a version made by another manufacturer after the originator biologic's patent expires, that's highly similar to the original in quality, safety, and efficacy — for example, a copycat version of semaglutide once its patent lapses. Mazdutide (IBI362) and Ecnoglutide on Slide 1, by contrast, are domestically-developed novel molecules — entirely new compounds, not biosimilars of an already-marketed molecule. Those are two different concepts. This page's use of 'domestic biosimilars' refers to a future scenario (post-2026) where, as patents on earlier molecules like semaglutide expire, domestic copycat/similar products enter the market and intensify price competition further — a long-run source of supply-side price pressure, complementary to but distinct from Slide 1's 'domestic novel molecules' (innovative drugs compete on differentiation, biosimilars compete on price). This page doesn't distinguish the two, which is an area where the wording could be more precise — but the underlying logic, that more supply, whether from novel drugs or biosimilars, pushes prices down, still holds.

5. 障碍② Injection Burden & Adherence (HIGH)

内容：需要每周一次皮下注射。国际真实世界证据中1年停药率约52%(Thomsen et al., EASD 2025; 丹麦)。中国specific数据不可得；由于肥胖适应症主要是自费，停药率可能有所不同。解决方向：→口服GLP-1制剂、长效注射剂、数字化依从性支持。

“Weekly SC injection required” — 和Slide 5“HOW GLP-1 RAs WORK”第01步的呼应：Slide 5第01步描述的‘weekly SC injection’是‘机制如何起作用’的中性描述；这一页把同一个事实重新框定为‘负担(Burden)’——同一个临床事实(每周打针)，在Slide 5是‘给药方式的客观描述’，在Slide 6是‘依从性障碍的根源’。这是这份报告里‘同一事实，不同叙事框架’的一个范例：取决于这一页要论证的观点，同一个事实可以被赋予不同的‘意义标签’。

“52% discontinuation” — 这是Slide 5 KEY INSIGHT‘real-world...typically lower’的具体来源，现在第一次给出完整引用：Slide 5的KEY INSIGHT埋下了‘real-world效果通常更低’的伏笔但没有给数字；这一页第一次给出来源——Thomsen et al., EASD 2025(欧洲糖尿病研究协会2025年会), 数据来自丹麦。“EASD”是会议摘要(conference abstract)而不是期刊正式发表的论文，这是一个值得注意的Tier等级问题——会议摘要通常早于正式论文发表，可信度略低于NEJM/Lancet这类同行评审期刊论文，但仍属于学术共同体内的、经过摘要评审的数据。

“China-specific data unavailable; discontinuation may differ because obesity use is largely self-pay” — 这句“诚实的不确定性声明”为什么如此重要：这句话做了一个非常重要的‘双向开放’声明——它没有简单地说‘中国停药率也是52%’(把丹麦数据直接套用到中国，这是范围混淆的错误)，而是说‘可能不同，原因是中国是自费场景’。但它特意不predict方向：自费可能导致‘患者因为花了自己的钱，更有动力坚持用药(停药率可能更低)’，也可能导致‘患者因为经济压力，更容易中途放弃(停药率可能更高)’——两种因果路径都成立，这一页没有强行选择一个方向，而是诚实地说‘数据不可得、方向不确定’。这是Slide 3 Tier体系里‘诚实标注假设边界’原则的又一次应用。

Content: weekly SC injection required. ~52% discontinuation at 1 year in international real-world evidence (Thomsen et al., EASD 2025; Denmark). China-specific data unavailable; discontinuation may differ because obesity use is largely self-pay. Solutions → oral GLP-1 formulations, longer-acting injectables, digital adherence support.

‘Weekly SC injection required’ — echoing Slide 5’s step 01 of ‘HOW GLP-1 RAs WORK’: Slide 5 step 01 described ‘weekly SC injection’ neutrally, as part of HOW the mechanism works. This page reframes the same fact as a ‘Burden’ — the same clinical fact (weekly injection) is ‘a description of the dosing method’ on Slide 5 and ‘the root cause of an adherence barrier’ on Slide 6. A clear example of ‘same fact, different narrative frame’ depending on the argument each page is making.

‘52% discontinuation’ — the concrete source behind Slide 5’s KEY INSIGHT ‘real-world...typically lower,’ cited in full for the first time: Slide 5’s KEY INSIGHT planted the seed of ‘real-world results are typically lower’ without a number; this page first cites the source — Thomsen et al., EASD 2025 (European Association for the Study of Diabetes annual meeting), data from Denmark. ‘EASD’ denotes a CONFERENCE ABSTRACT, not a formally published journal paper — worth noting as a tier consideration: conference abstracts typically precede formal publication and carry slightly lower reliability than NEJM/Lancet peer-reviewed papers, though still abstract-reviewed within the academic community.

‘China-specific data unavailable; discontinuation may differ because obesity use is largely self-pay’ — why this ‘honest uncertainty’ statement matters: This makes an important ‘bidirectionally open’ disclosure — rather than simply asserting ‘China’s discontinuation rate is also 52%’ (which would be a scope-conflation error, applying Danish data directly to China), it says ‘may differ, because China is self-pay.’ But it deliberately doesn’t predict the DIRECTION: self-pay could mean ‘patients, having spent their own money, are MORE motivated to persist (lower discontinuation)’ OR ‘patients, facing financial strain, are MORE likely to quit (higher discontinuation)’ — both causal pathways are plausible, and this page honestly says ‘data unavailable, direction uncertain’ rather than forcing a conclusion. Another application of Slide 3’s ‘honestly label assumption boundaries’ principle.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK“丹麦的医疗体系是高福利、高医保覆盖的体系，中国是自费为主——把丹麦的真实世界数据放在这份报告里，是不是‘范围不匹配’，就像Slide 3里批评的GVR/L.E.K.‘全适应症基准’一样的问题？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER这是一个很犀利的类比，但我认为两种情况有一个关键区别。Slide 3里GVR/L.E.K.的问题是‘范围(适应症/地理)不匹配，但被当作‘结论数字’直接使用’——也就是‘把苹和橘子的数字混在一起当结论’。而这里引用丹麦52%停药率，我的处理方式是‘把它当作‘国际真实世界证据的参考点(reference point)’，并且紧接着用一整句话明确声明‘中国数据不可得、可能不同、方向不确定’’——也就是说，我没有把52%当作‘中国的结论’，而是当作‘这类药物在有真实世界追踪数据的市场里，普遍存在的依从性问题量级’的一个例证，用来支撑‘依从性是一个真实存在的问题类别’这个定性判断，而不是‘中国停药率=52%’这个定量结论。如果要更严谨，理想情况下应该找到中国本土的真实世界研究(比如基于京东健康/阿里健康处方数据的复购率分析)作为补充——这是这一页可以改进、也是我会在‘数据来源’部分提到的方向。

EN： That's a sharp analogy, but I think there's a key difference between the two cases. The problem with GVR/L.E.K. on Slide 3 was that their scope (indication/geography) didn't match, yet their numbers were used directly AS the conclusion — mixing apples and oranges and presenting the result as the answer. Here, citing Denmark's 52% discontinuation rate, my treatment is different: I use it as a reference point for international real-world evidence, and immediately follow it with an explicit statement that China-specific data is unavailable, may differ, and the direction is uncertain. In other words, I'm not treating 52% as 'China's number' — I'm treating it as evidence that adherence problems of this magnitude are common in markets with real-world tracking data, which supports the qualitative judgment that 'adherence is a real problem category,' not the quantitative claim that 'China's discontinuation rate is 52%.' To make this more rigorous, ideally I'd supplement it with a China-specific real-world study — for example, a repeat-purchase analysis based on JD Health or Ali Health prescription data — which is an improvement area I'd flag in the data-sources discussion.

6. 障碍③ Weight Regain After Discontinuation (HIGH)

内容：停用GLP-1治疗后1年内，>60%已减掉的体重会反弹(Budini et al., Lancet eClinicalMedicine, 2026年3月；48项研究)。需要无限期或长期使用。解决方向：→联合疗法、行为干预整合、基于价值的定价模式。

“>60%体重反弹”和“48项研究” — 这是这一页(乃至全篇)证据等级最高的一个数据点：脚注里特别说明“systematic review of 48 studies, n=3,236 in meta-regression”——这是一个‘系统综述+meta回归’(systematic review + meta-regression)，发表在Lancet eClinicalMedicine(柳叶刀子刊，开放获取期刊)，2026年3月。‘系统综述’意味着这不是‘单一研究的发现’，而是‘汇总了48项独立研究、覆盖3,236名受试者后得出的综合结论’——这种证据形式在循证医学的证据等级金字塔里通常被认为是‘最高等级’(高于单一RCT, Randomized Controlled Trial)。这也是为什么这一条数据没有像‘Tier1/2/3’标注那样需要‘交叉验证’——它本身就是‘对多个一手研究的交叉验证结果’。

“Requires indefinite or long-term use” — 这句话如何把③和①②串联成一个“恶性循环”：这是这一页“四大障碍并非孤立”的关键证据——③告诉我们‘一旦停药，效果会大量流失，所以理论上需要‘长期甚至终身用药’；但①告诉我们‘这个药很贵、没有医保’；②告诉我们‘即使在有医保支持的市场，1年停药率也高达52%’。三者连起来构成一个逻辑闭环：‘药物有效 → 但需要长期使用才能维持效果 → 但长期使用意味着长期的高额自费支出 → 经济压力导致停药 → 停药导致体重反弹 → 患者可能重新开始治疗(循环)或放弃治疗(流失)’。这个闭环正是KEY INSIGHT“Price, adherence and reimbursement are the decisive variables”这句话的完整逻辑支撑。

解决方向“value-based pricing models(基于价值的定价模式)” — 这是什么、为什么放在这里：‘基于价值的定价’是一种定价机制创新——比如‘按疗效付费(pay-for-performance)’：如果患者在一定期限内没有达到预期的体重下降目标，厂商退还部分费用；或者‘订阅式定价(subscription model)’：把‘长期使用’的高总成本拆分成更平滑的现金流。放在‘体重反弹’这一条下面，逻辑是：‘既然这个药需要长期使用才有效，那么‘定价模式’本身就需要为‘长期使用’设计，而不是按‘单次购买’的逻辑定价’——这是‘产品特性(需要长期使用)反向决定商业模式设计’的一个例子。

词

Content: >60% of lost weight regained within 1 year of stopping GLP-1 therapy (Budini et al., Lancet eClinicalMedicine, Mar 2026; 48 studies). Requires indefinite or long-term use. Solutions → combination therapy, behavioral integration, value-based pricing models.

‘>60% weight regain’ and ‘48 studies’ — the highest-evidence-tier data point on this page (and arguably the deck): The footnote specifies ‘systematic review of 48 studies, n=3,236 in meta-regression’ — a systematic review + meta-regression published in Lancet eClinicalMedicine (an open-access Lancet-family journal), March 2026. ‘Systematic review’ means this isn’t ‘one study’s finding’ but ‘a synthesized conclusion across 48 independent studies covering 3,236 subjects’ — in the evidence-based-medicine hierarchy, this form of evidence is typically ranked at the TOP (above a single RCT). That’s also why this data point doesn’t need a Tier1/2/3 ‘cross-validation’ caveat — it IS already a cross-validation of multiple primary studies.

‘Requires indefinite or long-term use’ — how this links ③ to ① and ② into a vicious cycle: This is the key evidence that the ‘four barriers aren’t independent.’ ③ tells us that once stopped, most of the effect is lost, implying ‘long-term or even lifelong use is needed.’ ① tells us ‘this drug is expensive and not reimbursed.’ ② tells us ‘even in a reimbursed market, the 1-year discontinuation rate is 52%.’ Together they form a closed loop: ‘drug works → but needs long-term use to sustain effect → but long-term use means sustained high out-of-pocket spend → financial pressure drives discontinuation → discontinuation causes weight regain → patient may restart (loop) or abandon treatment (attrition).’ This loop is the full logical underpinning of the KEY INSIGHT’s ‘Price, adherence and reimbursement are the decisive variables.’

‘Value-based pricing models’ — what it is and why it’s here: Value-based pricing is a pricing-mechanism innovation — e.g., ‘pay-for-performance’ (manufacturer refunds part of the cost if a patient doesn’t hit a target weight-loss threshold within a set period), or ‘subscription models’ (smoothing the high total cost of long-term use into a more manageable cash flow). Placed under ‘weight regain,’ the logic is: ‘since this drug only works with long-term use, the PRICING MODEL itself must be designed for long-term use, not priced as a one-off purchase’ — an example of ‘product characteristics (need for long-term use) reverse-engineering business-model design.’

7. 障碍④ GI Side Effects & Tolerability (MODERATE)

内容：恶心44%，呕吐24%，腹泻30%(FDA标签数据)。是早期停药和负面患者体验的常见驱动因素。解决方向：→剂量滴定、优化下一代分子、改良制剂。

“(FDA label data)” — 三个百分比具体来自哪款药、哪个标签：脚注写明“GI data: FDA Wegovy label NDA 215256”——也就是说，44%/24%/30%这三个数字来自司美格鲁肽(Wegovy)在FDA的药品标签(Prescribing Information)，NDA编号215256。FDA药品标签里的不良反应数据，来自该药物III期临床试验中‘不良事件报告(adverse event reporting)’的统计——这是Slide 3定义里‘Tier1’的典型来源(官方监管文件)。

为什么单独用“FDA”标签、而不是“NMPA”标签：一个可能的原因是：FDA药品标签(Prescribing Information)的格式高度标准化、且在公开渠道(drugs@FDA数据库)可以直接检索到结构化的‘不良反应发生率表’(按不良反应类型和剂量分组列出百分比)；而NMPA药品说明书虽然也包含不良反应章节，但格式和详细程度可能不如FDA数据库那样‘表格化、易提取’。这是一个‘数据可获得性’决定‘引用来源选择’的例子——本质事实(同一分子的不良反应谱)应该是相通的，但‘从哪个监管机构的公开数据库提取数字’是一个实操选择。

为什么这条被定为“MODERATE”——和①②③形成对比：“恶心44%”看起来发生率很高(接近一半的患者)，但这一条被定为‘MODERATE’(全篇最低)。原因可能是：①这些不良反应大多是‘一过性的(transient)’——通常发生在剂量爬坡早期，随着身体适应或剂量稳定后会减轻；②有明确的‘可管理’(manageable)解决方案——‘剂量滴定(dose titration，即从低剂量开始逐步增加)’是FDA标签里推荐的标准做法，已经是‘标准临床实践的一部分’，不需要等待‘新的解决方案’；③和①(支付能力)、②③(长期依从性/反弹)相比，GI副作用更多影响‘治疗早期体验’，而不是‘决定整个治疗周期能否持续的结构性因素’。

Content: Nausea 44%, vomiting 24%, diarrhea 30% (FDA label data); a common driver of early discontinuation and negative patient experience. Solutions → dose titration, optimized next-gen molecules, improved formulations.

‘(FDA label data)’ — which drug/label do these three percentages come from: The footnote specifies ‘GI data: FDA Wegovy label NDA 215256’ — i.e., the 44%/24%/30% figures come from semaglutide’s (Wegovy) FDA Prescribing Information, NDA 215256. Adverse-event rates in an FDA label derive from that drug’s Phase 3 adverse-event reporting — a textbook Tier1 source (official regulatory document) per Slide 3’s definition.

Why specifically the ‘FDA’ label and not an ‘NMPA’ label: One plausible reason: FDA Prescribing Information is highly standardized and freely searchable (via the Drugs@FDA database) with structured ‘adverse reaction rate tables’ broken down by type and dose group, whereas NMPA drug inserts, while also containing an adverse-reactions section, may not be as tabular or easy to extract from. An example of ‘data availability’ driving ‘source choice’ — the underlying fact (the same molecule’s adverse-event profile) should be consistent, but WHICH regulator’s public database the figures are pulled from is a practical choice.

Why this barrier is rated ‘MODERATE’ — contrast with ①②③: ‘Nausea 44%’ looks high (nearly half of patients), yet this is the LOWEST-rated barrier on the page. Likely reasons: (1) these adverse events are mostly transient — occurring early during dose escalation and easing once the body adapts or the dose stabilizes; (2) there’s an established, manageable solution — ‘dose titration’ (starting low and escalating gradually) is the FDA label’s standard recommendation, already part of standard clinical practice, not awaiting a ‘new’ solution; (3) compared with ① (affordability) and ②③ (long-term adherence/regain), GI effects mainly affect the EARLY treatment experience rather than being a structural factor determining whether the entire treatment course can be sustained.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK“44%的恶心发生率，听起来比52%的停药率(障碍②)还要接近——会不会GI副作用其实是导致52%停药率的‘主要原因’，而不是一个独立的、影响较小的障碍？把它们列为两条独立障碍，是不是低估了GI副作用的实际影响？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER这是一个非常有洞察力的问题，直接指向‘这4个障碍之间是否存在因果重叠’。从临床文献来看，GI不良反应确实是‘早期停药(early discontinuation)’的常见原因之一——这一页第④条本身就写了‘A common driver of early discontinuation’，承认了这种关联。但52%这个1年停药率(来自Thomsen et al. EASD 2025)，作为一个‘汇总结果(aggregate outcome)’，背后的成因很可能是‘多因素叠加’的——包括GI副作用导致的早期退出、经济因素导致的中后期退出、以及患者主观感受(比如‘已经达到自己满意的体重，主动停药’)等。这一页把②(停药率/依从性，HIGH)和④(GI副作用，MODERATE)列为两条独立障碍，反映的是‘症状层面的现象(GI副作用)’和‘行为结果层面的现象(停药)’的区别——GI副作用是‘停药的众多原因之一’，但‘停药’本身作为一个更上游的、综合性的指标，被单独列出并赋予更高的严重程度(HIGH)，是因为它是‘最终业务结果(影响LTV)’，而GI副作用是‘导致这个结果的多个具体机制之一’。如果要更严谨，理想情况下应该有‘停药归因分析(reasons-for-discontinuation breakdown)’的数据，把52%进一步拆解为‘因GI副作用/因经济原因/因达到目标/因其他’等子类别——这是目前公开数据里比较缺乏的细分维度。

8. KEY INSIGHT 横条 The Page’s Thesis Bar

原文：“The access barriers — not efficacy — are what constrain China GLP-1 obesity commercialization in 2025–2026. Price, adherence and reimbursement are the decisive variables for market scale.”

结构分析：第一句“access barriers—not efficacy”是对斜体论点句(“not clinical”)的“二次重申+具体化”——把抽象的‘economic and behavioral’进一步落实为‘access barriers’这个更具体的词。第二句“Price, adherence and reimbursement”把四大障碍‘压缩’成三个变量：Price对应①(成本)，adherence对应②④(依从性/副作用)，reimbursement对应①里的‘No NRDL’——③(体重反弹)在这句总结里没有被直接点名，但它通过‘需要长期使用’间接影响‘adherence’这个变量。

“decisive variables for market scale” — 这句话如何“预告”后面的市场规模模型(Slide 7-9)：这是这一页对Slide 9市场模型的‘前情提要’——它告诉读者：‘接下来要看到的市场规模模型(Slide 9)里，价格、依从性(渗透率背后的行为因素)、医保报销，将是决定最终数字大小的关键变量，而不是疗效数字(Slide 5的15-22%)’。这意味着，如果读者想要‘压力测试’Slide 9的模型，应该重点关注‘价格假设、渗透率假设、医保假设’这几个输入项，而不是去质疑‘疗效是否足够好’——这是这一页为后续模型‘划定质疑边界’的作用。

Original text: “The access barriers — not efficacy — are what constrain China GLP-1 obesity commercialization in 2025–2026. Price, adherence and reimbursement are the decisive variables for market scale.”

Structural analysis: Sentence 1 (‘access barriers—not efficacy’) is a re-affirmation and concretization of the italic thesis (‘not clinical’) — turning the abstract ‘economic and behavioral’ into the more concrete ‘access barriers.’ Sentence 2 (‘Price, adherence and reimbursement’) compresses the four barriers into three variables: Price maps to ① (cost), adherence maps to ②④ (adherence/side effects), reimbursement maps to the ‘No NRDL’ part of ①. ③ (weight regain) isn’t named directly in this summary, but indirectly affects ‘adherence’ via ‘need for long-term use.’

‘Decisive variables for market scale’ — how this previews the upcoming market-sizing model (Slides 7–9): This is a preview for Slide 9’s market model — it tells the reader: ‘in the market-sizing model coming up, price, adherence (the behavioral driver behind penetration), and reimbursement will be the variables that determine the final number’s size — not the efficacy figures (Slide 5’s 15–22%).’ This means a reader ‘stress-testing’ Slide 9’s model should focus on its price/penetration/reimbursement assumptions, not question ‘whether efficacy is good enough’ — this page draws the ‘boundary of legitimate challenge’ for the model that follows.

9. 底部脚注 — 三条来源逐一核对 Footnote — Three Sources Checked

原文：“Treatment algorithm: Chinese Clinical Guidelines for Obesity (2024). Weight regain: Budini et al. Lancet eClinicalMedicine Mar 4 2026, systematic review of 48 studies, n=3,236 in meta-regression. GI data: FDA Wegovy label NDA 215256.”

三条来源对应三种不同性质的证据：第一条(治疗路径图)来自‘中国临床指南(2024)’——这是Tier1+2混合性质：临床指南通常由专业医学会(如中华医学会)组织专家基于证据制定并发布，兼具‘官方权威性(类似Tier1)’和‘专家共识(类似学术Tier2)’的特征。第二条(体重反弹)来自系统综述(Lancet eClinicalMedicine)——纯学术Tier1+，且是‘多研究汇总’的最高等级证据。第三条(GI数据)来自FDA官方药品标签——纯Tier1监管文件。三条来源覆盖了‘临床指南/学术综述/监管文件’三种不同类型的Tier1证据，体现了这一页‘不同性质的论点，匹配不同性质的最权威来源’的设计原则。

为什么“Treatment algorithm”只用了‘2024’一个年份标注，没有像其他两条那样标注期刊/机构细节：‘中国肥胖症诊疗指南(2024)’是一个相对宽泛的引用——中国近年发布过多个与肥胖相关的临床指南/共识(如中华医学会内分泌学分会、中国营养学会等机构发布的不同版本)。这一条引用的颗粒度不如另外两条精确(没有具体到‘第几卷第几页’或DOI)，是这一页脚注里相对‘弱’的一环——如果被追问‘具体是哪个学会、哪个版本的指南’，需要进一步核实并补充精确引用(比如‘中华医学会内分泌学分会《肥胖症诊疗指南(2024年版)》’)。

Original text: “Treatment algorithm: Chinese Clinical Guidelines for Obesity (2024). Weight regain: Budini et al. Lancet eClinicalMedicine Mar 4 2026, systematic review of 48 studies, n=3,236 in meta-regression. GI data: FDA Wegovy label NDA 215256.”

Three sources, three different evidence natures: Source 1 (treatment-pathway diagram) is ‘Chinese Clinical Guidelines (2024)’ — a Tier1+2 hybrid: clinical guidelines are typically issued by professional medical societies based on expert consensus and evidence review, combining ‘official authority (Tier1-like)’ with ‘expert consensus (academic Tier2-like)’ characteristics. Source 2 (weight regain) is a systematic review (Lancet eClinicalMedicine) — pure academic Tier1+, and the HIGHEST-tier form of evidence (multi-study synthesis). Source 3 (GI data) is an official FDA drug label — pure Tier1 regulatory document. The three sources cover three different Tier1 evidence TYPES (clinical guideline / academic systematic review / regulatory document), reflecting this page’s design principle: match each argument’s nature to the most authoritative source of that SAME nature.

Why ‘Treatment algorithm’ cites only a year (‘2024’), without journal/society detail like the other two: ‘Chinese Clinical Guidelines for Obesity (2024)’ is a relatively broad citation — China has issued multiple obesity-related clinical guidelines/consensus statements in recent years (e.g., from the Chinese Society of Endocrinology, Chinese Nutrition Society, etc., in different versions). This citation’s granularity is less precise than the other two (no volume/page/DOI) — the relatively ‘weak link’ in this footnote. If pressed on ‘which society, which version,’ it would need further verification and a more precise citation (e.g., ‘Chinese Society of Endocrinology, Guidelines for the Diagnosis and Treatment of Obesity (2024 edition)’).

10. 总结：这一页在“埋”什么 Summary — What This Slide Plants

元素 / Element

⭐ 这一页最该背的一句话 / The Sentence to Memorize

“Slide 5证明了GLP-1的临床疗效很强(15-22%)，但Slide 6说明‘未满足的需求不是临床层面的，而是经济和行为层面的’——四大障碍按严重程度排序为：①成本与医保(CRITICAL，目前无肥胖适应症NRDL报销，自费起始剂量约CNY1,400/月≈CNY16,800/年，与Slide3模型假设吻合)；②注射负担与依从性(HIGH，国际真实世界1年停药率约52%，中国数据不可得、自费场景下方向不确定)；③停药后体重反弹(HIGH，>60%在1年内反弹，48项研究的系统综述，意味着需要长期甚至终身用药)；④胃肠道不良反应(MODERATE，恶心44%/呕吐24%/腹泻30%，可通过剂量滴定管理)。这4个障碍构成一个相互强化的闭环，KEY INSIGHT的结论是：价格、依从性和医保报销，才是决定Slide9市场规模模型大小的关键变量——不是疗效。”

“Slide 5 proved GLP-1’s clinical efficacy is strong (15–22%), but Slide 6 establishes that ‘unmet needs are economic and behavioral, not clinical.’ The four barriers, ranked by severity: ① cost & reimbursement (CRITICAL — no obesity-specific NRDL coverage; self-pay starter dose ~CNY1,400/month ≈ CNY16,800/year, reconciling with Slide3’s model assumption); ② injection burden & adherence (HIGH — ~52% 1-year discontinuation in international real-world evidence; China data unavailable, direction uncertain under self-pay); ③ weight regain after discontinuation (HIGH — >60% regained within 1 year per a 48-study systematic review, implying long-term or lifelong use is required); ④ GI side effects (MODERATE — nausea 44%/vomiting 24%/diarrhea 30%, manageable via dose titration). These four barriers form a mutually-reinforcing loop, and the KEY INSIGHT concludes: price, adherence, and reimbursement — not efficacy — are the decisive variables for Slide 9’s market-sizing model.”

11. 综合问题：设计这一页要考虑哪些因素？数据来源都在哪？ Design Factors & Where to Find Sources

设计这一页（未满足需求/可及性障碍页）要考虑的因素：

① 归因清晰度——‘问题出在哪一层(临床/经济/行为)’这个判断，是否会直接决定后续模型(Slide9)的输入假设和解决方案(Slide11趋势)的方向，归因错了，后面整个论证链都会偏；② 严重程度分级的可防御性——CRITICAL/HIGH/MODERATE这类标签即使是定性判断，也需要能用‘对最终市场结果的解释力’来回答‘为什么是这个等级’；③ 跨页数字一致性——比如CNY1,400(本页)和CNY16,800(Slide3)是否经得起‘乘除验证’，这种隐藏的一致性是建立读者信任的细节；④ 地理范围的诚实标注——引用国际数据(丹麦52%停药率)时，是否明确说明‘中国数据不可得’，避免Slide3批评的‘范围混淆’错误；⑤ 障碍之间的因果关系——4个障碍是否被处理成‘孤立的清单’还是‘相互强化的系统’，后者信息密度更高，也更有说服力。

我所知道的、与这一页相关的数据来源类型：

【临床指南/诊疗规范】中华医学会(各专科分会，如内分泌学分会)发布的诊疗指南、共识声明——通常可在中华医学会官网或学会官方期刊(如《中华内分泌代谢杂志》)上检索PDF全文。

【药品价格】京东健康/阿里健康/美团买药等线上药房——搜索药品通用名/商品名可查实时零售价；第一财经(Yicai)、财联社等财经媒体在新药上市时通常会有‘定价/上市价格’的报道。

【医保目录】国家医保局(NHSA)官网‘药品目录公开查询’——可查询某药品是否在NRDL内、对应哪些适应症。

【真实世界依从性/停药率数据】EASD(欧洲糖尿病研究协会)、ADA(美国糖尿病协会)年会摘要库——通常是最新真实世界数据的‘首发地’(早于正式论文)；也可搜索基于保险理赔数据库(claims database)的真实世界研究，如使用Optum/IQVIA等数据源的论文。

【系统综述/meta分析】Lancet系列期刊(包括开放获取的Lancet eClinicalMedicine/Lancet Regional Health等)、Cochrane Database of Systematic Reviews——搜索‘drug class + weight regain/discontinuation + systematic review’。

【药品不良反应数据】FDA Drugs@FDA数据库(可下载Prescribing Information PDF，查Adverse Reactions章节的表格)；NMPA药品说明书查询(国家药监局官网‘数据查询-药品’)。

具体去哪找（实操路径）：

① 临床指南 → 中华医学会官网(cma.org.cn)各分会页面，或在中国知网(CNKI)搜索‘肥胖症诊疗指南 2024’查找学会发布的正式版本。 ② 药品上市价格 → 京东健康(jd.com健康频道)/阿里健康app搜索‘诺和盈/Wegovy’查零售价；或搜索‘Wegovy 中国上市 价格’查新闻报道(财新/第一财经/华尔街见闻)。 ③ 医保目录核查 → nhsa.gov.cn(国家医保局)→‘信息查询’→‘药品目录’，输入药品名查是否在目录内及适应症范围。 ④ 真实世界停药率数据 → easd.org/diabetesjournals.org(ADA)的年会摘要搜索引擎，搜索‘GLP-1 discontinuation real-world’；或在PubMed搜索‘semaglutide tirzepatide discontinuation cohort’找基于claims数据的论文。 ⑤ 系统综述(体重反弹) → thelancet.com搜索‘eClinicalMedicine weight regain GLP-1’，该期刊开放获取可直接读全文PDF。 ⑥ FDA不良反应数据 → accessdata.fda.gov/scripts/cder/daf/(Drugs@FDA)搜索‘Wegovy’，下载最新Label PDF，查‘6 ADVERSE REACTIONS’章节的表格。

Factors to consider when designing this ‘unmet needs / access barriers’ page: ① attribution clarity — the judgment of ‘which layer the problem sits in (clinical/economic/behavioral)’ directly steers the downstream model’s (Slide9) input assumptions and the solutions slide’s (Slide11) direction; a wrong attribution skews the whole subsequent argument chain. ② defensibility of severity tiers — CRITICAL/HIGH/MODERATE labels, even if qualitative, must be answerable via ‘explanatory power over the eventual market outcome.’ ③ cross-page numeric consistency — e.g., whether CNY1,400 (this page) and CNY16,800 (Slide3) survive a ‘multiply/divide check’; such hidden consistency builds reader trust. ④ honest geographic-scope labeling — when citing international data (Denmark’s 52% discontinuation), explicitly stating ‘China data unavailable’ avoids the scope-conflation error Slide3 criticized. ⑤ causal relationships among barriers — whether the 4 barriers are presented as an ‘isolated checklist’ or a ‘mutually-reinforcing system’; the latter carries more information density and persuasive power.

Data source types relevant to this page: [Clinical guidelines] Guidelines/consensus statements from Chinese medical societies (e.g., Chinese Society of Endocrinology) — searchable on the society’s website or its official journal. [Drug pricing] JD Health / Ali Health / Meituan online pharmacies for real-time retail prices; financial media (Yicai, cls.cn) for launch-price coverage. [Reimbursement catalogue] NHSA website ‘drug catalogue query’ for NRDL inclusion and covered indications. [Real-world adherence/discontinuation data] EASD/ADA annual meeting abstract archives (often the first venue for new real-world data, ahead of formal publication); claims-database studies (e.g., using Optum/IQVIA data) on PubMed. [Systematic reviews/meta-analyses] Lancet-family journals (incl. open-access Lancet eClinicalMedicine, Lancet Regional Health), Cochrane Database of Systematic Reviews. [Adverse-event data] FDA’s Drugs@FDA database (downloadable Prescribing Information PDFs, ‘Adverse Reactions’ tables); NMPA drug-label query on its official website.

Practical paths: ① clinical guidelines → cma.org.cn (Chinese Medical Association) society pages, or CNKI search ‘obesity diagnosis treatment guideline 2024.’ ② drug launch price → JD Health/Ali Health app search ‘Wegovy/诺和盈’ for retail price, or search ‘Wegovy China launch price’ on Caixin/Yicai/Wall Street CN. ③ reimbursement check → nhsa.gov.cn → ‘Information Query’ → ‘Drug Catalogue,’ search the drug name for NRDL status and covered indications. ④ real-world discontinuation data → EASD/ADA abstract search engines for ‘GLP-1 discontinuation real-world’, or PubMed for ‘semaglutide tirzepatide discontinuation cohort.’ ⑤ systematic review (weight regain) → thelancet.com search ‘eClinicalMedicine weight regain GLP-1’ (open access, full PDF). ⑥ FDA adverse-event data → accessdata.fda.gov/scripts/cder/daf/ (Drugs@FDA), search ‘Wegovy,’ download the latest Label PDF, check section ‘6 ADVERSE REACTIONS.’

Slide 7 Approved Products 已获批产品

Approved GLP-1 Obesity Products in China — Detailed Line-by-Line Analysis (Bilingual)
Overview

这一页是Slide 1“6款产品”、Slide 4“4种机制分类”与Slide 5“5个疗效数据点”的“实体清单(entity list)”——前面几页讲的是“分类标准”和“疗效证据”，这一页第一次把“这6款产品到底是谁、谁家的、什么时候批的、卖得怎么样”完整列出来。这一页的核心张力在于：表格里6家公司中4家是中国本土企业(暗示“国产创新崛起”的正面叙事)，但“Global Revenue”这一列展示的财务数据全部来自2家MNC——这种“数量上本土领先、规模上MNC领先”的反差，正是KEY INSIGHT要明确说清楚的内容。

This page is the ‘entity list’ behind Slide 1’s ‘6 products,’ Slide 4’s ‘4 mechanism categories,’ and Slide 5’s ‘5 efficacy data points’ — earlier pages covered classification criteria and clinical evidence; this is the first page to fully list WHO these six products are, WHO owns them, WHEN approved, and HOW they perform commercially. The page’s central tension: 4 of the 6 companies are Chinese domestic firms (a positive ‘domestic innovation rising’ narrative), yet the ‘Global Revenue’ column shows financial figures only for the 2 MNCs — this ‘leading in count, trailing in scale’ contrast is exactly what the KEY INSIGHT must clarify.

1. 标题、副标题与斜体提示句 Title, Subtitle & Header Note

原文：标题“Approved GLP-1 Obesity Products in China”；副标题“Six NMPA-Approved GLP-1 Obesity Products — Market Opened Within ~3 Years”；斜体提示句“Approvals span July 2023 – March 2026; domestic and MNC innovators now compete at different price points and mechanisms”。

副标题“Market Opened Within ~3 Years” — 与Slide 1“33个月加速期”的呼应：Slide 1把“2023年7月–2026年3月、33个月内获批6款产品”作为“隐藏论点”埋在时间窗里；这一页把同一个事实直接“翻译”成更口语化的“~3 Years”并放进副标题——这是“同一事实，从‘隐性论点’升级为‘显性标题’”的典型手法。读者读到Slide 1时可能没意识到‘时间窗’的含义，读到Slide 7时，标题直接把它点破：‘这是一个3年内从0到6的市场’。

斜体提示句的两层信息：第一层‘Approvals span July 2023 – March 2026’是对Slide 1时间线的精确复述(年月级别)；第二层‘domestic and MNC innovators now compete at different price points and mechanisms’预告了这一页表格的‘两条分类轴’——‘价格点(price points)’对应Slide 6障碍①讨论的‘成本’维度(不同产品定价不同)，‘机制(mechanisms)’直接对应Slide 4的4种机制分类。这句话相当于告诉读者：‘下面这张表，你可以同时按‘公司是国产还是MNC’和‘机制是哪一类’这两个维度去看。’

Original text: Title “Approved GLP-1 Obesity Products in China”; subtitle “Six NMPA-Approved GLP-1 Obesity Products — Market Opened Within ~3 Years”; italic note “Approvals span July 2023 – March 2026; domestic and MNC innovators now compete at different price points and mechanisms.”

‘Market Opened Within ~3 Years’ — echoing Slide 1’s ‘33-month acceleration window’: Slide 1 buried ‘6 products approved within 33 months (Jul 2023–Mar 2026)’ as a HIDDEN argument inside a date range. This page directly ‘translates’ the same fact into the more colloquial ‘~3 Years’ and puts it IN the subtitle — a classic move from ‘implicit argument’ to ‘explicit headline.’ A reader might not register the significance of the date range on Slide 1; on Slide 7, the title spells it out: ‘this is a zero-to-six market within 3 years.’

Two layers in the italic note: Layer 1, ‘Approvals span July 2023 – March 2026,’ precisely restates Slide 1’s timeline (year-month granularity). Layer 2, ‘domestic and MNC innovators now compete at different price points and mechanisms,’ previews the table’s TWO classification axes — ‘price points’ maps to Slide 6 Barrier ①’s cost dimension (different products, different prices); ‘mechanisms’ maps directly to Slide 4’s 4 mechanism categories. This sentence tells the reader: ‘read the table below along two axes — domestic vs. MNC, AND which mechanism class.’

2. NMPA批准时间线条 NMPA Approval Timeline Bar

原文：“NMPA APPROVAL TIMELINE ► Jul 2023: Liluping ► Jul 2023: Feisumei ► Jun 2024: Wegovy (诺和盈) ► Jul 2024: Mufengda ► Jun 2025: 信尔美 (Mazdutide) ► Mar 2026: Ecnoglutide”，左右两端分别标注“6 NMPA obesity GLP-1 approvals (Jun 2026)”、“Jul 2023 First domestic approval (Liluping/利鲁平)”、“Mar 2026 Most recent approval (Ecnoglutide/XW003)”。

为什么这条时间线要把6个产品“串成一条线”，而不是直接进入下面的表格：时间线提供的是‘序列感(sequence)’——表格里的6行是‘并列的实体’，时间线把这6个实体重新组织成‘一个不断发生的过程(process)’。这和Slide 1“6款产品”的呈现方式(一个静态数字“6”)不同——这里把“6”拆解成“6个具体的事件，按时间顺序发生”，让‘获批速度’这件事变得‘可感知’：读者能看到‘两个事件挤在2023年7月(同月)’、‘接下来近1年的空档(2023.7→2024.6)’、然后‘2024年6–7月又是两个事件挤在一起’等节奏变化。

左右两端标注的“对称结构” — 为什么“最早”和“最新”批准的都是国产产品：‘First domestic approval (利鲁平, 2023年7月)’和‘Most recent approval (Ecnoglutide, 2026年3月)’这两个标注，分别标注的是‘整条时间线的起点和终点’，而这两个‘端点’恰好都是‘国产’产品(利鲁平=华东医药；Ecnoglutide=先为达生物)——这不是巧合式的装饰，而是为KEY INSIGHT‘Domestic companies now hold 4 of 6 approvals’提供了‘视觉上的首尾呼应’：时间线的两端都在‘提示’读者‘国产企业在这个赛道里很活跃’，即使中间夹着两个MNC产品(Wegovy/Mufengda)。

“6 NMPA obesity GLP-1 approvals (Jun 2026)” — 为什么要重复标注“Jun 2026”：这是Slide 1“Study Period”声明的‘第N次重复’——再次确认‘6’这个数字的‘截止日期’是2026年6月(报告撰写时点)。重复这个时间戳的原因和Slide 2分析过的一样：确保‘如果未来有第7款产品获批，这一页的‘6’不会被认为是‘错误’，而是‘在声明的截止日期之前是准确的’。

Original text: “NMPA APPROVAL TIMELINE ► Jul 2023: Liluping ► Jul 2023: Feisumei ► Jun 2024: Wegovy (诺和盈) ► Jul 2024: Mufengda ► Jun 2025: 信尔美 (Mazdutide) ► Mar 2026: Ecnoglutide”, with end labels ‘6 NMPA obesity GLP-1 approvals (Jun 2026)’, ‘Jul 2023 First domestic approval (Liluping/利鲁平)’, ‘Mar 2026 Most recent approval (Ecnoglutide/XW003)’.

Why string the 6 products into a timeline rather than going straight to the table below: The timeline provides a sense of SEQUENCE — the table’s 6 rows are ‘parallel entities,’ while the timeline reorganizes these 6 entities into ‘an unfolding process.’ Unlike Slide 1’s presentation of ‘6 products’ as a static number, here ‘6’ is decomposed into ‘6 discrete events occurring in chronological order,’ making ‘approval velocity’ PERCEPTIBLE: the reader sees ‘two events crammed into the same month (Jul 2023)’, ‘a nearly year-long gap (Jul 2023→Jun 2024)’, then ‘two more events bunched in Jun–Jul 2024’, etc.

The ‘symmetric’ end labels — why both the EARLIEST and the MOST RECENT approvals are domestic products: ‘First domestic approval (Liluping, Jul 2023)’ and ‘Most recent approval (Ecnoglutide, Mar 2026)’ mark the START and END of the entire timeline — and both endpoints happen to be DOMESTIC products (Liluping = Huadong Medicine; Ecnoglutide = Sciwind Biosciences). This isn’t decorative coincidence; it provides a VISUAL BOOKEND for the KEY INSIGHT’s ‘Domestic companies now hold 4 of 6 approvals’ — both ends of the timeline signal ‘domestic firms are active in this race,’ even though two MNC products (Wegovy/Mufengda) sit in between.

‘6 NMPA obesity GLP-1 approvals (Jun 2026)’ — why repeat the ‘Jun 2026’ timestamp: This is the Nth repetition of Slide 1’s ‘Study Period’ disclosure — reconfirming that ‘6’ is accurate AS OF June 2026 (the report’s preparation date). Same purpose as discussed for Slide 2: ensures that if a 7th product is approved in the future, this page’s ‘6’ isn’t seen as ‘wrong,’ but ‘accurate as of the declared cutoff.’

3. 表格列设计 — 为什么是这6列 Table Column Design — Why These 6 Columns

六列：Brand / INN（商品名/通用名）｜ Company（公司）｜ NMPA Approved（NMPA批准日期）｜ Mechanism（机制）｜ China BMI Criteria（中国适应症BMI标准）｜ Global Revenue / Evidence Ref.（全球营收/证据来源）。

六列为什么构成一个MECE的“产品档案(product dossier)”：可以把这6列归纳为3对‘身份-背书’关系：①‘Brand/INN + Company’回答‘这是什么药、谁家的’(身份)；②‘NMPA Approved + Mechanism’回答‘监管层面什么时候批的、科学层面属于哪一类’(分类坐标，分别对应Slide 1时间线和Slide 4机制分类)；③‘China BMI Criteria + Global Revenue/Evidence Ref.’回答‘谁能用这个药(适应症门槛，对应Slide 4/Slide 6治疗路径)、这个药的商业证据是什么(对应Slide 1/Slide 5引用的财报/试验数据)’。六列没有一列是‘多余的装饰’，每一列都精确对应前面某一页已经建立的‘坐标系’——这是Slide 4总结里提到的‘分类目录与实体清单要能互相映射’原则的具体落地。

为什么最后一列叫“Global Revenue / Evidence Ref.”而不是单纯“Revenue”：这一列实际承载了‘三种不同性质的内容’(下文逐行会展开)：①对MNC产品(Wegovy/Mufengda)，是‘真实的财务营收数字’；②对国产创新产品(信尔美/Ecnoglutide)，是‘公司自称的‘全球首个’地位声明 + 疗效数字’，不是营收；③对老牌国产产品(利鲁平/菲塑美)，是‘营收未单独披露’的数据缺口声明。‘Revenue / Evidence Ref.’这个复合列名，提前承认了‘这一列不是纯粹的、可比的财务指标’，而是‘针对每个产品、目前能找到的最佳公开商业证据’——这是诚实标注‘数据异质性(heterogeneity)’的又一个例子。

Six columns: Brand/INN | Company | NMPA Approved | Mechanism | China BMI Criteria | Global Revenue/Evidence Ref.

Why these 6 columns form a MECE ‘product dossier’: The 6 columns reduce to 3 ‘identity–backing’ pairs: ① ‘Brand/INN + Company’ answers ‘what is this drug, whose is it’ (identity); ② ‘NMPA Approved + Mechanism’ answers ‘when was it approved regulatorily, what scientific category does it belong to’ (classification coordinates, mapping to Slide 1’s timeline and Slide 4’s mechanism classes); ③ ‘China BMI Criteria + Global Revenue/Evidence Ref.’ answers ‘who can use it (indication threshold, mapping to Slide 4/6’s treatment pathway) and what’s its commercial evidence (mapping to financial/trial data cited on Slides 1/5).’ No column is decorative — each maps precisely onto a coordinate system already established on an earlier page, a concrete instance of Slide 4’s ‘classification catalog must cross-map to entity list’ principle.

Why ‘Global Revenue / Evidence Ref.’ rather than simply ‘Revenue’: This column actually carries THREE different kinds of content (detailed row-by-row below): ① for the MNC products (Wegovy/Mufengda), it's a real financial revenue figure; ② for domestic innovative products (Mazdutide/Ecnoglutide), it's a company-stated ‘world’s first’ claim plus an efficacy figure — not revenue; ③ for legacy domestic products (Liluping/Feisumei), it's a disclosure-gap statement (‘revenue not separately disclosed’). The compound column name ‘Revenue / Evidence Ref.’ proactively acknowledges this column ISN’T a uniform, comparable financial metric — it's ‘the best publicly available commercial evidence for each product,’ another instance of honestly labeling data heterogeneity.

4. 表格行排列顺序 — 为什么和上面的时间线不一致 Table Row Order — Why It Doesn’t Match the Timeline Above

时间线顺序(按批准日期升序)：利鲁平(2023.7) → 菲塑美(2023.7) → 诺和盈(2024.6) → 穆峰达(2024.7) → 信尔美(2025.6) → Ecnoglutide(2026.3)。表格行顺序：诺和盈 → 穆峰达 → 信尔美 → Ecnoglutide → 利鲁平 → 菲塑美。

两种顺序的差异本质：时间线是严格的‘监管事件时间顺序’；表格顺序则是‘前4行(诺和盈/穆峰达/信尔美/Ecnoglutide)按批准日期升序(2024.6→2024.7→2025.6→2026.3)’+‘后2行(利鲁平/菲塑美)按批准日期升序(2023.7→2023.7)’——也就是说，表格把6个产品拆成了‘两组各自内部按时间排序的子序列’，但两组之间的顺序是‘倒过来的’(更新的4个在前，更老的2个在后)。

为什么要这样“拆成两组、组间倒序”排列：一个合理的解释是：前4行(2024-2026年获批)代表‘当前市场的主流竞争格局’——MNC双雄(诺和盈/穆峰达)+国产双星(信尔美/Ecnoglutide，且都带有‘世界第一’标签)，这4款产品是Slide 5疗效表、Slide 12竞争格局等后续页面‘重点讨论的对象’；后2行(2023年获批的利鲁平/菲塑美)是‘历史最早的两款、机制相对老旧(都是单靶点GLP-1 agonist，且‘revenue not separately disclosed’)’，更像是‘为完整性而保留的记录’。把‘读者最需要关注的4个’放在前面、‘背景性的2个’放在后面，是一种‘重要性排序(relevance-based ordering)’，而不是单纯的‘时间排序’——这和Slide 5表格‘不严格按数值排序、而是按叙事分组排序’的设计逻辑是一致的。

⚠ 这里的潜在风险：如果读者先看时间线(严格时间顺序)，再看表格(重要性顺序)，可能会下意识地问‘为什么这两部分顺序不一样，是不是排版错误？’——这是一个值得主动澄清的‘呈现一致性’问题，即使两种顺序各自都有合理逻辑。

Timeline order (ascending by approval date): Liluping (Jul 2023) → Feisumei (Jul 2023) → Wegovy (Jun 2024) → Mufengda (Jul 2024) → Mazdutide (Jun 2025) → Ecnoglutide (Mar 2026). Table row order: Wegovy → Mufengda → Mazdutide → Ecnoglutide → Liluping → Feisumei.

The essence of the two different orderings: The timeline is a strict regulatory-event chronology. The table order is ‘the first 4 rows (Wegovy/Mufengda/Mazdutide/Ecnoglutide) sorted ascending by approval date (Jun2024→Jul2024→Jun2025→Mar2026)’ PLUS ‘the last 2 rows (Liluping/Feisumei), also ascending (Jul2023→Jul2023).’ In other words, the table splits the 6 products into two internally-chronological sub-sequences, but the ORDER BETWEEN the two groups is REVERSED (newer 4 first, older 2 last).

Why split into two groups with reversed group-order: A plausible reading: the first 4 rows (approved 2024–2026) represent the CURRENT competitive landscape — an MNC duo (Wegovy/Mufengda) + a domestic duo (Mazdutide/Ecnoglutide, both carrying ‘world’s first’ labels) — these 4 are the focus of later pages (Slide 5’s efficacy table, Slide 12’s competitive landscape). The last 2 rows (Liluping/Feisumei, approved 2023) are the oldest, mechanistically older (both single-target GLP-1 agonists, both ‘revenue not separately disclosed’) — more like records kept for completeness. Putting the ‘4 the reader most needs to focus on’ first and the ‘2 background entries’ last is RELEVANCE-BASED ordering, not pure chronology — consistent with Slide 5’s table, which was also grouped by narrative relevance rather than strict value order.

⚠ A latent risk here: A reader who sees the strictly-chronological timeline first, then the relevance-ordered table, might instinctively ask ‘why don’t these two orderings match — is this a layout error?’ — a ‘presentation consistency’ issue worth proactively clarifying, even though each ordering has its own valid logic.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK“时间线按时间顺序排，表格又按另一种顺序排——这是不是说明这一页在‘设计’上不够统一？两种排序方式只能选一种吗？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER两种排序服务于不同的认知任务，我认为同时保留是合理的，但确实可以通过‘视觉提示’减少读者的困惑。时间线的任务是‘展示节奏/速度’——它必须严格按时间，否则‘加速获批’这个论点就无法成立。表格的任务是‘展示当前竞争格局的优先级’——把读者最需要关注的4个最新、最具代表性的产品放在最前面，符合‘金字塔原理(重要的先说)’。如果要改进，可以在表格里增加一列‘批准顺序编号(#1-#6)’，或者在表格标题旁加一句‘Sorted by current market relevance, not approval date’——用一句话主动声明排序逻辑的切换，就能化解‘是不是排版错误’的疑问。这也提醒我，在汇报时如果被问到‘为什么这两部分顺序不同’，我应该主动说明‘这是两种不同的排序逻辑，各自服务于不同的论点’，而不是含糊其辞。

EN： The two orderings serve different cognitive tasks, so I think keeping both is reasonable — though a visual cue could reduce reader confusion. The timeline's job is to show PACE/speed, so it must be strictly chronological, or the 'acceleration' argument falls apart. The table's job is to show the PRIORITY of the current competitive landscape — putting the 4 newest, most representative products that the reader most needs to focus on first, following the 'pyramid principle' (lead with what matters most). To improve this, I'd add a column showing the approval-order number (#1–#6), or add a line near the table title saying 'Sorted by current market relevance, not approval date' — proactively flagging the switch in sorting logic resolves the 'is this a layout error' concern in one sentence. This also reminds me that if asked in the interview 'why do these two sections use different orderings,' I should proactively explain that these are two different sorting logics, each serving a different argument, rather than being vague about it.

5. 六行数据逐一拆解 Row-by-Row Breakdown

① 诺和盈 (Semaglutide 2.4mg/wk) | Novo Nordisk | Jun 25, 2024 | GLP-1 agonist | BMI≥30; 或≥27+合并症 | Wegovy FY2025: DKK 79.1B (~USD 12B) [Novo Nordisk 2025 AR]

数字细节：DKK(丹麦克朗) 79.1B ≈ USD 12B——这是一个汇率换算后的近似值。来源标注为‘[Novo Nordisk 2025 AR]’(年报，Annual Report)，是Slide 3 Tier1‘公司年报/投资者发布’的典型例子——上市公司法定披露文件，有审计责任背书。

⚠ 攻击点与回答：“DKK转USD用的是什么汇率？79.1B DKK换算成USD是否真的约等于12B？”——按2025年DKK/USD汇率大致在1美元≈6.5-7丹麦克朗左右计算，79.1B÷6.5≈12.2B，÷7≈11.3B，‘~12B’落在这个区间内，是合理的近似换算。如果需要精确数字，应注明换算所用的具体汇率日期(比如‘按2025年12月31日汇率’或‘按年报披露当日汇率’)，因为汇率每天波动，‘~12B’本身已经是‘约数’的诚实表达(用了‘~’符号)。

② Mufengda 穆峰达 (Tirzepatide 2.5–15mg/wk) | Eli Lilly | Jul 19, 2024 | GLP-1/GIP dual | BMI≥28; 或≥24+合并症 | Zepbound FY2025: ~USD 13.5B [Lilly Q4 2025, Feb 4 2026]

数字细节：来源标注‘[Lilly Q4 2025, Feb 4 2026]’——这不是‘年报(Annual Report)’，而是‘第四季度财报发布(Q4 earnings release)’，发布日期2026年2月4日。这意味着‘Zepbound FY2025’这个全年数据，是在2026年2月通过‘全年业绩总结’的财报发布会公布的——这是上市公司‘财报季(earnings season)’的标准时间表(通常在财年结束后1-2个月内发布Q4及全年业绩)。

BMI≥28/≥24+ — 与Wegovy的BMI≥30/≥27+对比：这一行再次出现Slide 4里讨论过的‘不同产品BMI门槛不同’现象——Mufengda(穆峰达)的门槛(≥28/≥24+)比Wegovy(≥30/≥27+)更低，意味着‘理论可及人群范围更广’。这一列(China BMI Criteria)在这一页第一次以‘逐行对比’的形式呈现Slide 4脚注里提到的门槛差异，让‘产品specific门槛’这件事从‘Slide 4的一句话举例’变成‘Slide 7的6行完整数据’——这是‘定义在哪里展开、细节在哪里完整呈现’的报告结构设计。

③ 信尔美 (Mazdutide/IBI362) | Innovent Biologics (Lilly partner) | Jun 27, 2025 | GLP-1/GCG dual (world’s 1st) | BMI≥28; 或≥24+合并症 | Company-stated 1st GCG/GLP-1 dual agonist globally [NMPA; Innovent PRNewswire]

“Innovent Biologics (Lilly partner)” — 为什么要特别标注“(Lilly partner)”：这是一个非常重要、容易被忽略的细节——信达生物(Innovent)被标注为‘Lilly partner(礼来的合作伙伴)’，暗示信尔美(Mazdutide)的开发/商业化背后，可能存在与礼来(Eli Lilly，也就是上面②穆峰达的厂商)的合作关系。这意味着：表格里看起来‘国产vs MNC’对立的②③两行，背后的公司关系可能并不是‘纯粹竞争’，而可能存在‘合作/授权(licensing)’的复杂关系——这是‘4个国产获批’这个数字背后，需要留意的‘股权/合作结构’复杂性，不是所有‘国产’都是‘完全自主、零MNC关联’的。

“(world's 1st)” + “Company-stated” — 这个组合用词如何“自我设限”：‘world's 1st’(全球第一)是一个极强的声明，但前面加上‘Company-stated(公司自己声称)’，把这个声明的‘责任主体’明确归于‘信达/Innovent公司自己’，而不是‘分析师认证的事实’或‘第三方权威机构认证’。来源标注‘[NMPA; Innovent PRNewswire]’——NMPA对应‘获批’这个事实(Tier1)，PRNewswire对应‘world's 1st GCG/GLP-1 dual agonist’这个‘定位声明’(Tier2，且是公司自己的营销话语)。这种写法把‘监管事实’和‘公司营销声明’分开标注来源，体现了‘不同性质的信息匹配不同来源’的一贯原则。

④ Ecnoglutide (XW003) (cAMP-biased GLP-1) | Sciwind Biosciences | Mar 6, 2026 | cAMP-biased GLP-1RA (world's 1st) | Adults with obesity or overweight | ~15.1% adj. wt loss (Ph3) [Sciwind PRNewswire Mar 6 2026]

这一行的BMI Criteria列写的是“Adults with obesity or overweight”，而不是像其他5行那样给出具体BMI数字——这是这一页最值得主动指出的“数据空白”：其他5行的‘China BMI Criteria’列都是‘BMI≥X; 或≥Y+合并症’这种精确的数值化表达；Ecnoglutide这一行写的是定性描述‘Adults with obesity or overweight(成人肥胖或超重患者)’，没有给出具体BMI切点。结合这一行的来源仅为‘[Sciwind PRNewswire Mar 6 2026]’(纯Tier2)，一个合理的解释是：截至研究节点(2026年6月)，Ecnoglutide刚获批仅约3个月，其完整的NMPA说明书(包含精确BMI适应症切点)可能还未在公开渠道(如药智网/NMPA官网药品说明书查询)完全收录或更新，公司新闻稿对适应症的描述通常更笼统(‘obesity or overweight’)，而不会像说明书一样精确到‘≥28/≥24+’这种数字。

⑤ 利鲁平 Liluping (Liraglutide 3mg/day SC) | Huadong Medicine 华东医药 | Jul 4, 2023 | GLP-1 agonist | BMI≥30; 或≥27+合并症 | Domestic; revenue not separately disclosed ⑥ 菲塑美 Feisumei (Beinaglutide daily SC) | Benemae Pharma 仁会生物 | Jul 27, 2023 | GLP-1 agonist | BMI≥28; 或≥24+合并症 | Domestic; revenue not separately disclosed

两行的共同特征：都是2023年7月获批(整条时间线最早的两个事件，相隔仅23天)；都是‘GLP-1 agonist’单靶点机制(对应Slide 4分类①，且都不在Slide 5的5个疗效数据点之内——Slide 5的5行里利拉鲁肽是‘Liraglutide 3mg(Saxenda)’，引用的是Novo Nordisk的全球产品Saxenda，而不是华东医药的‘利鲁平’这个国产仿制/类似药版本——这是另一个值得注意的‘品牌-分子映射’细节)；都标注‘revenue not separately disclosed(营收未单独披露)’。

“利鲁平(华东医药)”与“Saxenda(诺和诺德的利拉鲁肽)”是同一个分子(利拉鲁肽)的不同品牌——这是一个潜在的“跨页一致性”问题：Slide 5表格第①行‘Liraglutide 3mg (Saxenda — SCALE, 56w)’引用的是诺和诺德原研产品Saxenda在SCALE试验里的疗效数据(~5-6%)；而这一页第⑤行‘利鲁平(华东医药)’是‘利拉鲁肽’这个分子的另一个中国本土品牌(可能是仿制药或生物类似药)。两者是‘同一个活性成分(利拉鲁肽)，不同品牌/不同厂商’。如果被问到‘Slide 5引用的Saxenda疗效数据(~5-6%)，能不能代表利鲁平的疗效’，回答逻辑应该和Slide 5里‘Tirzepatide/Zepbound vs 穆峰达’的回答类似：分子相同，疗效证据的源头相同(SCALE试验)，但‘利鲁平’作为国产版本是否有独立的、针对中国人群的桥接试验数据，目前没有在这份报告里列出。

“revenue not separately disclosed” — 为什么两行用完全相同的措辞，且和KEY INSIGHT如何呼应：这句‘营收未单独披露’的措辞在两行里完全一致，这是‘标准化的数据缺口声明’——表明分析师对这两款产品做了同样的‘尝试查找营收数据但未找到’的核实过程，得到了同样的结果。这两行的‘数据缺口’和KEY INSIGHT里‘China-only revenue for these products is not publicly disclosed’的声明是‘一脉相承’的——KEY INSIGHT那句话其实适用于全部6行(包括①②的‘Global’营收，也不是‘China-only’)，而⑤⑥这两行更进一步：‘连Global营收也没有单独披露’(因为华东医药/仁会生物的利鲁平/菲塑美产品线在其财报里可能没有单独成项，被归入更大的产品组合中)。

EN — Row-by-row (condensed): ① Wegovy (Novo Nordisk, Jun 25 2024, GLP-1 agonist, BMI≥30/≥27+, Wegovy FY2025 DKK79.1B≈USD12B [2025 AR]) — Tier1 annual-report figure; the DKK→USD ‘~12B’ is an honest approximation (exchange rates fluctuate daily). ② Mufengda (Eli Lilly, Jul 19 2024, GLP-1/GIP dual, BMI≥28/≥24+, Zepbound FY2025 ~USD13.5B [Lilly Q4 2025, Feb 4 2026]) — sourced to a Q4 EARNINGS RELEASE (not an AR), reflecting standard post-fiscal-year earnings-season timing; its lower BMI threshold (≥28/≥24+) vs. Wegovy’s (≥30/≥27+) is the first ROW-LEVEL instantiation of Slide 4’s ‘product-specific BMI threshold’ footnote. ③ Mazdutide/信尔美 (Innovent Biologics — NOTE explicitly tagged ‘(Lilly partner)’, Jun 27 2025, GLP-1/GCG dual ‘world’s 1st’, BMI≥28/≥24+, [NMPA; Innovent PRNewswire]) — the ‘(Lilly partner)’ tag is an easily-missed but important detail: it signals that the ‘domestic vs. MNC’ framing of rows ②/③ may actually involve a licensing/partnership relationship rather than pure competition, complicating the ‘4 of 6 domestic’ headline. The ‘world’s 1st’ claim is explicitly tagged ‘Company-stated,’ separating the regulatory FACT (NMPA approval, Tier1) from the company’s MARKETING claim (PRNewswire, Tier2). ④ Ecnoglutide (Sciwind, Mar 6 2026, cAMP-biased GLP-1RA ‘world’s 1st’, BMI Criteria written as qualitative ‘Adults with obesity or overweight’ rather than a numeric threshold like the other 5 rows — likely because, only ~3 months post-approval, the full NMPA label hasn’t been fully indexed publicly;. ⑤⑥ Liluping (Huadong Medicine, Jul 4 2023) and Feisumei (Benemae Pharma/仁会生物, Jul 27 2023) — the two oldest approvals (23 days apart), both single-target GLP-1 agonists, both ‘revenue not separately disclosed.’ Liluping is a DOMESTIC brand of the SAME molecule (liraglutide) as Slide 5’s Saxenda — same molecule, different brand/manufacturer, raising the same ‘does the cited Phase-3 data represent this brand’s efficacy’ question discussed for Tirzepatide/Zepbound vs. Mufengda on Slide 5. The identical ‘revenue not separately disclosed’ wording for both rows is a standardized data-gap disclosure, and directly underlies the KEY INSIGHT’s broader disclaimer that China-only revenue isn’t publicly disclosed for ANY of the 6 products.

6. KEY INSIGHT 横条 The Page’s Thesis Bar

原文：“China's obesity GLP-1 market went from zero to six approved products in 36 months. Domestic companies now hold 4 of 6 approvals. Revenue data shown is global, not China-specific — China-only revenue for these products is not publicly disclosed.”

三句话的功能分工：第一句‘zero to six in 36 months’是对副标题‘~3 Years’和时间线的‘数字化总结’(尽管如前所述，36个月这个数字与精确日历计算的32个月存在偏差)；第二句‘Domestic companies now hold 4 of 6 approvals’是这一页最重要的‘数量结论’，直接对应表格里⑤⑥(利鲁平/菲塑美)+③(信尔美/Innovent)+④(Ecnoglutide/Sciwind) = 4家中国公司，VS ①②(诺和诺德/礼来) = 2家MNC；第三句‘Revenue data shown is global, not China-specific…not publicly disclosed’是‘数据局限性声明’，适用于全部6行的最后一列。

“Domestic companies now hold 4 of 6 approvals” — 这句话最大的潜在攻击点：“数量领先”是否等于“市场领先”：这句话本身只是一个‘获批数量’的客观统计——4/6是事实(可逐行验证)。但如果不加限定，读者可能会把‘获批数量4/6(国产领先)’和‘市场地位’混为一谈。而紧跟着的第三句‘Revenue data shown is global...not publicly disclosed’恰好起到了‘平衡’作用——它间接提示读者：‘虽然国产产品数量上是4/6，但表格里唯一能看到的‘真金白银’的营收数字(Wegovy的DKK79.1B和Mufengda的USD13.5B)，都来自那2家MNC’，国产4款产品里有2款(信尔美/Ecnoglutide)只有‘世界第一’的定位声明和疗效数字，另外2款(利鲁平/菲塑美)连营收都没有披露。所以‘4 of 6’和‘营收数据局限’这两句话放在一起，实际上构成了一组‘数量vs质量(规模)’的对照——KEY INSIGHT没有直接说‘国产虽然数量多但规模还小’，但通过‘并列陈述事实、不下结论’的方式，让读者自己得出这个对比。

Original text: “China's obesity GLP-1 market went from zero to six approved products in 36 months. Domestic companies now hold 4 of 6 approvals. Revenue data shown is global, not China-specific — China-only revenue for these products is not publicly disclosed.”

Division of labor across the three sentences: Sentence 1 (‘zero to six in 36 months’) is a numeric summary of the subtitle’s ‘~3 Years’ and the timeline (though, as noted, ‘36 months’ deviates slightly from the precise 32-month calendar gap). Sentence 2 (‘Domestic companies now hold 4 of 6 approvals’) is the page’s most important COUNT-based conclusion, mapping to rows ⑤⑥ (Liluping/Feisumei) + ③ (Mazdutide/Innovent) + ④ (Ecnoglutide/Sciwind) = 4 Chinese companies, vs. ①② (Novo Nordisk/Eli Lilly) = 2 MNCs. Sentence 3 (‘Revenue data shown is global, not China-specific...not publicly disclosed’) is a DATA-LIMITATION disclosure applying to the last column across all 6 rows.

‘Domestic companies hold 4 of 6’ — the biggest latent challenge: does ‘leading in count’ equal ‘leading in market’: This sentence is itself just an objective approval-count statistic — 4/6 is verifiable row-by-row. But without qualification, a reader might conflate ‘4/6 approvals (domestic-leading)’ with ‘market position.’ Sentence 3 immediately following provides the BALANCE — it indirectly signals: ‘even though domestic products lead 4/6 in COUNT, the only REAL revenue figures visible in the table (Wegovy’s DKK79.1B and Mufengda’s USD13.5B) both come from the 2 MNCs’; of the 4 domestic products, 2 (Mazdutide/Ecnoglutide) only have ‘world’s first’ positioning claims and efficacy figures (not revenue), and the other 2 (Liluping/Feisumei) don’t even have disclosed revenue. So ‘4 of 6’ and ‘revenue data limitation’ together form a QUANTITY vs. QUALITY (scale) juxtaposition — the KEY INSIGHT never explicitly says ‘domestic leads in count but trails in scale,’ but by stating both facts side-by-side without drawing the conclusion, it lets the reader arrive at that contrast themselves.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK“‘Domestic companies now hold 4 of 6 approvals’——但其中信尔美(Innovent)被你自己标注为‘(Lilly partner)’，如果它和礼来有合作关系，算‘纯国产’吗？如果不算，是不是应该是‘3 of 6’？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER这是一个很好的‘定义边界’问题。‘domestic company(本土企业)’的判定标准，通常基于‘公司注册地/上市地/主要研发和生产基地’，而不是‘是否与任何外资企业有任何形式的合作’——信达生物(Innovent)是在香港上市、总部位于中国苏州的生物制药企业，按‘公司主体’的标准，它是‘中国本土企业’。‘(Lilly partner)’标注的是‘信达生物在某些产品上与礼来存在合作/授权关系’这个事实(这种合作在创新药行业很常见，比如license-in/license-out、联合开发等)，但这不改变‘信达生物作为公司主体的国籍/注册属性’。所以‘信尔美算国产产品’这个判断，依据的是‘开发主体/上市许可持有人(MAH，Marketing Authorization Holder)是谁’，而不是‘这个产品的研发历史上是否存在过任何跨国合作’——按这个标准，4/6是合理的。但您提的这一点提醒我：‘domestic vs MNC’这个二元分类，在创新药行业里因为license-in/license-out、合作开发非常普遍，实际上是一个‘光谱’而不是‘绝对的二分类’——如果要更严谨，应该在‘(Lilly partner)’这类标注旁边，进一步说明‘合作的具体性质(比如是‘信达licensed-in某个海外分子在中国开发’，还是‘信达自主研发、礼来仅为商业化合作伙伴’)’，这会让‘4 of 6’这个数字的‘含金量’更清晰。

EN： That's a great 'boundary of definition' question. Whether a company counts as 'domestic' is normally judged by where it's incorporated/listed and where its main R&D and manufacturing sites are — not by whether it has any form of partnership with a foreign company. Innovent is a Hong Kong-listed biopharma headquartered in Suzhou, China, so by the 'corporate entity' standard it IS a Chinese domestic company. The '(Lilly partner)' label simply flags the fact that Innovent has a collaboration/licensing relationship with Lilly on certain products — a very common arrangement in innovative drugs (license-in/license-out, co-development, etc.) — but that doesn't change Innovent's nationality/registration as a corporate entity. So 'Mazdutide counts as domestic' is based on WHO the developing entity / Marketing Authorization Holder (MAH) is, not on whether there's EVER been any cross-border collaboration in the product's R&D history — by that standard, 4/6 is reasonable. But your question is a good reminder: because license-in/license-out and co-development are so common in innovative pharma, 'domestic vs. MNC' is really more of a spectrum than a strict binary. To be more rigorous, a label like '(Lilly partner)' should ideally spell out the NATURE of the collaboration (e.g., 'Innovent licensed-in an overseas molecule for China development' vs. 'Innovent developed it independently and Lilly is only a commercialization partner') — that would make the 'real meaning' of the '4 of 6' figure much clearer.

domestic company 是什么？

domestic company = 本土企业 / 国内企业。

判断一个公司是不是本土企业，主要看：

公司总部在哪里；

公司注册在哪里；

主要研发、生产、商业化主体是谁；

上市许可持有人是谁。

7. 底部脚注 — 六条引用逐一核对 Footnote — Six Citations Checked

原文：“Liluping: Huadong Medicine Jul 4 2023; ChemLinked. Feisumei: Benemae Pharma/NMPA Jul 2023. Wegovy: NMPA Jun 25 2024; Reuters. Mufengda: Reuters Jul 19 2024. 信尔美: NMPA nmpa.gov.cn Jun 27 2025; Innovent PRNewswire. Ecnoglutide: Sciwind PRNewswire Mar 6 2026.”

6条引用 ↔ 6行数据的一对一映射，且每条都包含‘日期+来源’两个要素：和Slide 5的脚注设计一致——每个产品都有独立的引用，确保‘可追溯性’。但这6条引用的‘来源类型组合’各不相同：利鲁平=‘公司公告(Huadong Medicine) + ChemLinked’；菲塑美=‘公司(Benemae Pharma)/NMPA’；诺和盈=‘NMPA + Reuters’；穆峰达=‘仅Reuters’；信尔美=‘NMPA官网 + Innovent PRNewswire’；Ecnoglutide=‘仅Sciwind PRNewswire’。

“ChemLinked” — 一个新出现、之前几页都没提到的来源类型：ChemLinked是一个专注于中国医药/化妆品/食品法规与市场情报的英文行业资讯平台(隶属于Reachpharm/CIRS集团)，主要服务于希望了解中国监管动态的外资企业。把ChemLinked归类，大致属于Slide 3 Tier2里的‘专业医药媒体(类似Fierce Pharma/BioSpace，但聚焦中国法规)’——它的特点是‘英文报道中国监管事件’，对于这份报告(英文撰写、可能面向国际读者或双语背景的面试官)来说，是一个‘桥接中文监管信息和英文读者’的实用来源。

“穆峰达: Reuters Jul 19 2024” — 唯一一行“只有一个来源、且没有NMPA官方引用”的产品：其他5行都至少包含‘公司公告/NMPA/ChemLinked’中的一个‘官方或半官方’来源，但穆峰达这一行只标注了‘Reuters(路透社)’——按Slide 3的定义，路透社属于Tier2(‘主要通讯社’)，是‘对一手事件的报道’，原始一手来源(NMPA批准公告) 应该存在，但脚注里没有单独列出。这是这一页脚注里相对‘可以补强’的一处——理想情况下应该补充‘NMPA官网穆峰达肥胖适应症批准记录’的直接引用，使其和其他5行的‘来源完整度’保持一致。

Original text: “Liluping: Huadong Medicine Jul 4 2023; ChemLinked. Feisumei: Benemae Pharma/NMPA Jul 2023. Wegovy: NMPA Jun 25 2024; Reuters. Mufengda: Reuters Jul 19 2024. 信尔美: NMPA nmpa.gov.cn Jun 27 2025; Innovent PRNewswire. Ecnoglutide: Sciwind PRNewswire Mar 6 2026.”

6 citations ↔ 6 rows, one-to-one, each with date + source: Consistent with Slide 5’s footnote design — every product has an independent citation ensuring traceability. But the SOURCE-TYPE COMBINATION differs per row: Liluping = ‘company announcement (Huadong Medicine) + ChemLinked’; Feisumei = ‘company (Benemae Pharma)/NMPA’; Wegovy = ‘NMPA + Reuters’; Mufengda = ‘Reuters only’; Mazdutide = ‘NMPA website + Innovent PRNewswire’; Ecnoglutide = ‘Sciwind PRNewswire only.’

‘ChemLinked’ — a new source type not mentioned on earlier pages: ChemLinked is an English-language industry-intelligence platform focused on China pharma/cosmetics/food regulatory and market news (part of the Reachpharm/CIRS group), primarily serving foreign companies tracking China’s regulatory developments. It fits Slide 3’s Tier2 ‘specialist trade media’ category (akin to Fierce Pharma/BioSpace, but China-regulation-focused) — useful as a bridge between Chinese regulatory information and an English-reading audience (relevant for this English-language, possibly bilingual-interview-context report).

‘Mufengda: Reuters Jul 19 2024’ — the only row with a SINGLE source and no NMPA citation: Every other row includes at least one ‘official or semi-official’ source (company announcement/NMPA/ChemLinked), but Mufengda’s row cites only Reuters — a Tier2 ‘major wire service’ per Slide 3’s definition, i.e., ‘reporting on a primary event,’ whose primary source (the NMPA approval announcement) presumably exists but isn’t separately cited. This is a place this footnote could be strengthened — ideally adding a direct citation to ‘NMPA’s Mufengda obesity-indication approval record’ to bring it to parity with the other 5 rows’ source completeness.

8. 总结：这一页在“埋”什么 Summary — What This Slide Plants

元素 / Element

⭐ 这一页最该背的一句话 / The Sentence to Memorize

“中国GLP-1肥胖市场在约32-36个月内(2023年7月-2026年3月，不同页面有33/36个月的不同四舍五入表达)从0到6款NMPA批准产品；其中4款来自中国本土企业(华东医药/利鲁平、仁会生物/菲塑美、信达生物/信尔美、先为达/Ecnoglutide)，2款来自MNC(诺和诺德/诺和盈、礼来/穆峰达)；但表格里唯一可见的真实营收数字(诺和盈DKK79.1B、穆峰达USD13.5B)都来自这2家MNC，且都是全球营收、非中国specific；2款国产创新药(信尔美/Ecnoglutide)的‘全球首个’地位是公司自己的声明(Company-stated)，2款最早的国产药(利鲁平/菲塑美)连营收都未单独披露。所以‘国产4/6’是‘数量上的事实’，不能直接等同于‘商业规模上的领先’——这也是为什么KEY INSIGHT把‘数量’和‘营收数据局限’放在同一段，让读者自己做对比，而不是直接下结论。”

“China’s obesity GLP-1 market went from zero to six NMPA-approved products in roughly 32–36 months (Jul 2023–Mar 2026; different pages round this differently). Of the 6, four are domestic (Huadong/Liluping, Benemae/Feisumei, Innovent/Mazdutide, Sciwind/Ecnoglutide) and two are MNC (Novo Nordisk/Wegovy, Eli Lilly/Mufengda) — but the ONLY real revenue figures visible (Wegovy’s DKK79.1B, Mufengda’s USD13.5B) come from the 2 MNCs, both global not China-specific. The two domestic innovators’ ‘world’s first’ claims are company-stated, and the two oldest domestic products don’t even have disclosed revenue. So ‘4 of 6 domestic’ is a COUNT fact, not equivalent to commercial-scale leadership — which is why the KEY INSIGHT juxtaposes the count with the revenue-data limitation, letting the reader draw the contrast rather than stating a conclusion.”

9. 综合问题：设计这一页要考虑哪些因素？数据来源都在哪？ Design Factors & Where to Find Sources

设计这一页（已批产品实体清单页）要考虑的因素：

① 与前序页面的接口一致性——表格的每一列、每一行是否能在Slide 1/4/5/6里找到对应的‘坐标系’，避免‘孤立信息’；② 排序逻辑的双重性——时间线(时间顺序)与表格(相关性顺序)的并存是否会引发‘不一致’的疑问，是否需要额外说明；③ 数据异质性的诚实呈现——同一列(Revenue/Evidence Ref.)对不同产品承载不同性质的信息(财务数字/公司声明/数据缺口)，是否每一种都标注清楚；④ 公司归属的复杂性——‘domestic vs MNC’的二元标签在license-in/out普遍的行业里是否需要更细致的说明(如‘(Lilly partner)’标注)；⑤ 跨页数字精度的一致性——比如‘33个月’(Slide1) vs ‘36个月’(Slide7) vs ‘~3 years’(Slide7副标题)，以及Slide5‘15.1%” vs Slide7‘15.1% adj.”的标注差异。

我所知道的、与这一页相关的数据来源类型：

【监管批准记录】NMPA官网‘药品查询’/‘行政许可信息’栏目——查询具体产品的批准日期、适应症、说明书；CDE官网‘药品审评进度公示’。

【公司年报/财报】Novo Nordisk Annual Report(诺和诺德官网Investor栏目)；Eli Lilly Quarterly/Annual Earnings Release(礼来官网Investor Relations，10-K/10-Q via SEC EDGAR)；信达生物/华东医药/仁会生物的港交所/上交所披露易年报。

【行业法规情报平台】ChemLinked(chemlinked.com)——英文报道中国药品/食品/化妆品法规动态，适合查询‘某药品在中国获批’这类事件的英文报道；药智网/医药魔方——中文行业数据库，查询药品说明书、上市许可持有人(MAH)信息。

【通讯社新闻】Reuters/Bloomberg——搜索‘公司名+drug name+China approval’查询获批报道。

【公司新闻稿】各公司Newsroom/PRNewswire/GlobeNewswire——查询最新获批/数据发布的公司声明，注意区分‘公司声明(如world's 1st)’和‘监管事实(NMPA批准)’。

【汇率数据】用于DKK→USD等换算——可查Bloomberg/XE.com历史汇率，或直接使用公司年报里‘管理层讨论与分析(MD&A)’章节给出的换算汇率(公司通常会注明用于财务报表换算的汇率假设)。

具体去哪找（实操路径）：

① 查某产品NMPA批准记录与说明书 → nmpa.gov.cn → ‘数据查询’→‘国产药品’或‘进口药品’，输入药品名称查询批准文号、适应症、说明书PDF。 ② 查公司年报营收 → 港股公司用hkexnews.hk搜公司名找年报PDF；美股/欧股公司(Novo Nordisk/Eli Lilly)用公司官网Investor Relations或SEC EDGAR(sec.gov/edgar)搜10-K/20-F。 ③ 查‘某药品中国获批’的英文报道 → chemlinked.com站内搜索药品名或公司名；或在reuters.com/bloomberg.com搜索‘公司名+drug name+China NMPA approval’。 ④ 查‘上市许可持有人(MAH)/合作关系’ → 药智网(yaozh.com)或医药魔方(pharmcube.com)输入药品名查询MAH信息及合作授权历史；公司官网‘Pipeline’页面通常会注明‘in collaboration with...’。 ⑤ 查汇率换算依据 → 公司年报‘Notes to Financial Statements’或MD&A章节通常会注明‘average/closing exchange rate used’；或xe.com查询历史汇率。 ⑥ 查‘营收未单独披露’的验证 → 在该公司年报里搜索产品名(如‘利鲁平’/‘Liraglutide’)，如果只在‘产品管线介绍’章节出现、未出现在‘分产品收入明细表’中，即可佐证‘未单独披露’。

Factors to consider when designing this ‘approved products entity list’ page: ① interface consistency with prior pages — does every column/row map onto a coordinate system established on Slides 1/4/5/6, avoiding ‘orphan information’; ② dual ordering logic — does the coexistence of a chronological timeline and a relevance-ordered table raise ‘inconsistency’ questions that need addressing; ③ honest presentation of data heterogeneity — the same column (Revenue/Evidence Ref.) carries different KINDS of information (financial figures / company claims / data gaps) for different products — is each type clearly labeled; ④ complexity of company attribution — does the ‘domestic vs. MNC’ binary need finer notation (e.g., ‘(Lilly partner)’) in an industry where licensing is common; ⑤ cross-page numeric precision consistency — e.g., ‘33 months’ (Slide1) vs. ‘36 months’ (Slide7) vs. ‘~3 years’ (Slide7 subtitle), and Slide5’s ‘15.1%” vs. Slide7’s ‘15.1% adj.”

Data source types relevant to this page: [Regulatory approval records] NMPA website ‘Drug Query’/‘Administrative Licensing Information’ for approval dates, indications, label PDFs; CDE ‘Drug Review Status Disclosure.’ [Company financials] Novo Nordisk Annual Report (Investor section); Eli Lilly quarterly/annual earnings releases (IR page, 10-K/10-Q via SEC EDGAR); Innovent/Huadong Medicine/Benemae Pharma annual reports via HKEX/SSE disclosure portals. [Industry regulatory-intel platforms] ChemLinked (chemlinked.com) for English coverage of China drug/food/cosmetics regulatory events; Yaozh.com/Pharmcube for Chinese drug-label and Marketing Authorization Holder (MAH) data. [Wire services] Reuters/Bloomberg — search ‘company + drug + China approval.’ [Company press releases] Newsroom/PRNewswire/GlobeNewswire — for latest approvals/data, distinguishing company CLAIMS (e.g., ‘world’s 1st’) from regulatory FACTS (NMPA approval). [Exchange-rate data] for DKK→USD etc. — Bloomberg/XE.com historical rates, or the rate disclosed in a company’s MD&A section.

Practical paths: ① NMPA approval record & label → nmpa.gov.cn → ‘Data Query’ → ‘Domestic Drugs’/‘Imported Drugs’, search by drug name for approval number, indication, label PDF. ② company revenue → HK-listed: hkexnews.hk for AR PDFs; US/EU-listed (Novo Nordisk/Eli Lilly): company IR pages or SEC EDGAR (sec.gov/edgar) for 10-K/20-F. ③ English coverage of ‘China approval’ → search chemlinked.com by drug/company name, or reuters.com/bloomberg.com for ‘company + drug + China NMPA approval.’ ④ MAH/partnership info → yaozh.com or pharmcube.com, search drug name for MAH and licensing history; company ‘Pipeline’ pages often note ‘in collaboration with...’ ⑤ exchange-rate basis → company AR ‘Notes to Financial Statements’/MD&A for ‘average/closing exchange rate used’, or xe.com for historical rates. ⑥ verifying ‘revenue not separately disclosed’ → search the product name in the company’s AR; if it appears only in the ‘pipeline overview’ section and not in a ‘revenue by product’ table, that supports ‘not separately disclosed.’

10. 面试官深度追问 / Deep-Dive Grilling — 营收数据被深挖

[CRITICAL] 诺和盈全球营收USD 120亿——但中国数字是多少？为什么没有？

⚠ ATTACK "You show Wegovy at USD 12 billion — but that's global. What's the China number? Why don't you have it?"

EN： China-specific GLP-1 obesity revenue is not separately disclosed by Novo Nordisk as of June 2026. What's public: Novo Nordisk's China total GLP-1 revenue ≈ USD 1B for all indications in 2024 — but this includes Ozempic for diabetes, a much larger China indication than obesity, and the company doesn't split obesity from diabetes revenue in China. I include the global Wegovy figure as commercial proof-of-concept — it shows the franchise has proven global commercial viability — but I do not use it as a China market-size input. My China market size comes from the bottom-up model, not company revenue disclosure.

中：截至2026年6月，诺和诺德未单独披露中国肥胖 GLP-1 营收。公开可用的是诺和诺德中国全适应症 GLP-1 总营收——2024年约USD 10亿，但包含糖尿病 Ozempic（中国更大的适应症），公司不拆分中国肥胖与糖尿病营收。我引用全球诺和盈数字作为商业验证（证明司美格鲁肽肥胖品牌具有全球商业可行性），但不用于中国市场规模输入——中国市场规模来自自下而上模型，不来自公司营收披露。

[MEDIUM] 信尔美2025年上市、Ecnoglutide 2026年3月获批——基本没有营收，为什么列入已批产品？

⚠ ATTACK "Mazdutide launched in 2025 and Ecnoglutide in March 2026 — they have almost no revenue yet. Why include them in the approved products slide?"

EN： This slide's purpose is to document the regulatory landscape — what's NMPA-approved and when. Revenue is a secondary data point shown where available. For recently-launched/just-approved products, the absence of disclosed revenue is itself informative: it shows the market is still nascent, with most commercial volume concentrated in Wegovy and Mufengda. Including Mazdutide and Ecnoglutide without revenue is accurate and honest — it reflects the regulatory reality of six approvals while acknowledging the limited commercial history of newer entrants.

中：本页目的是记录监管格局——哪些产品获得 NMPA 批准以及何时获批。营收是次要数据点，有则展示。对近期上市/刚批准的产品，"无披露营收"本身就有信息价值：说明市场仍处于新兴阶段，大部分商业销量集中在诺和盈和穆峰达。不带营收数据列入信尔美和 Ecnoglutide 是准确且诚实的——反映了6个批准的监管现实，同时承认新进入者有限的商业记录。

Slide 8 Pipeline 管线

Representative China GLP-1 Pipeline — Detailed Line-by-Line Analysis (Bilingual)
Overview

这一页是Slide 6“解决方向(箭头)”和Slide 7“已批6款产品”的“未来时”——前面所有页面讨论的都是“已经发生”的事(已批准的产品、已发表的疗效)，这一页第一次把镜头转向“还没发生、但即将发生”的事：哪些产品正在路上，它们会怎样改变Slide 6里‘价格’和‘依从性’这两个关键变量。这一页也是全篇‘数据来源最难标准化’的一页——因为管线数据本质上是‘尚未定型的信息’(NDA受理日期、Phase状态、早期疗效数字都可能随时变化)，所以这一页放弃了Slide 5-7那种‘底部统一脚注’的格式，转而把‘来源/限制条件’直接嵌入每一行的‘Key Milestone’列——这是一个值得主动指出的‘格式差异’。

This page is the ‘future tense’ of Slide 6’s ‘solution arrows’ and Slide 7’s ‘6 approved products’ — every prior page discussed things that have ALREADY happened (approved products, published efficacy); this page is the first to turn the camera toward what hasn’t happened yet but is COMING, and how it will reshape Slide 6’s two key variables, price and adherence. It’s also the hardest page in the deck to standardize sourcing for — pipeline data is inherently UNSETTLED (NDA-acceptance dates, phase status, and early efficacy figures can all change at any time) — so unlike Slides 5–7’s unified bottom footnote, this page embeds sources/caveats directly into each row’s ‘Key Milestone’ column — a format difference worth proactively noting.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK“60-70个资产里，你选出来的5个是怎么挑的？有没有可能你只挑了‘看起来威胁最大’的5个，制造一种‘国产药很快就会赶超’的紧迫感，而忽略了大部分资产其实进展缓慢或已经失败？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER这是一个非常合理的‘选择性偏差(selection bias)’质疑，我想分两部分回答。第一，这一页的选择标准在标题里已经写明：‘high-priority near-term obesity threats(高优先级、近期的肥胖适应症威胁)’——也就是说，筛选维度是‘适应症必须是肥胖(排除纯糖尿病管线)’+‘时间维度必须是near-term(已经进入Phase3/NDA阶段，而不是早期Phase1/临床前)’。60-70这个数字里，大部分可能是‘早期阶段(Phase2)’或‘糖尿病适应症’的资产，按照这两个筛选条件，能进入‘肥胖+近期’这个交集的资产数量本身就会大幅减少，5个是‘筛选后剩余的代表性样本’，不是‘从60-70个里随便挑的5个’。第二，我确实没有列出‘筛选后还剩多少个、5个占筛选后总数的比例是多少’——这是一个可以改进的地方：如果能补充一句‘在60-70个资产中，约有X个进入Phase3或NDA阶段且适应症为肥胖，本表展示其中5个代表性资产’，会让‘代表性’这个词更有数据支撑。但即使有这个改进，‘选择5个里哪5个’仍然带有分析师的主观判断——我认为这种判断本身是合理的(选择‘疗效数字最高、监管进度最快’的几个，确实是‘威胁’的合理代理指标)，但应该承认这是‘分析师判断’，不是‘穷尽式列举’。

EN： That's a very fair 'selection bias' challenge, and I'd answer it in two parts. First, the selection criteria are stated in the title itself: 'high-priority near-term obesity threats' — meaning the filter is 'indication must be obesity (excluding pure diabetes pipelines)' AND 'timing must be near-term (already at Phase3/NDA, not early Phase1/preclinical).' Most of the 60–70 assets are likely either early-stage (Phase2) or diabetes-indication, so applying these two filters already shrinks the pool dramatically — the 5 shown are the representative remainder AFTER filtering, not '5 cherry-picked out of 60–70.' Second, I admittedly didn't state how many assets remain after filtering or what share the 5 represent — that's an area for improvement: adding a line like 'of the 60–70 assets, roughly X reach Phase3/NDA with an obesity indication, and this table shows 5 representative ones' would give 'representative' more data backing. But even with that improvement, WHICH 5 to show still involves analyst judgment — I think that judgment is itself reasonable (picking the assets with the highest efficacy and fastest regulatory progress is a sensible proxy for 'threat'), but it should be acknowledged as analyst judgment, not an exhaustive list.

2. 三色图例 — NEAR-TERM / MID-TERM / PRICE The Three-Badge Legend

原文：“NEAR-TERM — NDA submitted; potential approval early 2027”；“MID-TERM — Phase 3 / NDA accepted; not yet approved”；“PRICE — Biosimilar — may erode pricing floor post-2026”。

这三个徽章为什么不是“按公司”或“按机制”分类，而是“按对市场的影响类型+时间窗”分类：NEAR-TERM和MID-TERM都是‘时间维度’的分类(分别对应‘2027年初可能获批’和‘尚未获批，但已进入Phase3/NDA阶段’)，而PRICE是‘影响类型’的分类(不是时间，而是‘这一类资产对价格体系的冲击’)。这种‘两个时间维度+一个影响类型维度’混合的图例设计，反映了这一页试图回答的核心问题：‘Slide 6里的‘价格/依从性/医保’这三个决定市场规模的变量，会在什么时候、被什么类型的资产改变？’——NEAR-TERM/MID-TERM回答‘什么时候’，PRICE回答‘通过什么机制改变价格’。
