This page’s ‘Obese Proxy × ... × Annual Cost’ FORMULA presents 5 variables (Slide 9’s ①② merge into ‘Obese Proxy’; ③④ map to ‘Diagnosis’ and ‘Eligibility’; ⑤ maps to ‘Penetration’; and a new term, ‘Annual Cost per Patient,’ converts a patient COUNT into a DOLLAR figure) — emphasizing INDEPENDENCE: a formula implies each variable can be set independently and then multiplied.

The implicit ‘variable independence’ assumption — a simplification worth proactively flagging: A×B×C×D×E mathematically implies B doesn’t depend on A, C doesn’t depend on A or B, etc. — i.e., MUTUAL INDEPENDENCE. In reality, ‘Diagnosis’ and ‘Penetration’ are likely NOT fully independent — regions with HIGHER diagnosis rates (e.g., Tier-1/2 cities with richer healthcare resources) likely ALSO have HIGHER penetration rates (same reason — richer resources/affordability), meaning diagnosis and penetration may be POSITIVELY CORRELATED rather than independent. If positively correlated, the simple product ‘diagnosis% × penetration%’ likely UNDERSTATES the true joint probability of ‘diagnosed AND penetrated’ (since correlated variables produce a higher joint probability than the product of independent ones). This is an inherent limitation of MOST bottom-up/top-down market models, which use multiplicative formulas because directly estimating a JOINT DISTRIBUTION is impractical with limited data — but acknowledging ‘the formula assumes independence; reality may show positive correlation (likely understating, not overstating, the result)’ is an honest, directionally-informed answer.

3. 表格行①②：人口/患病率基数 — 三档情景中“唯一不变”的两行 Rows ①② — the Only Two Rows Held Constant Across Scenarios

行①“Age 16+ proxy (NBS 2025 1% survey)”：三档情景均为‘1,173.7M’，来源标注‘NBS 2025 1% Population Sample Survey — Tier 1’。行②“Obese BMI ≥28 proxy (17.1%)”：三档情景均为‘17.1% → 200.7M’，来源标注‘Zhang et al. 2024 × NBS 2025 1% survey — Tier 1 proxy’。

为什么①②在三档情景里“完全不变” — 这意味着“情景差异”的来源被精确限定在哪几行：这是这一页‘三档情景’设计里最重要、但最容易被忽略的结构特征——‘三档情景(Conservative/Base/Optimistic)’的差异，100%来自‘行③④⑤(三个带*的ASSUMPTION行)’，行①②(人口和患病率，PRIMARY/Tier1数据)在三档情景里‘原封不动’。这意味着：‘这个模型的‘不确定性’，全部被归因于‘行为/商业假设(诊断率/适应症符合率/渗透率)’，‘流行病学事实(人口基数和肥胖率)’被视为‘确定的常数’’——这和Slide 6/9一致：‘流行病学是PRIMARY、相对确定的；经济行为变量才是‘gating variables’、需要做情景分析的对象’。

行①②首次出现“Tier 1”/“Tier 1 proxy”标签 — 与Slide 9的“PRIMARY”标签是同一含义吗：Slide 9用的是‘PRIMARY’(对二元判断：有官方/学术数据支撑 vs 分析师假设)；这一页行①用‘Tier 1’，行②用‘Tier 1 proxy’——‘Tier 1’直接呼应Slide 3里‘Tier1(官方统计/年报)’的定义；‘Tier 1 proxy’在‘Tier1’后面加了‘proxy(代理)’——呼应了我们在Slide 9里讨论的‘②是18+的proxy(用16+代替)、④的17.1%是‘10省研究方向性应用到全国’的proxy’这两层‘代理/近似’关系。‘PRIMARY’(Slide9)→‘Tier1/Tier1 proxy’(Slide10)，是‘同一套‘数据可信度’判断，在不同页面用了术语略有差异但内核一致的标注体系’——如果被问‘这两个标签是不是矛盾’，应该说明‘是同一个分级思路在不同页面的不同措辞，Slide10的‘Tier1/Tier1 proxy’更精确地区分了‘直接来自官方统计的数字(行①)’和‘需要做一次‘代理转换’的数字(行②)’’。

Row ① ‘Age 16+ proxy (NBS 2025 1% survey)’: 1,173.7M across all 3 scenarios, tagged ‘Tier 1’. Row ② ‘Obese BMI ≥28 proxy (17.1%)’: 17.1% → 200.7M across all 3 scenarios, tagged ‘Zhang et al. 2024 × NBS 2025 1% survey — Tier 1 proxy’.

Why ①② are COMPLETELY UNCHANGED across scenarios — pinning down WHERE ‘scenario difference’ comes from: This is the most important — and easiest to overlook — structural feature of the 3-scenario design: 100% of the Conservative/Base/Optimistic DIFFERENCE comes from rows ③④⑤ (the three *-tagged ASSUMPTION rows); rows ①② (population & prevalence, PRIMARY/Tier1) are HELD FIXED. This means: ‘ALL of this model’s uncertainty is attributed to behavioral/commercial assumptions (diagnosis/eligibility/penetration); epidemiological facts (population base & obesity rate) are treated as FIXED CONSTANTS’ — consistent with Slides 6/9: ‘epidemiology is PRIMARY and relatively certain; economic-behavioral variables are the ‘gating variables’ subject to scenario analysis.’

Rows ①②’s first appearance of ‘Tier 1’/‘Tier 1 proxy’ — same meaning as Slide 9’s ‘PRIMARY’: Slide 9 used ‘PRIMARY’ (a binary: official/academic-backed vs. analyst assumption); this page uses ‘Tier 1’ for row ① and ‘Tier 1 proxy’ for row ② — ‘Tier 1’ directly echoes Slide 3’s definition (official statistics/annual reports); ‘Tier 1 proxy’ adds ‘proxy’ after ‘Tier 1,’ echoing the two layers of ‘proxy/approximation’ discussed on Slide 9 (② is a proxy for 18+ using 16+; ④’s 17.1% is a ‘10-province directionally-applied” proxy for the nation). ‘PRIMARY’ (Slide9) → ‘Tier1/Tier1 proxy’ (Slide10) is the SAME credibility framework, expressed with slightly different terminology on different pages but consistent in spirit — if asked ‘are these two labels contradictory,’ the answer is they’re the same grading approach worded differently, with Slide10’s ‘Tier1/Tier1 proxy’ more precisely distinguishing ‘a number straight from official statistics (row ①)’ from ‘a number requiring one ‘proxy conversion’ step (row ②).’

4. 表格行③④⑤：三个带*的情景变量 Rows ③④⑤ — the Three *-Tagged Scenario Variables

行③“Diagnosis + treatment-seeking *”：17% / 20% / 23%，来源‘ANALYST ASSUMPTION — sensitivity-tested’。行④“Commercially reachable / label-eligible proxy *”：42% / 45% / 48%，来源‘ANALYST ASSUMPTION — NMPA label criteria’。行⑤“GLP-1 penetration rate 2025*”：0.8% / 1.0% / 1.2%，来源‘ANALYST ASSUMPTION — nascent, self-pay market’。

三行的“对称区间宽度” — ±3pp / ±3pp / ±0.2pp，这个“对称”本身说明了什么：行③(20%±3pp)、行④(45%±3pp)、行⑤(1.0%±0.2pp，相对幅度是±20%)——三行都是‘以Base Case为中心，正负对称浮动’的区间。这种‘对称区间’是市场模型里最常见的‘敏感性分析(sensitivity analysis)’做法——本质上是‘如果我对这个假设的‘真实值’不是100%确定，那么用‘Base±X’来表示‘我认为真实值大概率落在这个区间里’’。但‘对称’本身是一个‘建模选择’，不是‘从数据推导出来的事实’——比如，如果‘诊断率在中国是‘普遍低估’的(Slide 9里‘consistent with chronic disease underdiagnosis’)，那么‘诊断率20%’这个Base Case本身可能已经偏向‘保守’，‘真实值高于20%的可能性’可能大于‘真实值低于20%的可能性’——如果是这样，‘不对称区间(比如17%-28%，而不是17%-23%)’可能更符合‘诊断不足’这个判断的逻辑。这一页选择了‘对称±3pp’这种‘数学上简洁、但没有体现‘诊断不足’这一判断方向性’的处理方式。

行⑤“nascent, self-pay market”这个理由，为什么只用在“来源”列、没有用在“区间宽度”的设定上：行⑤的‘来源/Status’列写的是‘ANALYST ASSUMPTION — nascent, self-pay market(新兴、自费市场)’——这句话解释了‘为什么1.0%这个Base Case本身比美国的2%低’(Slide 9讨论过的‘锚定美国一半’)，但‘区间(0.8%-1.2%)’本身的宽度(±0.2pp，相对±20%)，并没有被‘nascent self-pay market’这个理由进一步说明——比如‘新兴市场的渗透率，是不是应该比‘成熟市场’有‘更宽的不确定性区间(因为新兴市场的数据更少、波动性更大)’？如果是，±20%这个相对区间宽度，可能‘偏窄’(低估了‘新兴市场’本身带来的额外不确定性)。这是‘来源理由(为什么是1.0%)’和‘区间理由(为什么是±0.2pp)’之间的‘断层’——前者有解释，后者没有。

Row ③ ‘Diagnosis + treatment-seeking *’: 17%/20%/23%, ‘ANALYST ASSUMPTION — sensitivity-tested’. Row ④ ‘Commercially reachable/label-eligible proxy *’: 42%/45%/48%, ‘ANALYST ASSUMPTION — NMPA label criteria’. Row ⑤ ‘GLP-1 penetration rate 2025*’: 0.8%/1.0%/1.2%, ‘ANALYST ASSUMPTION — nascent, self-pay market’.

The ‘symmetric range width’ across all three rows — ±3pp/±3pp/±0.2pp — what this symmetry itself implies: Row ③ (20%±3pp), row ④ (45%±3pp), row ⑤ (1.0%±0.2pp, i.e., ±20% relative) — all three are SYMMETRIC ranges around the Base Case. Symmetric ranges are standard market-model sensitivity practice — essentially ‘if I’m not 100% sure of the true value, Base±X represents my belief that the true value likely falls in this range.’ But SYMMETRY ITSELF is a MODELING CHOICE, not a data-derived fact. E.g., if diagnosis rates in China are SYSTEMATICALLY UNDERESTIMATED (Slide 9’s ‘consistent with chronic disease underdiagnosis’), then the ‘20% diagnosis” Base Case might ALREADY skew CONSERVATIVE — the probability the TRUE value exceeds 20% might be GREATER than the probability it’s below 20%. If so, an ASYMMETRIC range (e.g., 17%–28%, not 17%–23%) might better reflect the ‘underdiagnosis’ judgment’s directionality. This page chose a mathematically-simple ±3pp symmetric range that doesn’t encode that directional judgment.

Row ⑤’s ‘nascent, self-pay market’ rationale — why it justifies the BASE VALUE but not the RANGE WIDTH: Row ⑤’s ‘Source/Status’ column says ‘ANALYST ASSUMPTION — nascent, self-pay market’ — this explains WHY the Base Case (1.0%) is LOWER than the US’s 2% (the ‘anchored to half the US’ logic from Slide 9), but the RANGE (0.8%–1.2%, ±0.2pp) ITSELF isn’t further justified by ‘nascent self-pay market.’ E.g., shouldn’t a NASCENT market’s penetration carry a WIDER uncertainty range than a MATURE market’s (less data, more volatility)? If so, the ±20% relative width might UNDERSTATE the EXTRA uncertainty inherent to being a nascent market. This is a gap between ‘the rationale for the BASE VALUE (why 1.0%)’ and ‘the rationale for the RANGE WIDTH (why ±0.2pp)’ — the former is explained, the latter isn’t.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK“③④⑤三行在三档情景里是‘同步移动’的(Conservative都取低值/Optimistic都取高值)——但现实中，‘诊断率提高’和‘适应症符合率提高’和‘渗透率提高’，是不是真的会‘同时发生’？有没有可能‘诊断率提高了，但渗透率反而因为‘诊断出更多轻症患者(不在适应症范围内)’而下降’？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER这是一个很深刻的问题，指出了‘三档情景’设计里一个隐含的假设：‘③④⑤三个变量在‘好/坏’方向上是‘一致的(co-move)’’。我认为这个假设有其合理性，但确实不是‘唯一可能的世界’。合理性在于：可以构造一个‘统一的宏观叙事’来解释为什么三者co-move——比如‘Optimistic情景=医保政策放宽+医生教育增加+药品降价(Slide6/8讨论的解决方向都兑现)’，这个单一的‘政策环境改善’宏观因素，会同时推高‘诊断率(医生教育→更多诊断)’、‘适应症符合率(医保放宽可能扩大‘愿意诊断为肥胖’的BMI范围)’和‘渗透率(降价→更多人负担得起)’——在这个叙事下，三者co-move是合理的。但您提到的‘反向关系’场景(诊断率提高但渗透率因‘诊断出更多不符合条件的轻症患者’而被‘稀释’)，确实是‘三者不一定co-move’的一个反例——如果发生这种情况，‘诊断率提高、但适应症符合率(行④)同时下降’，而这一页的三档情景设计里，行③和行④是‘同向移动’的(都在Optimistic里取高值)，没有覆盖‘行③上升、行④下降’这种‘交叉情景(cross scenario)’。如果要更严谨，可以做‘情景矩阵(scenario matrix)’而不是‘单一情景轴(single scenario axis)’——比如‘诊断率×适应症符合率’做2x2矩阵，而不是假设两者总是同向。但这会让模型从‘3个情景’变成‘更多情景组合’，复杂度大幅上升——‘单一情景轴+一个统一的宏观叙事’是‘简洁性 vs 完整性’权衡下的选择，我认为是‘可以接受但应该承认局限’的简化。

EN： That's a very insightful question — it identifies an implicit assumption in the three-scenario design: that rows ③④⑤ move TOGETHER in the same good/bad direction (co-move). I think that assumption has some justification, though it isn't the only possible world. The justification: you can construct a single macro narrative explaining why all three co-move — e.g., 'Optimistic = looser reimbursement policy + more physician education + lower drug prices (the solution arrows from Slides 6/8 all materialize),' and this one macro factor — an improving policy environment — would simultaneously push UP the diagnosis rate (more physician education → more diagnoses), the label-eligibility rate (looser reimbursement may widen the BMI range doctors are willing to diagnose as obesity), AND the penetration rate (lower prices → more people can afford it). Under that narrative, co-movement is reasonable. But the inverse scenario you raise — diagnosis rate rises, yet penetration gets DILUTED because the newly-diagnosed patients are milder cases who don't meet the label criteria — is a real counter-example where the three DON'T necessarily co-move. If that happened, the diagnosis rate would rise while the label-eligibility rate (row ④) fell — and this page's three-scenario design has rows ③ and ④ moving in the SAME direction (both at their high end in Optimistic), with no 'cross scenario' covering 'row ③ up, row ④ down.' To be more rigorous, you could build a scenario MATRIX rather than a single scenario axis — e.g., a 2x2 of 'diagnosis rate × label-eligibility rate' instead of assuming they always move together. But that turns '3 scenarios' into many more combinations, sharply increasing complexity — 'a single scenario axis plus one unifying macro narrative' is a simplicity-vs-completeness tradeoff that I think is acceptable, as long as the limitation is acknowledged.

5. 表格行⑥⑦：计算结果与价格代理 Rows ⑥⑦ — Calculated Patients & the Price Proxy

行⑥“Treated patients (calculated)”：~115,000 / ~180,600 / ~266,000，来源‘Calculated from above inputs’。行⑦“Annual cost proxy (starter CNY 16,800/year)”：三档情景均为‘USD 2,300’，来源‘Yicai/Reuters/Fortune 2024 starter-dose pricing proxy’。

行⑥算式核对：200.7M×17%×42%×0.8%≈11.5万；200.7M×20%×45%×1.0%≈18.06万(标注180,600，与Slide9的181k有约400人的微小取整差异)；200.7M×23%×48%×1.2%≈26.6万 — 三档算式均自洽。180,600 vs Slide 9的‘~181k’：精确值应为200.7M×20%×45%×1%=180,630——‘181k’是‘向上四舍五入到千位’的结果，‘180,600’是‘保留到百位’的结果，两者都是‘180,630’的合理舍入，不存在矛盾——但‘两个不同页面用了不同精度的舍入’，是‘形式上不完全一致’的细节，如果被追问‘到底是181,000还是180,600’，应该说‘精确计算值是180,630，Slide9四舍五入到千位写作181k，这一页保留到百位写作180,600，两者是同一个数字的不同精度呈现’。

行⑦“三档情景里唯一‘价格不变’的一行” — 与Slide 6/8讨论的“价格竞争/biosimilar降价”是否矛盾：我们在Slide 6(障碍①‘market price competition ongoing as of 2026’)和Slide 8(COMPETITIVE IMPLICATION‘domestic biosimilars...may force MNCs to reprice…reducing per-patient revenue’)里，反复讨论了‘价格未来会下降’这个趋势；但这一页的‘Annual cost proxy’在Conservative/Base/Optimistic三档里都是‘USD2,300(不变)’——也就是说，‘Optimistic情景(更高的诊断率/适应症符合率/渗透率)’，并没有同时假设‘价格因为渗透率提高、竞争加剧而下降’。这意味着：‘这一页的‘Optimistic’，是‘更多人在‘当前价格水平’下使用GLP-1’，而不是‘更多人在‘因竞争降价后的更低价格’下使用GLP-1’’——如果Slide6/8描述的‘价格竞争’在2025-2026年间已经发生，那么‘Optimistic情景下的612M’可能‘低估了患者数量、但同时高估了单价’(净效应方向不确定)；反之，如果价格竞争主要发生在‘2026年之后(post-2026, 参考Slide8‘PRICE’徽章的‘post-2026’标注)，那么‘行⑦在‘2025年’这个时间点保持价格不变，是‘合理的(因为价格竞争还没开始)’。这是一个‘模型的时间范围(2025)’和‘趋势讨论的时间范围(2026+)’之间的‘边界一致性’问题，值得主动说明。

“Yicai/Reuters/Fortune 2024” — 三个媒体来源并列，“Fortune”是新出现的来源：‘Yicai(第一财经)’和‘Reuters(路透社)’在Slide 6/7已经出现过；‘Fortune(财富杂志)’是第一次出现——Fortune是一家美国老牌商业杂志，常报道‘新药定价/上市’这类商业新闻(英文读者熟悉度高)。三个来源并列，可能是‘针对‘诺和盈starter dose CNY16,800/年’这同一个事实，分析师分别核对了中文财经媒体(Yicai)、国际通讯社(Reuters)和美国商业杂志(Fortune)三个独立来源，确认数字一致’——这是‘多来源交叉验证(triangulation)’的一个例子，比Slide5-9里‘一个数字一个来源’的模式更‘稳健’，但三个来源具体哪个是‘首发’、哪两个是‘转载/引用’，这一页没有进一步区分。

Row ⑥ ‘Treated patients (calculated)’: ~115,000/~180,600/~266,000, ‘Calculated from above inputs’. Row ⑦ ‘Annual cost proxy (starter CNY 16,800/year)’: USD2,300 across all 3 scenarios, ‘Yicai/Reuters/Fortune 2024 starter-dose pricing proxy’.

Row ⑥ arithmetic check: 200.7M×17%×42%×0.8%≈115k; ×20%×45%×1.0%≈180,630 (Slide9’s ‘~181k’ vs. here ‘180,600’ — a ~400-unit rounding difference; both are reasonable roundings of 180,630, no contradiction — just different rounding precision across pages); ×23%×48%×1.2%≈266k — all three scenarios internally consistent.If asked ‘is it 181,000 or 180,600,’ the answer: the precise value is 180,630; Slide9 rounds to the nearest thousand (181k), this page keeps the hundreds digit (180,600) — same number, different display precision.

Row ⑦ — the ONLY row where PRICE is held constant across all 3 scenarios — does this conflict with Slide 6/8’s ‘price competition/biosimilar erosion’ discussion: Slides 6 (Barrier ①, ‘market price competition ongoing as of 2026’) and 8 (‘domestic biosimilars...may force MNCs to reprice...reducing per-patient revenue’) repeatedly discussed FUTURE PRICE DECLINES; yet this page’s ‘Annual cost proxy’ is USD2,300 in ALL THREE scenarios. So ‘Optimistic’ here means ‘MORE people using GLP-1 at TODAY’S price,’ not ‘more people at a LOWER, competition-driven price.’ If the price competition Slides 6/8 describe materializes WITHIN 2025–2026, then ‘Optimistic $612M’ might UNDERSTATE patient count but OVERSTATE per-patient price (net effect uncertain); conversely, if price competition is mainly POST-2026 (per Slide 8’s ‘PRICE’ badge, ‘post-2026’), then holding price fixed FOR 2025 is reasonable (competition hasn’t kicked in yet). This is a ‘model time-scope (2025) vs. trend-discussion time-scope (2026+)’ boundary-consistency point worth proactively clarifying.

‘Yicai/Reuters/Fortune 2024’ — three media sources together; ‘Fortune’ is new: ‘Yicai’ and ‘Reuters’ appeared on Slides 6/7; ‘Fortune’ (the US business magazine, well-known to English readers, frequently covers drug-pricing/launch news) appears for the first time here. Three sources together likely means: ‘for the same fact (Wegovy’s starter dose ~CNY16,800/year), the analyst cross-checked a Chinese financial outlet (Yicai), an international wire service (Reuters), and a US business magazine (Fortune), and all three agree’ — a TRIANGULATION example, more robust than the ‘one number, one source’ pattern on Slides 5–9, though this page doesn’t specify which was the ORIGINAL report and which two are re-reports.

6. 三档情景的文字描述 The Three Scenario Descriptions

Conservative: “USD 264M / Low diagnosis & penetration”。Base Case: “USD 416M / Moderate access; self-pay dominant”。Optimistic: “USD 612M / Wider eligibility & higher uptake”。

每个情景的文字描述，只点名了“③④⑤三个变量中的2个” — 这种“选择性点名”是否暴露了“叙事”和“数字”之间的缝隙：Conservative点名‘diagnosis & penetration’(行③⑤)，没提行④(eligibility)；Optimistic点名‘eligibility & higher uptake(uptake可理解为penetration)’(行④⑤)，没提行③(diagnosis)。但实际上，三档情景里行③④⑤是‘全部同步移动’的(都从低到高)——也就是说，‘Conservative’的数字(264M)实际上也包含了‘行④从45%降到42%’的影响，但文字描述没有提到‘eligibility’；‘Optimistic’的数字(612M)也包含了‘行③从20%升到23%’的影响，但文字描述没有提到‘diagnosis’。这种‘文字叙事只挑2个变量、但计算用了3个变量’的现象，本质上是‘简化叙事(每个情景用一个简短的‘故事’来命名，而不是逐一罗列所有变量的变化)’——可以理解，但严格来说，‘文字描述’和‘数字计算’之间存在‘描述不完整(但计算完整)’的小缝隙。

“self-pay dominant(自费为主)”只出现在Base Case的描述里 — 为什么：‘self-pay dominant’这个描述，本质上是‘对2025年中国市场现状的事实陈述’(无论哪个情景，2025年的GLP-1肥胖适应症都是‘自费为主’，因为Slide6已经确认‘无肥胖适应症NRDL报销’)——这句话与其说是‘Base Case特有的特征’，更像是‘对所有三个情景都适用的‘背景设定’，只是恰好写在了Base Case这一行里’。如果Conservative/Optimistic的描述里也加上‘self-pay dominant’，会显得‘三个情景共享同一个‘市场结构’前提，差异只在‘行为参数的取值’’——这其实是更准确的表述，但可能因为‘避免重复’，‘self-pay dominant’只写了一次(在Base Case)。

Conservative: ‘USD 264M / Low diagnosis & penetration’. Base Case: ‘USD 416M / Moderate access; self-pay dominant’. Optimistic: ‘USD 612M / Wider eligibility & higher uptake’.

Each scenario’s description names only 2 of the 3 ③④⑤ variables — does this ‘selective naming’ expose a gap between narrative and numbers: Conservative names ‘diagnosis & penetration’ (③⑤), omitting ④ (eligibility); Optimistic names ‘eligibility & higher uptake’ (penetration, ④⑤), omitting ③ (diagnosis). But in fact ALL THREE of ③④⑤ move together (all low→high across scenarios) — i.e., ‘Conservative’’s $264M also reflects ‘④ dropping from 45% to 42%,’ yet the description doesn’t mention eligibility; ‘Optimistic’’s $612M also reflects ‘③ rising from 20% to 23%,’ yet the description doesn’t mention diagnosis. This ‘narrative names 2 variables but the calculation uses 3’ is essentially SIMPLIFIED STORYTELLING (each scenario gets a short ‘story’ rather than enumerating every variable change) — understandable, but strictly speaking there’s a small ‘description incomplete (calculation complete)’ gap.

‘Self-pay dominant’ appears only in the Base Case description — why: ‘Self-pay dominant’ is essentially a FACTUAL STATEMENT about 2025 China’s market structure (true under ANY scenario, since Slide 6 already established ‘no obesity-specific NRDL reimbursement’ regardless of scenario) — more a SHARED BACKGROUND CONDITION across all 3 scenarios than a Base-Case-SPECIFIC feature; it just happens to be written on the Base Case row. Repeating ‘self-pay dominant’ in the Conservative/Optimistic descriptions too would more accurately convey ‘all 3 scenarios share the same market-structure premise, differing only in behavioral-parameter values’ — but to avoid repetition, it’s likely stated only once (on Base Case).

7. BENCHMARK CHECK — 三个第三方来源逐一拆解 Three Third-Party Sources, One by One

原文：“GVR receptor-agonist: China GLP-1 all-use → USD 4,557.2M by 2033, CAGR 13.9% (2026–2033). GVR weight-loss: USD 161.7M (2024) / USD 558.5M (2030). F&S / Hengrui IPO Report (May 2025): China GLP-1 all-indication RMB 9.4B (2023) → RMB 70.9B (2028E). L.E.K. (May 2025): ~RMB 100B by 2030. Broad GLP-1 all-indication benchmarks are shown separately from weight-loss-specific benchmarks; model output is analyst obesity-use scenario.”

GVR的“两页报告” — 同一个出版商(GVR/Grand View Research)，“All-Use”页和“Weight-Loss”页的数字差了近10倍：‘GVR receptor-agonist (all-use) → USD4,557.2M by 2033’ vs ‘GVR weight-loss → USD558.5M by 2030’——即使粗略地把‘4,557.2M(2033)’按‘13.9% CAGR’往回折算到2030年(约÷(1.139)^3≈1.477，得3,087M)，仍然是‘weight-loss页2030年558.5M’的约5.5倍。这是‘同一家研究机构、同一份大类研究(GLP-1受体激动剂)、仅因为‘统计口径(all-use 包含糖尿病等全部适应症 vs weight-loss仅减重)’不同，市场规模数字相差5倍以上’的‘活生生的例子’——这比Slide 3‘抽象地提醒‘L.E.K./GVR数字是all-indication’’更有说服力，因为这一页‘把同一个出版商的两份报告并排放在一起’，让‘范围(scope)对数字的影响’变得‘肉眼可见’。

GVR weight-loss页的“USD161.7M(2024)” — 比我们模型的“Conservative 264M(2025)”还要低，这意味着什么：如果GVR的‘weight-loss专属’页面认为‘2024年中国GLP-1减肥药市场约161.7M美元’，而我们的模型认为‘2025年(仅一年后)Conservative情景就有264M’——264/161.7≈1.63，即‘我们模型最保守的情景，也比GVR‘weight-loss专属’数字的前一年高出约63%’。进一步看，GVR weight-loss页‘2030年558.5M’，落在‘我们模型2025年的Base(416M)和Optimistic(612M)之间’——也就是说，‘我们的模型认为2025年(更早)就能达到的市场规模，接近GVR认为要到2030年(更晚)才能达到的水平’。这意味着：‘我们的bottom-up模型，比GVR的weight-loss专属预测，隐含了‘更快的市场增长速度假设’’——这是一个‘模型 vs 同口径第三方基准’的‘实质性差异(不是范围不匹配，是‘同口径但增速假设不同’)’，值得主动说明。

F&S/Hengrui IPO Report — “Hengrui IPO”这个标注本身揭示的“来源动机”问题：‘F&S(Frost & Sullivan)/Hengrui IPO Report(恒瑞IPO报告)’——恒瑞医药正是Slide8里‘HRS9531’的研发方(Memory里‘Key companies tracked’之一)。‘Hengrui IPO Report’这个标注意味着‘这份市场规模数字，来自恒瑞IPO招股书里、由F&S提供的行业市场研究章节’——港股/A股IPO招股书里的‘行业概览(Industry Overview)’章节，按惯例由第三方咨询机构(F&S是港股IPO里最常见的此类供应商之一)撰写，其市场规模预测‘有时被认为存在‘偏乐观’的倾向’(因为‘行业空间越大’，对发行人估值的支撑叙事越有利)。RMB9.4B(2023)→RMB70.9B(2028E)，5年CAGR≈(70.9/9.4)^(1/5)-1≈50%——这个≈50%的CAGR，比GVR的13.9%高出约3.6倍。

L.E.K.的“~RMB100B by 2030” — 与GVR“USD4,557.2M by 2033”的对比，以及“L.E.K. May2025” vs 这一页脚注“L.E.K. Mar2026”的日期差异：L.E.K.‘~RMB100B by 2030’，按约7.2-7.3的汇率≈USD13.7-13.9B；GVR‘USD4,557.2M(≈4.56B) by 2033’——L.E.K.对‘2030年’的预测(≈13.8B)，已经是GVR对‘2033年(更晚3年)’预测(4.56B)的约3倍。两个‘all-indication’第三方来源，对‘更早年份’给出的数字反而是‘更晚年份的另一个来源’的3倍——这进一步印证了KEY INSIGHT想说的‘第三方基准之间彼此的差异，比它们和我们模型的差异更大’。另外，Slide8的斜体提示句引用‘L.E.K. (May 2025)’(60-70个管线资产)，而这一页脚注写的是‘L.E.K. Mar 2026’(~RMB100B市场规模)——这可能是‘L.E.K.在不同时间发布的两份不同报告(一份关于管线资产数量，另一份关于市场规模预测)’，也可能是‘同一份报告的不同章节，但报告的‘发布/更新日期’在两页被引用为不同日期’——如果被问及，应如实说明‘这是同一研究机构(L.E.K.)在相近时间(2025年5月/2026年3月)发布的两份不同主题(管线资产统计/市场规模预测)的报告，分别在Slide8和Slide10被引用’，而不是简单地说‘两个日期一样’(掩盖差异)。

GVR’s ‘two reports’ — same publisher (Grand View Research), ‘All-Use’ vs. ‘Weight-Loss’ pages differ by ~10x: ‘GVR receptor-agonist (all-use) → USD4,557.2M by 2033’ vs. ‘GVR weight-loss → USD558.5M by 2030’ — even rough-discounting 2033’s $4,557.2M back to 2030 at 13.9% CAGR (÷(1.139)^3≈1.477 → ~$3,087M), it’s STILL ~5.5x the weight-loss page’s $558.5M for 2030. This is a LIVE EXAMPLE — same research house, same broad topic (GLP-1 receptor agonists), differing 5x+ purely due to SCOPE (all-use including diabetes vs. weight-loss-only) — far more persuasive than Slide 3’s abstract reminder that ‘L.E.K./GVR figures are all-indication,’ because this page puts TWO REPORTS FROM THE SAME PUBLISHER side-by-side, making the scope effect VISIBLE.

GVR weight-loss’s ‘USD161.7M (2024)’ — LOWER than our model’s ‘Conservative $264M (2025)’ — what this means: If GVR’s weight-loss-SPECIFIC page puts China’s 2024 GLP-1-for-obesity market at ~$161.7M, and our model’s 2025 (just ONE year later) Conservative case is $264M — 264/161.7≈1.63, i.e., our model’s MOST CONSERVATIVE scenario is ~63% ABOVE GVR’s weight-loss figure for the PRIOR year. Further, GVR weight-loss’s 2030 figure ($558.5M) sits BETWEEN our 2025 Base ($416M) and Optimistic ($612M) — i.e., OUR MODEL’S 2025 figures already approach what GVR thinks won’t be reached until 2030. This means our bottom-up model implies a FASTER growth-rate assumption than GVR’s weight-loss-specific forecast — a SUBSTANTIVE difference vs. a SAME-SCOPE third-party benchmark (not a scope mismatch, but a GROWTH-RATE assumption mismatch), worth proactively explaining.

F&S/Hengrui IPO Report — what the ‘Hengrui IPO’ tag itself reveals about source MOTIVATION: ‘F&S (Frost & Sullivan)/Hengrui IPO Report’ — Hengrui is the same company behind Slide 8’s ‘HRS9531’ (one of our tracked companies). ‘Hengrui IPO Report’ means this market-size figure comes from the ‘Industry Overview’ chapter of Hengrui’s IPO PROSPECTUS, conventionally drafted by a third-party consultancy (F&S being a common such provider for HK IPOs) — such market forecasts are sometimes seen as skewing OPTIMISTIC (a larger ‘industry TAM’ supports a more favorable valuation narrative for the issuer). RMB9.4B(2023)→RMB70.9B(2028E), 5-yr CAGR≈(70.9/9.4)^(1/5)-1≈50% — about 3.6x GVR’s 13.9%.

L.E.K.’s ‘~RMB100B by 2030’ vs. GVR’s ‘USD4,557.2M by 2033’, and the ‘L.E.K. May2025’ (Slide8) vs. ‘L.E.K. Mar2026’ (this page’s footnote) date difference: L.E.K.’s ‘~RMB100B by 2030’ ≈ USD13.7–13.9B at ~7.2–7.3 FX; GVR’s ‘USD4,557.2M (≈4.56B) by 2033’ — L.E.K.’s 2030 forecast (~$13.8B) is ALREADY ~3x GVR’s 2033 (later!) forecast ($4.56B). Two ‘all-indication’ third-party sources disagree by 3x for an EARLIER year vs. a LATER year from the other source — further confirming the KEY INSIGHT’s point that third-party benchmarks disagree MORE WITH EACH OTHER than with our model. Also, Slide 8’s italic note cites ‘L.E.K. (May 2025)’ (60–70 pipeline assets) while this page’s footnote cites ‘L.E.K. Mar 2026’ (~RMB100B market size) — this could be TWO DIFFERENT L.E.K. reports (one on pipeline asset counts, one on market-size forecasts) published close in time, or the SAME underlying research cited with different version/update dates on the two slides. If asked, the honest answer is ‘these are two different-topic reports (pipeline census vs. market-size forecast) from the same research house, published around May2025/Mar2026, cited on Slides 8 and 10 respectively’ — not glossing over the date difference.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK“你的模型(416M)和GVR‘weight-loss专属’的2030年预测(558.5M)很接近——既然GVR也有一个‘口径相同(减重专属)’的数字，为什么不直接用GVR的数字、或者拿GVR的数字做更细致的对照，而只是简单地说‘third-party benchmarks是all-indication，cross-check only’？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER这是一个非常好的问题，提醒我KEY INSIGHT和脚注的措辞(‘Broad GLP-1 all-indication benchmarks are shown separately from weight-loss-specific benchmarks’)，确实更多是在强调‘GVR receptor-agonist(all-use)/F&S/L.E.K.三者是all-indication’，对‘GVR weight-loss这个同口径数字’的讨论相对简略——而您提到的‘416M vs 558.5M(2030)’这个对比，恰恰是‘同口径(都是weight-loss-specific)’下最有意义的交叉核对，比‘416M vs 4,557.2M(all-use, 2033)’这种‘范围不同’的对比更有价值。我认为正确的态度是：①承认‘GVR weight-loss(161.7M/2024, 558.5M/2030)’是这一页‘四个第三方数字里，唯一一个和我们模型‘口径可比’的’；②主动呈现‘416M(2025) vs 161.7M(2024)/558.5M(2030)’这个对比——我们模型的2025年数字，介于GVR的2024和2030数字之间，但更接近2030——这意味着‘我们的模型隐含的增长速度，比GVR weight-loss页隐含的增长速度更快’；③解释‘为什么我们的模型增速更快’——一个可能的理由是，GVR的weight-loss预测可能是在‘更早的时间点(比如2024年初)’做的，当时‘中国只有1-2款GLP-1肥胖产品获批’，GVR的增速假设可能没有充分反映‘Slide1时间线里2024-2026年密集获批6款产品’这个‘供给侧加速’的最新事实；而我们的模型(基于2026年6月的最新信息)，自然会反映‘供给侧已经加速’这一更新的现实。所以‘416M比GVR weight-loss页2025年的隐含值更高’，可能不是‘我们的模型过于乐观’，而是‘GVR的weight-loss预测数据相对较旧、未充分捕捉2024-2026年的供给侧加速’——但这只是‘一个合理的假设’，没有去查证GVR weight-loss报告的具体发布日期和方法论细节，如果要严谨回答，应该去核实。

EN： That's an excellent question, and it reminds me that the KEY INSIGHT and footnote wording ('broad GLP-1 all-indication benchmarks are shown separately from weight-loss-specific benchmarks') really emphasizes that GVR's receptor-agonist (all-use), F&S, and L.E.K. are all all-indication, while discussion of GVR's weight-loss-SPECIFIC figure is comparatively thin — and yet the '416M vs 558.5M (2030)' comparison you're pointing to is exactly the most meaningful SAME-SCOPE cross-check, more valuable than the scope-mismatched '416M vs 4,557.2M (all-use, 2033)' comparison. I think the right approach is: ① acknowledge that GVR weight-loss (161.7M/2024, 558.5M/2030) is the ONLY one of the four third-party figures on this page that's genuinely SCOPE-COMPARABLE to our model; ② proactively present the comparison '416M (2025) vs 161.7M (2024) / 558.5M (2030)' — our model's 2025 figure sits between GVR's 2024 and 2030 figures, but closer to 2030, meaning our model implies a FASTER growth rate than GVR's weight-loss page implies; ③ explain WHY our growth rate is faster — one plausible reason is that GVR's weight-loss forecast may have been produced at an EARLIER point in time (e.g., early 2024), when China had only 1–2 GLP-1 obesity products approved, so GVR's growth assumptions may not fully reflect the SUPPLY-SIDE ACCELERATION captured in Slide 1's timeline (6 products approved in quick succession during 2024–2026); our model, built on information current as of June 2026, naturally reflects that more recent supply-side acceleration. So '416M being higher than GVR weight-loss's implied 2025 value' may not mean 'our model is too optimistic' — it may mean 'GVR's weight-loss forecast is relatively dated and hasn't fully captured the 2024–2026 supply-side acceleration.' But that's only a plausible hypothesis — I haven't verified GVR's weight-loss report's exact publication date and methodology, and a rigorous answer would require checking that.

8. KEY INSIGHT与底部脚注 KEY INSIGHT & Footnote

KEY INSIGHT原文：“BENCHMARK CHECK: GVR receptor-agonist (→USD 4,557.2M by 2033, CAGR 13.9%), F&S/Hengrui IPO Report (RMB 9.4B→70.9B 2023–2028E), and L.E.K. (~RMB 100B by 2030) are all broad all-indication GLP-1 benchmarks. GVR weight-loss-only page: USD 161.7M (2024)/558.5M (2030). USD 416M base case is an analyst obesity-only scenario output, not a third-party market-size datapoint.”

最后一句“not a third-party market-size datapoint” — 这是整份报告“自我定位”的最终声明：从Slide 3第一次提出‘区分分析师模型和第三方数据’，到Slide 6/8反复强调‘China-specific数据缺口’，到Slide 9‘PRIMARY vs ASSUMPTION’，再到这一页‘Tier1 vs *’——这条线索在这句话里‘收尾’：‘416M是‘分析师情景模型的输出’，不是‘第三方市场规模数据点’’。这句话同时是‘诚实的免责声明’和‘价值主张’——‘免责’在于‘不能把416M等同于‘行业共识’或‘权威数字’’；‘价值主张’在于‘正因为是‘自下而上’构建的，每一个假设都可以被拆解、质疑、调整(这正是这份报告整体的设计目的——可防御性)’，而‘第三方数字(如GVR/F&S/L.E.K.)’往往是‘黑箱’，无法拆解。

脚注公式“Obese proxy (NBS 2025 1% survey × Zhang 2024) × diag% × elig% × penetration% × annual cost” — 与正文的MODEL FORMULA相比，多了什么：脚注里的公式把‘Obese proxy’进一步拆解为‘(NBS 2025 1% survey × Zhang 2024)’——即‘人口基数×肥胖率’两个来源的乘积，比正文MODEL FORMULA(直接写‘Obese Proxy’一项)更细。这是‘脚注作为‘给追问者看的详细版’，正文作为‘给一般读者看的简化版’’的典型设计——正文公式5项，脚注公式实质上是6项(因为‘Obese proxy’被拆成了2项)，这和Slide9的6步漏斗‘完全对应’——脚注公式其实是‘把Slide9的6步骤和这一页的5项公式做了一次‘翻译对照’’。

The closing sentence ‘not a third-party market-size datapoint’ — the deck’s final self-positioning statement: From Slide 3’s first ‘distinguish analyst model from third-party data,’ through Slides 6/8’s repeated ‘China-specific data gap,’ to Slide 9’s ‘PRIMARY vs. ASSUMPTION,’ to this page’s ‘Tier1 vs. *’ — this thread CONCLUDES here: ‘$416M is the output of an ANALYST SCENARIO MODEL, not a THIRD-PARTY MARKET-SIZE DATAPOINT.’ This sentence is BOTH an honest disclaimer (‘don’t equate $416M with ‘industry consensus’ or an ‘authoritative figure’’) AND a value proposition (‘precisely BECAUSE it’s built bottom-up, every assumption can be unpacked, challenged, adjusted — the report’s whole design goal of DEFENSIBILITY — whereas third-party figures (GVR/F&S/L.E.K.) are typically BLACK BOXES that can’t be unpacked.’)

Footnote formula ‘Obese proxy (NBS 2025 1% survey × Zhang 2024) × diag% × elig% × penetration% × annual cost’ — what’s added vs. the body’s MODEL FORMULA: The footnote further decomposes ‘Obese proxy’ into ‘(NBS 2025 1% survey × Zhang 2024)’ — i.e., ‘population base × obesity rate’ — more granular than the body’s single ‘Obese Proxy’ term. A classic ‘footnote = detailed version for those who dig deeper; body = simplified version for general readers’ design — the body has 5 terms, the footnote effectively has 6 (since ‘Obese proxy’ splits into 2), EXACTLY matching Slide 9’s 6-step funnel — the footnote formula is essentially a TRANSLATION TABLE between Slide 9’s 6 steps and this page’s 5-term formula.

找到了GVR这份报告的原文（grandviewresearch.com，发布于2025年4月30日）。这给了几个可以用来"反驳/质疑"的切入点：

漏洞1：GVR的161.7M(2024)是"全球市场份额分摊法(top-down)"，不是"流行病学自下而上法(bottom-up)"

原文写道："China accounted for 1.2% of the global GLP-1 agonists weight loss drugs market in 2024"——而全球市场规模GVR给的是"USD 13.84 billion in 2024"。13.84B × 1.2% ≈ 166M ≈ 161.7M，对得上。

也就是说，161.7M这个数字的算法是"全球总盘子 × 中国份额%"，和我们Slide9-10"从14亿人口一步步漏斗到181k患者"的bottom-up方法完全是两种不同的方法论——你完全可以说：

"GVR的161.7M是top-down分摊法的产物，其准确性取决于(a)全球总盘子13.84B的准确性，以及(b)'中国占全球1.2%'这个份额假设的准确性；我们的416M是bottom-up流行病学模型，两者方法论不同，差异本身不能简单解释为'谁对谁错'，而是'两种独立方法论的交叉验证存在差距'。"

漏洞2：GVR这份报告发布于2025年4月——数据vintage早于Slide7的6款产品中至少2款的获批

报告发布时间是2025年4月30日。而Slide7的6款产品里：

信尔美(Mazdutide) 2025年6月27日获批

Ecnoglutide 2026年3月6日获批

这两款都是在GVR这份报告发布之后才获批的——GVR的"2025-2030 CAGR 19%"这个增速假设，在制定时根本不知道这两款产品的存在，更不可能纳入它们对市场的增量贡献。这是一个可验证、可引用日期的"数据vintage滞后"证据，比我们之前泛泛说"GVR可能滞后"更有力。

漏洞3：原文还提到"Semaglutide (Wegovy) was the largest revenue generating drug in 2024"——161.7M可能主要反映的是"诺和盈一款产品、且只有半年(2024年6月获批)的收入"

诺和盈2024年6月才在中国获批，如果它是2024年China市场的"最大收入来源"，意味着161.7M这个数字里，诺和盈只贡献了半年的销售。2025年随着诺和盈满年运营+穆峰达(2024.7获批)满年运营+信尔美新增，市场规模理论上应该有一次"非线性跳升"，而GVR给的"19% CAGR"是一个线性平滑增速，可能没有充分体现"2024→2025"这个"从半年销售到全年销售+新增2款产品"的跳升效应。

漏洞4：全球总盘子本身的数字在GVR不同报告间就不一致

搜索结果里另一份GVR报告("Anti-obesity Medication Market")给出的是"global anti-obesity medication market USD6.62B(2023)→USD77.24B(2030), CAGR31.66%"——这和"GLP-1 agonists weight loss drugs market USD13.84B(2024)→USD48.84B(2030), CAGR18.54%"是两个不同的全球数字(口径不同：anti-obesity全品类 vs GLP-1专属)，但都来自GVR。如果"中国占全球1.2%"这个份额套用到"6.62B(2023)"而不是"13.84B(2024)"，161.7M这个数字本身就会变——说明161.7M对"用哪个全球基准做分母"高度敏感。

建议写法（放进BENCHMARK CHECK或备注里）：

"GVR's China weight-loss figure (161.7M, 2024) is derived top-down (China = 1.2% of a USD13.84B global GLP-1 weight-loss market), published April 2025 — predating the Mazdutide (Jun 2025) and Ecnoglutide (Mar 2026) approvals. Its 19% CAGR (2025-2030) was set before these two additional domestic launches, and may understate near-term acceleration. Our 416M is bottom-up (epidemiology-driven); the two methodologies' divergence reflects different approaches, not a direct error in either."

⭐ 这一页最该背的一句话 / The Sentence to Memorize

“2025年中国GLP-1肥胖药市场的Base情景规模约USD416M，来自一个5项相乘的自下而上模型：(11.7亿16+人口proxy)×(17.1%肥胖BMI≥28proxy=200.7M)×(20%诊断+就医)×(45%适应症符合，NMPA标准)×(1.0%渗透率，锚定美国FAIR Health约2%的一半)=~180,600人，再×USD2,300年治疗费(Yicai/Reuters/Fortune交叉验证)=~416M。三档情景(Conservative264M/Base416M/Optimistic612M)的差异，100%来自诊断率(17/20/23%)、适应症符合率(42/45/48%)和渗透率(0.8/1.0/1.2%)三个带*的假设变量，人口和患病率(行①②)在三档中保持不变；价格(USD2,300)在三档中也保持不变，这是‘2025模型’与‘2026+价格竞争趋势’之间的时间边界，需要主动说明。BENCHMARK CHECK把GVR(receptor-agonist all-use→4,557.2M by 2033 / weight-loss专属→161.7M(2024)/558.5M(2030))、F&S/Hengrui IPO报告(9.4B→70.9B RMB, 2023-2028E, CAGR~50%)和L.E.K.(~100B RMB by 2030)并列——三个all-indication基准互相之间的分歧(GVR13.9% CAGR vs F&S~50% CAGR；L.E.K.2030年预测已是GVR2033年预测的3倍)，远大于它们与我们416M模型的分歧。416M比GVR weight-loss专属的2025年隐含值更高(更接近GVR的2030预测558.5M)，意味着我们模型隐含的增速假设比GVR weight-loss页更快——这是一个‘同口径但增速假设不同’的实质性差异，值得主动说明可能源于GVR数据相对滞后于2024-2026年的供给侧加速。最终结论：416M是‘分析师情景模型输出’，不是‘第三方市场规模数据点’——这是整份报告‘Tier体系/分析师模型vs第三方数据’这条主线的最终收口。”

“China’s 2025 obesity-GLP-1 Base case (~$416M) comes from a 5-term bottom-up formula: (1.17B age16+ proxy) × (17.1% BMI≥28 obese proxy = 200.7M) × (20% diagnosed+seeking) × (45% label-eligible, NMPA criteria) × (1.0% penetration, anchored to half of FAIR Health’s US ~2%) = ~180,600 patients, × USD2,300 annual cost (Yicai/Reuters/Fortune-verified) = ~$416M. The 3-scenario spread (Conservative $264M/Base $416M/Optimistic $612M) comes 100% from the three *-tagged variables (diagnosis 17/20/23%, eligibility 42/45/48%, penetration 0.8/1.0/1.2%); population & prevalence (rows ①②) and price (row ⑦, $2,300) are held fixed across all 3 — the latter creating a ‘2025 model’ vs. ‘2026+ price-competition trend’ time-boundary worth proactively addressing. The BENCHMARK CHECK juxtaposes GVR (receptor-agonist all-use → $4,557.2M by 2033 / weight-loss-only → $161.7M (2024)/$558.5M (2030)), the F&S/Hengrui IPO Report (RMB9.4B→70.9B, 2023–2028E, ~50% CAGR), and L.E.K. (~RMB100B by 2030) — these three ALL-INDICATION benchmarks disagree with EACH OTHER (GVR’s 13.9% CAGR vs. F&S’s ~50%; L.E.K.’s 2030 figure already 3x GVR’s 2033 figure) far more than any disagrees with our $416M. $416M EXCEEDS GVR’s SAME-SCOPE (weight-loss) implied 2025 value, sitting closer to GVR’s 2030 figure — implying our model assumes FASTER growth than GVR’s weight-loss forecast, possibly because GVR’s data predates the 2024–2026 supply-side acceleration. Final conclusion: $416M is an ANALYST SCENARIO-MODEL OUTPUT, not a THIRD-PARTY MARKET-SIZE DATAPOINT — the closing statement of the deck’s entire ‘Tier system / analyst model vs. third-party data’ thread.”

10. 综合问题：设计这一页要考虑哪些因素？数据来源都在哪？ Design Factors & Where to Find Sources

设计这一页（情景模型+第三方基准对照页）要考虑的因素：

① 结论的完整归因——最终数字(416M)是否在某一页被‘完整定义’(模型类型+情景+年份)，避免读者在不同页面看到‘裸数字’时产生误解；② 公式vs漏斗的呈现选择——乘法公式简洁但暗含独立性假设，是否需要一句话承认‘变量可能相关’；③ 情景设计的对称性与方向性——敏感性区间是否对称、是否应该根据‘已知的系统性偏差方向(如诊断不足)’设计非对称区间；④ 情景叙事与计算的一致性——文字描述(‘Low diagnosis & penetration’)是否完整覆盖了实际变动的所有变量；⑤ 模型的时间范围边界——哪些变量‘随情景变化’、哪些‘在模型的时间范围内被假设为常数’(如价格)，是否与其他页面讨论的‘未来趋势’存在边界衔接问题；⑥ 第三方基准的选择与排列——是否选取了‘口径相同(同样是weight-loss-specific)’的基准做‘实质对照’，而不只是‘口径不同(all-indication)’的基准做‘范围声明’；⑦ 第三方来源本身的‘动机/偏倚’——如IPO招股书附带的市场研究，是否存在‘偏乐观’的结构性原因。

我所知道的、与这一页相关的数据来源类型：

【行业市场研究报告(全口径)】Grand View Research(grandviewresearch.com)——通常按‘产品/技术(如GLP-1 receptor agonist)’和‘应用(如weight management/diabetes)’分别发布报告，同一主题可能有多份不同细分范围的报告，需要仔细核对‘Scope’章节。

【IPO招股书行业概览】港交所披露易(HKEXnews)——搜索‘Hengrui/恒瑞 prospectus’或‘IPO’，下载招股书PDF，‘Industry Overview’章节通常会标注‘Source: [咨询公司名] Report’及该咨询公司的委托声明(commissioned report disclaimer)。

【咨询公司市场预测】Frost & Sullivan(frost.com)、L.E.K. Consulting(lek.com)——官网‘Insights’或新闻稿可能有公开摘要；完整数据通常出现在‘被引用的客户文件(如IPO招股书、企业官网‘市场概览’页)’里，而非F&S/L.E.K.自己直接公开发布。

【价格/汇率交叉验证】Yicai(第一财经，yicai.com)、Reuters(reuters.com)、Fortune(fortune.com)——搜索‘Wegovy China price’/‘诺和盈 中国 价格’查看多方报道；汇率换算可参考xe.com或公司年报披露的汇率假设。

具体去哪找（实操路径）：

① 查GVR的两份报告 → grandviewresearch.com搜索‘GLP-1 receptor agonist market’(all-use)和‘weight loss drugs market China’(weight-loss specific)，对比两份报告的‘Report Scope/Segmentation’章节，确认‘适应症范围’定义。 ② 查Hengrui IPO招股书里的F&S市场数据 → hkexnews.hk搜索‘恒瑞/Hengrui’相关上市文件(如H股上市的A1表格或聆讯后资料)，在‘Industry Overview’章节查找‘GLP-1’相关市场规模数字及F&S的委托声明。 ③ 查L.E.K.的市场规模数据 → 由于L.E.K.通常不直接公开完整报告，可尝试在被其报告引用的公司公告/招股书/投资者陈述中搜索‘L.E.K.’+‘GLP-1’+‘China’，或在行业媒体(医药魔方/MedTrend)搜索‘L.E.K. 中国 GLP-1 市场规模’的二次报道。 ④ 查价格交叉验证 → 分别在yicai.com、reuters.com、fortune.com搜索‘Wegovy China launch price’/‘诺和盈 上市 价格’，对比三方报道的具体数字和发布时间，判断‘首发来源’。 ⑤ 核实CAGR计算 → 用公式CAGR=(终值/初值)^(1/年数)-1，自行核对脚注里给出的起止值与标注CAGR是否一致(如本页GVR的13.9%、F&S隐含的~50%)。

Factors to consider when designing this ‘scenario model + third-party benchmark’ page: ① full attribution of the headline conclusion — is $416M FULLY DEFINED (model type + scenario + year) somewhere, preventing misreading of ‘bare numbers’ elsewhere; ② formula vs. funnel presentation — a multiplicative formula is concise but implies independence; should a line acknowledge potential correlation; ③ symmetry & directionality of scenario design — should sensitivity ranges be symmetric, or should KNOWN systematic biases (e.g., underdiagnosis) inform an asymmetric range; ④ narrative-calculation consistency — do scenario descriptions (‘Low diagnosis & penetration’) cover ALL variables that actually change; ⑤ the model’s time-scope boundary — which variables vary BY scenario vs. are held CONSTANT within the model’s timeframe (e.g., price), and whether this creates a boundary issue with ‘future trends’ discussed elsewhere; ⑥ selection/ordering of third-party benchmarks — are SAME-SCOPE (weight-loss-specific) benchmarks used for SUBSTANTIVE comparison, vs. DIFFERENT-SCOPE (all-indication) benchmarks used merely for SCOPE DISCLOSURE; ⑦ third-party sources’ own ‘motivation/bias’ — e.g., IPO-prospectus market research’s potential structural optimism.

Data source types relevant to this page: [Full-scope industry market research] Grand View Research (grandviewresearch.com) — typically publishes separate reports by PRODUCT/TECHNOLOGY (e.g., GLP-1 receptor agonist) vs. APPLICATION (weight management/diabetes); check each report’s ‘Scope’ section carefully. [IPO prospectus industry overviews] HKEXnews — search ‘Hengrui prospectus/IPO,’ download the filing PDF; the ‘Industry Overview’ chapter typically cites ‘Source: [consultancy] Report’ with a commissioned-report disclaimer. [Consultancy market forecasts] Frost & Sullivan (frost.com), L.E.K. Consulting (lek.com) — some public summaries on ‘Insights’; full data usually appears in CLIENT documents (IPO prospectuses, company ‘market overview’ pages) rather than published directly. [Price/FX cross-verification] Yicai (yicai.com), Reuters, Fortune — search ‘Wegovy China price’ across all three to triangulate; FX via xe.com or a company’s disclosed FX assumptions.

Practical paths: ① GVR’s two reports → grandviewresearch.com, search ‘GLP-1 receptor agonist market’ (all-use) and ‘weight loss drugs market China’ (weight-loss-specific), compare each report’s ‘Report Scope/Segmentation’ for indication definitions. ② F&S data in Hengrui’s IPO prospectus → hkexnews.hk, search Hengrui-related listing documents, locate the ‘Industry Overview’ chapter’s GLP-1 market figures and F&S’s commissioned-report disclaimer. ③ L.E.K.’s market-size figure → since L.E.K. rarely publishes full reports directly, search company announcements/prospectuses/investor presentations that CITE ‘L.E.K.’+‘GLP-1’+‘China,’ or trade media (PharmCube/MedTrend) for secondary coverage of ‘L.E.K. China GLP-1 market size.’ ④ price cross-verification → search ‘Wegovy China launch price’ separately on yicai.com, reuters.com, fortune.com, compare figures and publish dates to identify the ORIGINAL source. ⑤ verify CAGRs → CAGR=(end/start)^(1/years)-1; recompute each footnote’s stated start/end values against its stated CAGR (e.g., GVR’s 13.9%, F&S’s implied ~50%).

11. 面试官深度追问 / Deep-Dive Grilling — 核心计算被追问（最重要的一页）

⚑ 这是最重要的分析页。面试官会问：为什么是这个数字？怎么算出来的？如果某个假设变了会怎样？

[CRITICAL] USD 416M 的置信区间是多少？±20%？±50%？

⚠ ATTACK "What's your confidence interval around the USD 416M? Is it ±20%? ±50%?"

EN： My three scenarios effectively define the plausible range: USD 264M to 612M — about 2.3× from conservative to optimistic. This wide range reflects genuine uncertainty in a nascent self-pay market. The key driver of width is penetration rate: moving from 0.8% to 1.2% swings output by ~50%. Informally: the base case of USD 416M is my best estimate for 2025, but I wouldn't be surprised if the true figure were anywhere from USD 200M to 700M. The conservative scenario bounds the downside (no NRDL, low physician awareness, high drop-off); the optimistic captures early NRDL signal or stronger-than-expected multi-product uptake.

中：我的三情景实际上定义了合理范围：2.64亿–6.12亿美元——保守到乐观约2.3倍。这个宽范围反映了新兴自费市场真实的不确定性。区间宽度的关键驱动是渗透率：从0.8%到1.2%使输出摆动约50%。基础情景4.16亿美元是我的最佳估计，但考虑模型假设依赖性，真实数字在2-7亿美元区间不会让我惊讶。保守情景设定下行边界（无NRDL、低医生意识、高脱落）；乐观情景捕捉早期NRDL信号或多款产品的高于预期采用。

[HIGH] CNY 16,800 年均费用——这个数字具体来自哪里？

⚠ ATTACK "CNY 16,800 annual cost — where exactly does that number come from?"

EN： Derived from Wegovy's China launch price ≈ CNY 1,400/month for the starter dose (2.4mg), reported by Yicai/Reuters at the November 2024 launch. Annualized: 1,400 × 12 = CNY 16,800. I use the starter-dose proxy because most patients remain on starter/sub-maximal doses in real-world use. Held constant across all three scenarios because pricing sensitivity is captured in the penetration assumption, not the cost parameter. I acknowledge this is a proxy — actual average annual cost would vary by dose escalation, treatment duration, product mix — but I don't have observed China average-cost data.

中：来自诺和盈中国上市价格——起始剂量(2.4mg)约1,400元/月，2024年11月上市时由一财和路透报道。年化：1,400×12=1.68万。用起始剂量代理年费用，因真实市场中大多数患者维持在起始或次最大剂量。三情景保持不变，因定价敏感性已通过渗透率假设捕捉。承认这是代理值：实际平均年费用会因剂量递增、治疗时长、产品组合变化，但我没有中国实际观测的平均年费用数据。

[HIGH] 如果实际年费用是CNY 25,000（因患者升至更高剂量），你的模型怎么变？

⚠ ATTACK "If I told you the true annual cost is CNY 25,000 because patients escalate to higher doses, how does your model change?"

EN： If annual cost is CNY 25,000 instead of CNY 16,800 (≈ 49% higher), holding patients constant at 180,600, base case moves from USD 416M to ≈ USD 620M. But I'd push back on the premise: higher per-patient cost may suppress penetration in a price-sensitive self-pay market — price and penetration aren't independent. CNY 25,000 × 1.0% vs CNY 16,800 × 1.0% is an apples-to-apples sensitivity, but in reality higher price likely means lower penetration, so the two effects partially offset.

中：若年费用从1.68万升至2.5万（约高49%），保持患者数18.06万不变，基础情景输出从4.16亿升至约6.20亿美元。但我要挑战这个前提：更高的每患者费用可能抑制渗透率，因为中国是价格敏感的自费市场——价格与渗透率不是独立的。2.5万×1.0% vs 1.68万×1.0%是同等条件比较，但现实中更高价格可能意味着更低渗透率，两个效应部分相互抵消。

Slide 11 Forecast & Drivers 预测与驱动

Overview

*Market Forecast 2025–2030 & Growth Drivers — Detailed Line-by-Line Analysis (Bilingual)*

这一页是整份报告里第一次把镜头从Slide10的“2025单点情景模型”拉长到“2025–2030的演变路径”。Slide10回答的是“2025年市场有多大、怎么算出来的”，Slide11回答的是“2025年之后，什么会让这个数字变大、变快或变慢”。这一页的核心结构是“3个宏观维度(标题) → 5张驱动卡片(右侧) → 1条时间线(左下) → 1张柱状图(底部，数据来自xlsx)”，四层内容层层递进、互相映射。本页页码显示“10”，与Slide10显示“9”一致（封面页不计入页码的惯例）。

第一部分：标题、副标题与斜体提示句 Title, Subtitle & Header Note

原文：标题“Market Forecast 2025–2030 & Growth Drivers”；副标题“China GLP-1 Growth Depends on Price, Access and Product Unlocks”；斜体提示句“Official policy and NDA milestones support the unlock story; 2025 revenue is an analyst model output, not observed market data.”

标题的两段结构 —— 从“是什么”到“为什么会变”：“Market Forecast 2025–2030”是时间窗声明，直接承接Slide10“2025 Scenario Model”——Slide10锁定了2025年这一个时点的三档情景(Conservative 264M / Base 416M / Optimistic 612M)，Slide11把镜头从“单点快照”拉长成“2025→2030的演变路径”。“& Growth Drivers”则把“为什么会变”拆解成可以逐一核查的驱动因素列表。这是一个从what到why/how的转场，逻辑上紧密衔接Slide10。

副标题“Price, Access, Product Unlocks”—— 三分类框架与右侧五卡片的映射：这三个词精确对应右侧5张驱动卡片：Price ↔ 卡片01(Biosimilar Price Erosion)；Access ↔ 卡片02(NRDL Reimbursement Scenario) + 卡片04(NHC Policy Tailwind，两者都关乎“能不能买到/能不能报销”)；Product Unlocks ↔ 卡片03(Potential Domestic Approvals) + 卡片05(Oral/Next-Gen Formulations)。也就是说，副标题的3个词是5张卡片的“降维总结”——3个宏观杠杆，对应5个具体触发事件。这是典型的“标题先给框架、正文填充细节”的金字塔结构，和Slide7标题/斜体句“两层信息”的设计手法是一致的报告风格。

“Unlocks”这个用词的选择 —— 为什么不是“Growth Factors”或“Catalysts”：“Unlock”暗含“当前市场处于被锁住、受限的状态”。这与Slide10模型里GLP-1 penetration rate仅0.8%–1.2%这一极低渗透率、以及KEY INSIGHT“China's obesity indication remains early-stage”是直接呼应的——正因为Slide10已经确立“2025年是一个渗透率不到1.2%的极早期市场”，“unlock”这个词才有叙事张力：市场目前很小，但存在5个具体机制可能把它“解锁”放大。

斜体提示句的两层信息：第一层“Official policy and NDA milestones support the unlock story”——把“unlock story”的可信度，绑定在两类已经发生、可在政府/监管网站核实的事实上：①官方政策(policy)，对应卡片04的NHC“3年体重管理行动”；②NDA里程碑，对应卡片03里Hengrui HRS9531、Hansoh olatorepatide的NDA accepted记录。两者都是Tier1来源(政府/药监公开记录)，构成了卡片标签“CONFIRMED”“STRUCTURAL”的依据。第二层“2025 revenue is an analyst model output, not observed market data”——这是Slide10 KEY INSIGHT(“USD 416M base case is an analyst obesity-only scenario output, not a third-party market-size datapoint”)在Slide11的再次重复。这次重复的位置很关键：它出现在本页最开头，而本页底部即将展示一张2025–2028E的柱状图(数据见第三部分)，柱状图第一根柱子对应的就是这个“model output”。把免责声明放在标题区、图表之前，是“先声明、后展示数字”的顺序设计，确保读者在看到具体数字之前已被提醒其性质。

为什么两层信息要用分号连接在同一句里：句子结构是“A支持B的故事；但C是模型输出，不是观测数据”。A(政策/NDA)与C(2025 revenue model)是两类性质完全不同的内容——A是“已发生的、可验证的事实”，C是“基于这些事实+分析师假设推算出的情景值”。这个句子结构本身就是Slide10“Solid facts vs Scenario levers”二分法在文字层面的预演，本页左下方的Growth Trigger Timeline随后会用“Solid facts: policy / NDA status”与“Scenario levers: price / NRDL”两个图例把这个区分可视化呈现。

为什么本页要在标题区就先做“免责声明”，而不是等到图表旁边再说：如果免责声明只放在图表脚注里，读者很可能“先被柱状图的视觉冲击吸引(看到一条向上的增长曲线)，再去读小字脚注”——这是信息呈现的常见陷阱(视觉先入为主)。把核心声明前置到标题区的斜体句里，相当于在“读者还没有看到任何数字”的阶段就先建立认知框架：【接下来你会看到一条增长曲线，但请记住它的性质】。这是一种主动管理读者预期的设计，体现了整份报告“分析假设必须先于其结论被读者看到”的一贯原则。

EN — Title, Subtitle & Note: The title's two-part structure ("Market Forecast 2025–2030" + "& Growth Drivers") moves the lens from Slide 10's single-point 2025 scenario snapshot to a 2025–2030 trajectory, then immediately decomposes "why it might change" into a checkable driver list — a what-to-why transition that connects tightly to Slide 10.

The subtitle's three words — Price, Access, Product Unlocks — map precisely onto the five driver cards on the right: Price ↔ Card 01 (Biosimilar Price Erosion); Access ↔ Card 02 (NRDL Reimbursement Scenario) + Card 04 (NHC Policy Tailwind, both about whether the drug can be bought/reimbursed); Product Unlocks ↔ Card 03 (Potential Domestic Approvals) + Card 05 (Oral/Next-Gen Formulations). The subtitle is a dimensionality-reduced summary of the five cards — three macro levers mapping to five concrete trigger events, the same pyramid structure (headline frame, then body detail) used on Slide 7.

The word "Unlocks" (rather than "Growth Factors" or "Catalysts") implies the market is currently in a locked/constrained state — directly echoing Slide 10's 0.8–1.2% GLP-1 penetration assumptions and its KEY INSIGHT that "China's obesity indication remains early-stage." Because Slide 10 already established a sub-1.2%-penetration early-stage market, "unlock" carries narrative tension: small today, but five concrete mechanisms could expand it.

The italic note has two layers. Layer 1 — "Official policy and NDA milestones support the unlock story" — ties the story's credibility to two categories of already-occurred, verifiable facts: official policy (Card 04's NHC "3-Year Weight Management Campaign") and NDA milestones (Card 03's Hengrui/Hansoh NDA acceptances), both Tier-1 government/regulator sources underpinning the "CONFIRMED"/"STRUCTURAL" tags. Layer 2 — "2025 revenue is an analyst model output, not observed market data" — repeats Slide 10's KEY INSIGHT. Its placement at the very top of this page, ahead of the bar chart shown later (whose first bar IS this model output), is a deliberate "disclose first, display numbers second" sequencing.

Why join both layers with a semicolon in one sentence: the structure is "A supports B's story; but C is model output, not observed data." A (policy/NDA) and C (the 2025 revenue model) are different in kind — A is verified fact, C is a scenario value derived from those facts plus analyst assumptions. This sentence is a textual preview of Slide 10's "Solid facts vs. Scenario levers" dichotomy, which the Growth Trigger Timeline below visualizes explicitly via its two legend entries.

Why front-load the disclaimer in the title area rather than only in the chart footnote: if the disclaimer only appeared next to the chart, a reader's first impression would be the visual impact of a rising bar chart, with the caveat read only afterward — a classic visual-primacy trap. Placing the core caveat in the title's italic note, before any numbers are shown, establishes the interpretive frame before the reader sees the chart — consistent with the report's overall principle that analyst assumptions must be disclosed before, not after, the conclusions they support.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK
标题说“Growth Depends on Price, Access and Product Unlocks”，但这三者里只有“Product Unlocks”(NDA accepted)是已发生的confirmed事实，“Price”(专利悬崖/价格侵蚀)和“Access”(NRDL)都是scenario、尚未确认的事件——如果增长“depends on”两个未确认的情景，那2026–2030的增长路径的可信度有多高？是不是整页的论证基础就是不稳的？

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER
这正是右侧5张卡片要用01–05编号、并各自标注NEAR-TERM/SCENARIO/CONFIRMED/STRUCTURAL/EMERGING不同确定性等级的原因——标题并没有声称“三者都已确定会发生”，而是说“市场未来落在Slide10哪一档情景(264/416/612M)、以及2026年之后如何演变，取决于这三个维度各自怎么走”，无论它们最终往哪个方向演变，这个“取决于”关系本身都成立。本页左下方Growth Trigger Timeline的图例里也明确写着“2025 model output; 2030 not official forecasted”——也就是说，整条2026–2030路径本身就被标注为非官方预测、非确定性陈述。可以这样回应：“这张timeline不是我们预测市场会怎样，而是市场会落在哪个情景、取决于这五件事各自的进展——它是一张情景敏感性结构图，不是一条确定的增长曲线。”

EN: This is exactly why the five cards carry numbers 01–05 with distinct confidence tags (NEAR-TERM/SCENARIO/CONFIRMED/STRUCTURAL/EMERGING). The title doesn't claim all three will happen — it claims that where the market lands within Slide 10's three scenarios (264/416/612M), and how it evolves post-2025, depends on how each of these three dimensions plays out, regardless of direction. The Growth Trigger Timeline's own legend states "2025 model output; 2030 not official forecasted" — the 2026–2030 path is itself explicitly labeled as non-official, non-deterministic. A good response: "This timeline isn't a prediction of where the market will go — it's a sensitivity map of which scenario it lands in, depending on how these five levers play out."

第二部分：底部柱状图 — China GLP-1 Obesity-Use Market Size, Conservative Penetration Scenario（与xlsx数据对照） Bottom Bar Chart, Cross-Checked Against the Excel Model

原文（图表标题与脚注）：“China GLP-1 Obesity-Use Market Size - Conservative Penetration Scenario”；脚注：“Market size = label-eligible pool × GLP-1 penetration × annualized starter-dose pricing proxy. Values are analyst model outputs, not observed sales. Pricing held constant at RMB 16.8k/year for slide consistency; price erosion is discussed separately as a downside/access driver.”

图表实际数值（提取自pptx内嵌chart1.xml，与配套Excel“China_GLP1_Obesity_Market_Size_Conservative_Projection.xlsx”中“Market Size Model”工作表第I列“Revenue / Market Size (RMB bn)”逐一核对，数字完全一致）：2022 = 0；2023 = 0.303；2024 = 0.911；2025 = 3.035；2026E = 3.937；2027E = 5.440；2028E = 7.540（单位：人民币 十亿元 / RMB bn）。Excel同时给出USD参考值（按FX=RMB/USD 7.25换算）：2025 ≈ USD 418.6M；2026E ≈ USD 543.0M；2027E ≈ USD 750.4M；2028E ≈ USD 1,040.1M。

为什么柱状图放在Slide11而不是Slide10：Slide10的核心是“2025这一个时点、三档情景(264/416/612M)的横向比较”——它是一张“某一年的三种可能性”的对比表。Slide11的柱状图则是“沿着一条固定参数路径(20%诊断率/45%可及性/渗透率1.0%→2.5%)、跨越2022–2028年的纵向演变”——它是一张“一种情景随时间变化”的趋势图。横向对比放在Slide10，纵向趋势放在Slide11(标题正是“Market Forecast 2025–2030”)，是“同一份底层模型，两种切片方式分别服务于两页不同的论点”的设计。

⚠ 核心问题：图表标题写的是“Conservative”，但2025年的数字(3.035bn RMB ≈ USD418.6M)对应的是Slide10的哪一档？对照Slide10表格：Conservative情景用diagnosis17% / eligibility42% / penetration0.8% → 2025产出USD~264M；Base Case用diagnosis20% / eligibility45% / penetration1.0% → 2025产出USD~416M；Optimistic用23%/48%/1.2% → USD~612M。本图表/Excel模型2025年使用的正是diagnosis20% / eligibility45% / penetration1.0%——这一组参数在Slide10里被标记为“Base Case”，对应USD416M，而本图表2025年的USD418.6M与之高度吻合(差异仅来自obese pool基数200.696M vs 200.7M的四舍五入)。也就是说：本图表标题里的“Conservative”，其2025年起点参数实际等于Slide10的“Base Case”，而不是Slide10自己的“Conservative”(264M)分支。

这个命名错位是怎么产生的、应该如何理解：结合Excel“Key assumption”区块的注释——“2026E/2027E/2028E penetration: 1.3% / 1.8% / 2.5%”，以及“Use this chart only as a conservative penetration scenario, not an official market forecast”——可以判断，这里“Conservative”修饰的对象是2026–2028年渗透率的“增速路径”(从1.0%每年递增0.3–0.7个百分点)，而不是“2025年的起点选择”。换句话说，模型的设计逻辑是：“以Slide10的Base Case(2025=416M)为锚点(而不是更悲观的264M为锚点)，然后对2026年之后的渗透率提升幅度采取相对保守、渐进的假设”——是“未来路径上的保守”，不是“当前基期选择上的保守”。这是一个需要在汇报中主动澄清的术语问题，否则容易被解读为“这张图的起点本应该是264M”。

建议的澄清表达（用于面试/答辩）：“这张图的‘Conservative’指的是2026–2028年渗透率爬坡速度的假设是保守的(每年仅提升0.3–0.7个百分点)，它的2025年起点沿用了Slide10的Base Case参数(416M)作为锚点，并不是Slide10自己的Conservative分支(264M)。如果要完全对齐术语，可以把图表标题改为‘Base-Case-Anchored Conservative Growth Path’，或在脚注里加一句‘2025 anchor uses Base Case parameters (20%/45%/1.0%); 2026–2028 penetration growth path is conservative’。”

柱状图时间范围(2022–2028E，共7根柱)与左侧Growth Trigger Timeline时间范围(2025–2030E，5个节点)不完全重合——这是另一处“呈现一致性”细节：图表止于2028E是因为Excel模型本身只量化到2028E；2029–2030E超出了当前模型的量化范围，因此Growth Trigger Timeline对2030E只给出定性描述(“Market expansion expected; no official obesity-only forecast”)，而不给数字。这恰好与本页底部图例“2025 model output; 2030 not official forecasted”相互印证——图表“能画到哪一年”和timeline“能给数字到哪一年”是同一个边界(2028E)，2029–2030之间的过渡没有交代，是一个可以被追问的“数据空白年份”，但本质上是模型量化范围的自然边界，不是疏漏。

“Pricing held constant at RMB 16.8k/year”与标题区“Price”驱动因素(卡片01)的呼应——这是本页内部最重要的一处“逻辑闭环”：本图表把价格固定在RMB16.8k/年(对应Slide10的Annual cost proxy USD2,300，来源为Yicai/Reuters/Fortune 2024 starter-dose pricing proxy)，意味着图表里2025→2028E的全部增长(3.035→7.540bn，约2.5倍)，100%来自渗透率上升(1.0%→2.5%，约2.5倍)，价格因素被人为隔离在外。但标题区卡片01“Biosimilar Price Erosion”恰恰预告了“2026年专利到期后价格可能下降”——如果价格真的下降，会同时发生两件事：①价格下降本身可能直接降低单位revenue；②价格下降可能进一步刺激渗透率上升(更可负担→更多患者)。这两个效应方向相反(量升价跌)，净效应不确定。本图表只展示了“量”的效应(渗透率路径)，完全没有展示“价”的效应——这正是脚注最后一句“price erosion is discussed separately as a downside/access driver”要主动声明的：这张图不是‘价格不变情景下的预测’，而是‘为了让图表可读、暂时把价格变量冻结，价格变化的影响需要叠加在这张图之外单独讨论’。

数据来源可信度评估：①Obese pool与diagnosis/eligibility/penetration参数——与Slide10共享同一组来源(NBS 2025 1%人口抽样调查、Zhang et al. 2024 PMID 39719333)，diagnosis/eligibility/penetration三个百分比均为“ANALYST ASSUMPTION”，已在Slide10标注“*”并做sensitivity-tested；②定价代理(RMB16.8k/年)——来源为Reuters 2024年11月关于诺和诺德Wegovy在华上市的报道(具体URL已在Excel“Model notes”区块列出)，属于Tier2一手报道，时间新(2024)，但是“gross list-price proxy”(标价/挂网价代理)，不是“net price”(扣除折扣/集采后的实际成交价)——如果未来集采或医院谈判带来净价下降，本图表的全部数值都会需要下修；③FX汇率7.25——属于分析师在建模时点选取的参考汇率，未标注具体取值日期，是可以进一步补强的一处来源细节(理想情况下应注明‘按某年某月某日银行间汇率’)。

EN — Bottom Bar Chart vs. Excel Model: The chart's title ("China GLP-1 Obesity-Use Market Size - Conservative Penetration Scenario") and footnote (market size = label-eligible pool × GLP-1 penetration × annualized starter-dose pricing proxy; values are model outputs, not observed sales; pricing held constant at RMB 16.8k/year, with price erosion discussed separately) frame a 2022–2028E bar series. Values extracted from the embedded chart XML match the "Revenue / Market Size (RMB bn)" column of the companion Excel "Market Size Model" sheet exactly: 2022=0, 2023=0.303, 2024=0.911, 2025=3.035, 2026E=3.937, 2027E=5.440, 2028E=7.540 (RMB bn), with USD references (FX 7.25) of roughly $418.6M, $543.0M, $750.4M and $1,040.1M for 2025–2028E.

While Slide 10 is a HORIZONTAL comparison (three 2025 scenarios side by side: 264/416/612M), Slide 11's chart is a VERTICAL trajectory (one parameter path across 2022–2028E) — the same underlying model sliced two different ways for two different arguments, matching the page title "Market Forecast 2025–2030."

Core issue: the chart is titled "Conservative," yet its 2025 value (RMB3.035bn ≈ USD418.6M) uses diagnosis 20% / eligibility 45% / penetration 1.0% — exactly Slide 10's BASE CASE parameters (→USD416M), not Slide 10's own Conservative branch (17%/42%/0.8% → USD264M). Cross-referencing the Excel's note that 2026E–2028E penetration follows 1.3%/1.8%/2.5% and the instruction to "use this chart only as a conservative penetration scenario, not an official market forecast," the word "Conservative" here describes the CONSERVATIVE GROWTH PATH for 2026–2028E penetration (a gradual +0.3–0.7pp/year increase), anchored to Slide 10's Base Case 2025 starting point — not a conservative choice of starting point itself. This naming mismatch is worth proactively clarifying in a defense: "the chart's 2025 anchor is Slide 10's Base Case (416M); 'Conservative' refers to the 2026–2028 penetration growth assumptions, not the 2025 starting scenario."

2022 = 0: The Excel labels 2022–2024 as "Actual-era model output," yet 2022 shows zero. This does not mean zero products were sold in China in 2022 — it means the model's penetration-rate input for the obesity indication was set to 0 that year (non-zero values begin in 2023 at 0.1%). A cleaner label would be "not estimated" rather than "0" to avoid implying an empirically false zero-market claim.

Chart range (2022–2028E, 7 bars) vs. Growth Trigger Timeline range (2025–2030E, 5 nodes): the chart stops at 2028E because the Excel model is only quantified through 2028E; 2029–2030E lie beyond the model's scope, which is why the timeline's 2030E node is purely qualitative ("Market expansion expected; no official obesity-only forecast") with no number — consistent with the page's legend "2025 model output; 2030 not official forecasted."

The constant-price assumption and Card 01 (Price): holding price flat at RMB16.8k/year means the entire 2025→2028E growth (≈2.5x) comes purely from penetration rising 1.0%→2.5% (also ≈2.5x) — price effects are deliberately isolated. But Card 01 ("Biosimilar Price Erosion") flags that prices may fall post-2026 patent cliff, which would simultaneously (a) lower per-unit revenue and (b) potentially raise penetration via affordability — opposing effects with an uncertain net impact. The chart shows only the volume effect; the footnote's final sentence ("price erosion is discussed separately") is the explicit acknowledgment that price effects sit outside this chart and must be layered on separately.

Source reliability: the obese-pool and diagnosis/eligibility/penetration parameters share Slide 10's Tier-1/analyst-assumption sourcing (NBS 2025 1% survey; Zhang et al. 2024). The RMB16.8k/year pricing proxy traces to a November 2024 Reuters report on Wegovy's China launch (a Tier-2 primary report, but a GROSS LIST-PRICE proxy, not a net/post-procurement price — if national procurement or hospital negotiations lower net prices, every figure in this chart would need downward revision). The FX rate of 7.25 is an analyst reference rate without a stated as-of date, a detail that could be strengthened by specifying the exact date used.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK
“你这张图标题写的是‘Conservative’，但2025年起点用的明明是Slide10里的‘Base Case’参数(416M)，不是Slide10自己的‘Conservative’(264M)——这两份材料的术语对不上，是不是说明模型本身存在不一致？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER
这是一个术语层面、而不是计算层面的问题——两份材料的底层公式和输入数据来源完全一致(都来自Slide10的model formula和NBS/Zhang et al.数据)，差异只在于‘Conservative’这个词在两处修饰的对象不同：在Slide10里，‘Conservative’修饰的是‘2025年这一个时点的三组参数组合(17%/42%/0.8%)’；在本图表/Excel里，‘Conservative’修饰的是‘2026–2028年渗透率提升速度的假设路径(每年+0.3–0.7个百分点)’，其2025年起点本身沿用了Slide10的Base Case(416M)作为锚点。我同意这是一个值得改进的命名一致性问题——更准确的标题应该是类似‘Base-Case-Anchored, Conservative Forward Growth Path’，或在脚注里加一句说明锚点参数。但这不影响数字本身的可信度，因为锚点(416M)和Slide10已审计过的Base Case完全一致，2026–2028的递增路径(1.3%/1.8%/2.5%)也在Excel里完整列出、来源可追溯。

EN: This is a terminology issue, not a calculation issue — both materials share the same formula and input sources (Slide 10's model formula plus NBS/Zhang et al. data). "Conservative" describes different things in each place: on Slide 10 it describes one of three 2025 parameter sets (17%/42%/0.8%); in this chart/Excel it describes the 2026–2028 penetration growth-rate path (+0.3–0.7pp/year), anchored at Slide 10's Base Case (416M) for 2025. I'd agree this naming should be tightened — e.g., "Base-Case-Anchored Conservative Forward Growth Path" — but it doesn't affect the reliability of the numbers themselves: the 2025 anchor matches Slide 10's audited Base Case exactly, and the 2026–2028 growth path (1.3%/1.8%/2.5%) is fully disclosed and traceable in the Excel file.

年复合增长率(CAGR)的公式是标准的：

CAGR = (期末值 / 期初值)^(1/年数) − 1

用xlsx里的Revenue数据算一下(2025→2028E，3年期)：

2025: RMB 3.035bn

2028E: RMB 7.540bn

CAGR = (7.540/3.035)^(1/3) − 1 ≈ 2.485^(0.333) − 1 ≈ 35.5%

逐年的增速（year-over-year）：

2025→2026E: 3.035→3.937，约 +29.7%

2026E→2027E: 3.937→5.440，约 +38.2%

2027E→2028E: 5.440→7.540，约 +38.6%

这个增速几乎完全由渗透率的变化驱动——因为模型里obese pool基本不变(200M左右)、价格固定(RMB16.8k/年)，唯一变化的输入就是GLP-1渗透率(1.0%→1.3%→1.8%→2.5%)。验证一下：1.3%/1.0%=1.30，1.8%/1.3%≈1.385，2.5%/1.8%≈1.389——和上面算出的年增速(29.7%/38.2%/38.6%)基本一致(细微差异来自obese pool逐年微降)。

所以如果被问"35.5%的CAGR怎么来的"，可以说："这不是一个外部引用的增长率，是用我们模型里2025和2028两年的revenue输出反推出来的几何平均增速，本质上反映的是'渗透率从1.0%涨到2.5%'这个假设路径——如果被问'为什么渗透率会这样涨'，要回到Growth Trigger Timeline的5个驱动因素去解释，而不是CAGR本身。"

要不要我把这段CAGR推导也加进文档里，作为柱状图部分的补充？

3. 面试官深度追问 / Deep-Dive Grilling — 增长预测被挑战

[HIGH] 你说NRDL是情景性的——对2026-2027年NRDL纳入的概率估计是多少？

⚠ ATTACK "You say NRDL is a scenario. What's your probability estimate for NRDL inclusion in 2026-2027?"

EN： I deliberately avoid a point probability — that implies precision I don't have. Directionally: the NHC 2024 sixteen-ministry campaign policy signal is meaningfully positive. Historical precedent — diabetes GLP-1 (Ozempic) entered NRDL negotiations — suggests the pathway exists. However, the cost-effectiveness hurdle for obesity is higher than diabetes (less acute clinically), and NHSA typically requires 50-70% price cuts for NRDL entry. Whether Novo Nordisk and domestic companies accept that is uncertain. I'd characterize it as: "possible in the 2026-2027 NRDL cycle, more likely for a domestic company than an MNC, but not base case."

中：我刻意避免给出点概率——那会暗示我没有的精确性。方向性来说：NHC 2024年16部委行动计划的政策信号是有意义的积极因素。糖尿病GLP-1（Ozempic进入NRDL谈判）的历史先例说明路径存在。但肥胖药的成本效益门槛高于糖尿病（临床急迫性较低），NHSA通常要求50-70%降价才能进NRDL。诺和诺德和国内企业能否接受这个价位不确定。我的表述："2026-2027 NRDL周期有可能，国内企业比MNC更有可能，但不是基础情景"。

[HIGH] 你的时间线显示2030年"市场扩张"但没给数字，能给我一个范围吗？

⚠ ATTACK "Your timeline shows 2030 'market expansion' but you give no number. Can you give me a range?"

EN： A scenario-based range with explicit assumptions: Scenario A — no NRDL, penetration grows to 3-5% via price competition/domestic approvals → ≈ USD 1.0-1.5B by 2030. Scenario B — NRDL achieved for ≥1 domestic product by 2027, penetration 8-12% → ≈ USD 2.5-4.0B. Scenario C — optimistic: NRDL + oral formulations + multiple domestic products, penetration 12-15% → potentially USD 5-8B. I don't present a single 2030 figure because the range is too wide and NRDL is the dominant swing factor — false precision would mislead. These scenarios are internally consistent with the bottom-up model, just run forward with different penetration assumptions.

中：可以给出情景化范围，并明确假设。情景A（无NRDL，价格竞争和国内批准推动渗透率至3-5%）：约10-15亿美元（2030年）。情景B（1个或多个国内产品2027年前实现NRDL，渗透率达8-12%）：约25-40亿美元。情景C（乐观：NRDL+口服制剂+多款国内产品，渗透率12-15%）：可能50-80亿美元。不给单一2030数字是因为范围太宽，NRDL变量是最主要的摆动因素，给出虚假精确度会产生误导。这些情景与自下而上模型逻辑内部一致——只是用不同渗透率假设向前推。

Slide 12 Competitive Landscape 竞争格局

Competitive Landscape & Player Positioning — Detailed Line-by-Line Analysis (Bilingual)
Overview

本文档逐元素拆解第12页：每句话的目的、数据来源、逻辑、可能被攻击的点和标准回答。 *This document breaks down Slide 12 element by element: purpose, data source, logic, attack points, and standard answers.*

1. 标题、副标题与斜体提示句 Title, Subtitle & Header Note

中文

原文：标题“Competitive Landscape & Player Positioning”；副标题“Competitive Landscape: Company-Level Financial Benchmarking”；斜体提示句“Company financials & strategic positioning — product approvals and pipeline details covered in Slides 7 & 8”。

为什么这一页放在Slide10/11之后：Slide10回答“2025年市场有多大”，Slide11回答“2025–2030市场会怎么变”，这两页都是“市场层面(market-level)”的分析；Slide12把镜头切换到“公司层面(company-level)”——“市场这么大、会这样变化，谁在里面竞争、各自处于什么财务位置”。这是一个从“蛋糕有多大”到“切蛋糕的人是谁、各自手里有多少刀”的转场，是市场分析报告里标准的“TAM→竞争格局”顺序。

副标题“Company-Level Financial Benchmarking”——为什么强调“Company-Level”：这个限定词非常关键，它提前为整页设了一个“范围边界”：这一页比较的是“公司整体财务状况”(总营收、整体毛利率)，不是“某个GLP-1产品的财务状况”。这个边界后面会在脚注里被反复强化(“Gross margins are company-level, not GLP-1 obesity product-level”)。

斜体提示句——“分工声明”：“product approvals and pipeline details covered in Slides 7 & 8”明确告诉读者：“如果你想看‘这家公司有哪些药、获批进度如何’，去看Slide7/8；这一页不重复那些内容，只看‘钱’。”这是一种“跨页分工(cross-slide division of labor)”的声明，避免内容冗余，也提前回应了“为什么这一页没有列产品管线细节”的潜在疑问。

这一页的标题为什么是“Competitive Landscape & Player Positioning”而不是“Company Comparison”：“Positioning”一词暗示这不只是“数字并列摆放”，而是要从数字里读出“每家公司在竞争格局中处于什么位置”——这为页面下方的KEY INSIGHT(“MNCs retain a major global revenue-scale advantage...while domestic companies show comparable or higher gross margins...”)埋下了铺垫：数字本身只是“原料”，“positioning”才是这一页真正要交付的“结论”。

EN

Original text: Title "Competitive Landscape & Player Positioning"; subtitle "Competitive Landscape: Company-Level Financial Benchmarking"; italic note "Company financials & strategic positioning — product approvals and pipeline details covered in Slides 7 & 8."

Why this page follows Slides 10/11: Slide 10 answers "how big is the 2025 market," Slide 11 answers "how will it evolve through 2030" — both are market-level analyses. Slide 12 shifts the lens to company-level: "given this market size and trajectory, who is competing in it and where does each player stand financially?" This is the standard TAM → competitive-landscape sequencing in market reports.

Why the subtitle stresses "Company-Level": This qualifier sets a critical scope boundary upfront — the comparisons on this page are of overall company financials (total revenue, overall gross margin), not of any single GLP-1 product's financials. This boundary is reinforced repeatedly in the footnote ("Gross margins are company-level, not GLP-1 obesity product-level").

The italic note as a division-of-labor statement: "product approvals and pipeline details covered in Slides 7 & 8" tells the reader explicitly: for product lists and approval timelines, go to Slides 7/8; this page focuses only on the money. This cross-slide division of labor avoids redundancy and preempts the question of why pipeline detail is absent here.

Why "Competitive Landscape & Player Positioning" rather than "Company Comparison": "Positioning" signals that the page isn't merely placing numbers side by side — it's reading those numbers for where each player sits within the competitive landscape. This sets up the page's KEY INSIGHT ("MNCs retain a major global revenue-scale advantage...while domestic companies show comparable or higher gross margins..."): the raw numbers are the material; "positioning" is the actual deliverable.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK
“你说这一页只看‘公司层面财务’，不涉及产品管线——但表格里又有一列叫‘Obesity Asset Revenue / Status Reference’，这不就是‘产品层面’的数据吗？这和‘Company-Level’的范围声明是不是矛盾？”

✓ 标准回答 / ANSWER
中文：不矛盾，但确实需要澄清这一列的“双重身份”。‘Total Revenue’和‘Overall Gross Margin’两列是严格的公司整体口径(company-level)，这是‘Company-Level Financial Benchmarking’这个副标题真正限定的对象；而‘Obesity Asset Revenue / Status Reference’这一列，是为了让读者能把‘公司整体规模’和‘其GLP-1肥胖资产目前所处的商业化阶段’放在同一行对照——它的作用更像是‘背景标注(reference)’，而不是这一页‘基准比较(benchmarking)’的主体。如果要更严谨，副标题可以写成‘Company-Level Financial Benchmarking, with Obesity-Asset Status as Context’，但考虑到列宽和可读性，现在的处理方式(把它放在表格最后一列、并在脚注里逐一注明每个数字的真实属性)是在“信息完整性”和“标题简洁性”之间的一个平衡。

EN: Not a contradiction, but the column does carry a dual role worth clarifying. "Total Revenue" and "Overall Gross Margin" are strictly company-level figures — these are what "Company-Level Financial Benchmarking" actually constrains. The "Obesity Asset Revenue / Status Reference" column instead lets the reader see, on the same row, where each company's GLP-1 obesity asset currently sits commercially — it functions more as contextual reference than as part of the benchmarking proper. A more precise subtitle might read "Company-Level Financial Benchmarking, with Obesity-Asset Status as Context," but given space constraints, placing it as the final column (with each figure's true nature spelled out in the footnote) is a reasonable balance between completeness and a concise title.

2. 表格结构 — 为什么是这6列 Table Structure — Why These 6 Columns

中文

六列：Company (Ticker) ｜ Type ｜ Total Revenue (Latest FY) ｜ Overall Gross Margin ｜ Obesity Asset Revenue / Status Reference ｜ Key Strategic Differentiator。

六列的MECE分组：可以归纳为3对“身份-能力-资产”关系：①‘Company (Ticker) + Type’回答“这是谁、属于哪一类玩家”(身份)——Ticker提供可核查的上市公司唯一标识，Type字段(MNC/Domestic)直接对应下方两个分组框(MNC INNOVATORS / DOMESTIC INNOVATORS)；②‘Total Revenue + Overall Gross Margin’回答“这家公司整体的‘体量’和‘赚钱能力’如何”(公司层面财务能力)；③‘Obesity Asset Revenue / Status Reference + Key Strategic Differentiator’回答“这家公司的GLP-1肥胖业务目前到了什么阶段、它凭什么和别人不一样”(资产层面定位)。这3对刚好对应KEY INSIGHT里被比较的两个维度——“规模(scale)”对应②，“差异化定位(differentiation)”对应③，①是分组的依据。

为什么选这5家公司、且只选5家：Novo Nordisk和Eli Lilly是Slide7/8里6款已获批产品中两家MNC的母公司(对应Wegovy/诺和盈和Zepbound/穆峰达)；Hengrui(恒瑞)和Hansoh(翰森)是Slide11卡片03里两家“NDA accepted”的国产企业(HRS9531/olatorepatide)；Innovent(信达生物)是Slide7里信尔美(Mazdutide)的开发方。也就是说，这5家公司不是“随机挑选的竞争者”，而是“前面Slide7/8/11已经逐一介绍过的具体产品/资产”的“母公司视角”——这一页是把“产品维度”(Slide7/8/11)折叠回“公司维度”，让读者从‘这个药怎么样’切换到‘这家公司怎么样’。利鲁平(华东医药)和菲塑美(仁会生物)这两家‘revenue not separately disclosed’的国产老牌企业没有出现在这一页——这是一个值得注意的‘选择性’，下文会进一步讨论。

“Type”列只有MNC/Domestic两个值——这是一个二元简化：和Slide7里讨论过的“domestic vs MNC”二元分类一样，这里的Type列把5家公司简化成两类。Innovent虽然在Slide7里被标注为“(Lilly partner)”，但在这一页的Type列里仍归类为“Domestic”——这延续了Slide7里‘domestic的判定标准是公司注册地/上市许可持有人，而不是是否存在跨国合作’这一标准。

EN

Six columns: Company (Ticker) | Type | Total Revenue (Latest FY) | Overall Gross Margin | Obesity Asset Revenue/Status Reference | Key Strategic Differentiator.

MECE grouping: Three identity–capability–positioning pairs: ① 'Company (Ticker) + Type' answers who this is and what kind of player (Ticker = a verifiable listed-company identifier; Type = MNC/Domestic, mapping directly to the two summary boxes below); ② 'Total Revenue + Overall Gross Margin' answers how large and how profitable the company is overall (company-level financial capacity); ③ 'Obesity Asset Revenue/Status Reference + Key Strategic Differentiator' answers what stage the company's GLP-1 obesity business is at and what makes it different. These three pairs map onto the KEY INSIGHT's two comparison axes — scale (②) and differentiation (③), with ① as the grouping basis.

Why these 5 companies, and only 5: Novo Nordisk and Eli Lilly are the parent companies of the two MNC products from Slides 7/8 (Wegovy and Zepbound/Mufengda); Hengrui and Hansoh are the two domestic companies from Slide 11 Card 03 with NDA-accepted assets (HRS9531/olatorepatide); Innovent is the developer of Mazdutide from Slide 7. So these aren't randomly chosen competitors — they're the parent-company view of products/assets already introduced individually on Slides 7/8/11. This page folds the product dimension back into the company dimension, shifting the reader from "how good is this drug" to "how is this company positioned." Notably, Liluping (Huadong Medicine) and Feisumei (Benemae Pharma) — the two legacy domestic firms with "revenue not separately disclosed" on Slide 7 — do NOT appear here, a selective omission discussed further below.

"Type" as a binary simplification: As with Slide 7's domestic-vs-MNC discussion, the Type column reduces 5 companies to two categories. Innovent, tagged "(Lilly partner)" on Slide 7, is still classified "Domestic" here — consistent with Slide 7's standard that domestic status is determined by company registration/MAH holder, not by the existence of cross-border partnerships.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK
“Slide7里6款获批产品对应的是6家公司(诺和诺德/礼来/信达/华东医药/仁会生物 + Sciwind)，但这一页只挑了5家、漏掉了华东医药、仁会生物和Sciwind(Ecnoglutide)——这是不是‘选择性呈现’，是不是因为它们‘revenue not separately disclosed’，数据不好看就不放进来？”

中文：
这三家被排除，理由并不完全相同，我分开说明，其中一个理由确实需要诚实承认‘和数据好不好看有关’。

华东医药——它是一家业务多元化的大型药企(医药工业、医药商业、医美等多板块)，总营收数百亿元人民币，但贝那鲁肽/利拉鲁肽类产品只是其众多业务线中的一小部分。把它的‘公司总营收/总毛利率’拿来和诺和诺德对比，反映的主要是华东医药其他业务板块的体量，对‘GLP-1赛道竞争力’这个论点没有解释力——这是一个‘指标失焦’的问题，排除是合理的。

Sciwind(先为达/Ecnoglutide)——核查后发现，先为达截至这份报告制作期仍处于港股IPO冲刺阶段(18A)，尚未正式上市，没有面向公众的、经审计的年度Total Revenue/Gross Margin报表可供引用。这是一个‘信息可得性’问题，排除理由成立。

仁会生物——这是三者中唯一一个我需要修正的：它的情况和华东医药正好相反。贝那鲁肽(谊生泰/菲塑美)是仁会生物唯一的主营业务，常年占其总营收的96%-98%以上，并不是‘被其他业务稀释’。仁会生物总营收常年只有几千万到一亿元人民币级别，且长期巨额亏损(累计亏损超6亿元)。它被排除的真实原因，不是‘数据不可得’，而是‘量级和可比性’——把一家年营收几千万、长期亏损的公司，和年营收数百亿、毛利率80%+的诺和诺德/礼来放进同一张benchmarking表，数量级相差4-5个量级，不仅不能形成有意义的对比，反而会让整张表的尺度失真。如果一定要追问‘是不是因为数字不好看才不放’，更准确的说法是：它的数字不是‘不好看’，而是‘和这一页的可比量级不在同一个数量级，放进去本身就会破坏这张表的可读性’。

需要特别强调的是：这不是为了‘掩盖国产企业的弱点’——这一页选用的国产代表(恒瑞、翰森、信达)本身都是营收数十亿至三百多亿元人民币级别的大型上市公司，仁会生物这种体量在‘国产GLP-1参与者’内部本身就是异常值(outlier)，不能代表‘国产企业在这个赛道上的真实体量’，强行把它放进来反而会误导读者对‘国产竞争力’的整体判断。

如果需要在脚注里体现，可以加一句：“Huadong Medicine and Sciwind are excluded due to lack of GLP-1-attributable or comparable audited company-level financials at time of writing; Benemae Pharma is excluded as an outlier whose company-wide revenue scale (RMB tens of millions, persistently loss-making) is not commensurate with the other companies shown.”

EN:
The three exclusions don't share a single reason, and one of them does require an honest 'yes, partly about the numbers' admission.

Huadong Medicine — a large, diversified pharma group (manufacturing, distribution, aesthetics, etc.) with total revenue in the tens of billions of RMB, of which its liraglutide-class GLP-1 product is only a small slice. Comparing its company-wide revenue/margin to Novo Nordisk's would mostly reflect the size of its OTHER business lines, not GLP-1 competitiveness — a metric-mismatch problem, and the exclusion is reasonable on that basis.

Sciwind (Ecnoglutide) — as of this report's preparation, Sciwind was still in the process of a Hong Kong 18A IPO and not yet publicly listed, with no audited, publicly available annual Total Revenue/Gross Margin figures to cite. This is a genuine data-availability issue, and the exclusion is justified.

Benemae Pharma — this is the one I need to correct, and it's the opposite situation from Huadong. Beinaglutide (its GLP-1 product) is essentially Benemae's ONLY business, consistently 96–98%+ of total revenue — not diluted by other segments. Benemae's total revenue has run in the tens of millions of RMB, with persistent large losses (cumulative losses exceeding RMB 600M). The real reason for its exclusion is not 'data unavailable' but scale and comparability: placing a company with tens-of-millions-RMB revenue and persistent losses next to Novo Nordisk/Eli Lilly (hundreds of billions in revenue, 80%+ margins) would not produce a meaningful benchmark — it would distort the table's scale. If pressed on 'was it excluded because the numbers don't look good,' the more accurate framing is: it's not that the numbers look bad, it's that they're 4–5 orders of magnitude off from everything else on this page, which would itself undermine the table's readability.

Importantly, this is not about hiding a weakness in domestic players — the domestic comparators shown (Hengrui, Hansoh, Innovent) are themselves large listed companies with revenues from several billion to over RMB 30B. Benemae is an outlier even WITHIN the set of domestic GLP-1 players, and including it would distort, not clarify, the reader's picture of domestic competitiveness.

A footnote addition could read: "Huadong Medicine and Sciwind are excluded due to lack of GLP-1-attributable or comparable audited company-level financials at time of writing; Benemae Pharma is excluded as an outlier whose company-wide revenue scale (RMB tens of millions, persistently loss-making) is not commensurate with the other companies shown."

3. 第一行：Novo Nordisk — 来源核验 Row 1: Novo Nordisk — Source Verification

中文

原文：Novo Nordisk (NYSE: NVO / CPH: NOVO B) │ MNC │ Total Revenue: DKK 309.1B (~USD 46.7B, FY2025) │ Overall Gross Margin: ~81% (FY2025) │ Obesity Asset Revenue: USD 12.0B (Wegovy FY2025) │ Key Strategic Differentiator: First-mover obesity franchise; SELECT CV outcomes evidence; global manufacturing scale。

“DKK 309.1B”的可信度核查：经检索Novo Nordisk 2025年报(annualreport.novonordisk.com)，原文明确披露“Sales increased by 6% measured in Danish kroner...to DKK 309,064 million in 2025”——即DKK309.1B，与本行数字完全一致(精确到小数点后一位)。这是Tier1来源(公司年报，经审计的财务数字)，可信度最高。

Ticker标注“NYSE: NVO / CPH: NOVO B”——为什么列两个交易所代码：Novo Nordisk是双重上市公司(哥本哈根证券交易所主要上市CPH:NOVO B，纽交所以ADR形式NYSE:NVO)。列出两个代码，是为了让不同背景的读者(国际投资者熟悉NVO，欧洲/丹麦背景读者熟悉NOVO B)都能直接核对。这也间接传达了“这是一家全球性大型上市公司”的信息，呼应Type列的“MNC”标签。

“~81% (FY2025)”毛利率——为什么用“~”和区间式表达：毛利率(gross margin)通常按“(收入-销售成本)/收入”计算，公司年报里可能给出“gross margin”或需要从“cost of goods sold”反推。“~81%”的“~”符号是诚实标注“这是一个近似值/分析师计算值”，而不是逐字照抄年报某一句话——这与全篇“分析师假设标*、近似值标~”的标注惯例一致。

“USD 12.0B (Wegovy FY2025)”与Slide7数字的一致性：Slide7第①行写的是“Wegovy FY2025: DKK79.1B (~USD12B) [Novo Nordisk 2025 AR]”，这一行的“USD12.0B”与之完全一致——这是“同一个数字在两页之间保持一致”的跨页核查，体现了报告内部的一致性。但需要注意：根据检索到的Novo Nordisk 2025年报原文，“Sales of Wegovy increased by 11% measured in Danish kroner...to DKK 51,015 million”这一数字(看起来更像是某一报告期的Wegovy销售额，需要进一步核实其统计区间是全年累计还是单季度)与“DKK79.1B”之间存在差异，需要在后续版本中用年报“Note”章节里‘按产品线披露的全年Wegovy销售额’这一项做最终核对，确保‘79.1B/12B’这个数字的统计口径(全年累计 vs 某一季度累计)被准确标注。

“First-mover obesity franchise; SELECT CV outcomes evidence; global manufacturing scale”——三个差异化点的来源与含义：“First-mover”指Novo Nordisk的司美格鲁肽(Wegovy)是全球最早大规模商业化的现代GLP-1减肥药(2021年FDA批准)；“SELECT CV outcomes evidence”指SELECT心血管结局试验(发表于NEJM，证实Wegovy可降低心血管事件风险)，这是Tier1的同行评审证据，也是Novo Nordisk区别于“仅有体重数据”竞品的核心卖点；“global manufacturing scale”指其在丹麦、美国、法国等地的大规模产能投资，这是2023-2024年全球“供不应求”局面下的关键竞争优势。三点分别对应“先发优势(时间)、临床证据(科学)、产能(供给)”三个不同维度，不是同质化的重复。

EN

Original text: Novo Nordisk (NYSE: NVO / CPH: NOVO B) | MNC | Total Revenue: DKK309.1B (~USD46.7B, FY2025) | Overall Gross Margin: ~81% (FY2025) | Obesity Asset Revenue: USD12.0B (Wegovy FY2025) | Key Strategic Differentiator: First-mover obesity franchise; SELECT CV outcomes evidence; global manufacturing scale.

Verifying "DKK309.1B": Novo Nordisk's 2025 Annual Report (annualreport.novonordisk.com) states sales increased to DKK309,064 million in 2025 — i.e., DKK309.1B, matching this row exactly to one decimal. This is a Tier-1, audited-financials source — the highest reliability tier.

Why two tickers ("NYSE: NVO / CPH: NOVO B"): Novo Nordisk is dual-listed (primary listing CPH: NOVO B on Nasdaq Copenhagen; ADR NYSE: NVO). Listing both lets readers from different backgrounds (international investors know NVO; European/Danish readers know NOVO B) verify directly — and signals "this is a large global MNC," reinforcing the Type="MNC" tag.

The "~81% (FY2025)" gross margin — why approximate notation: Gross margin is typically (revenue − cost of goods sold)/revenue, often requiring derivation from annual-report line items rather than a single quoted figure. The "~" honestly flags this as an approximate/analyst-derived figure, consistent with the report's convention of marking analyst assumptions with "*" and approximations with "~".

Consistency of "USD12.0B (Wegovy FY2025)" with Slide 7: Slide 7 Row ① states "Wegovy FY2025: DKK79.1B (~USD12B) [Novo Nordisk 2025 AR]" — identical to this row's USD12.0B, a useful cross-slide consistency check. However, the retrieved 2025 Annual Report text shows "Sales of Wegovy increased by 11%...to DKK51,015 million," a figure that appears to correspond to a specific reporting period for Wegovy and differs from "DKK79.1B" — this should be reconciled in a future revision against the Annual Report's product-line revenue note, confirming whether "79.1B/12B" reflects full-year cumulative sales or a different period, and labeling the basis explicitly.

The three differentiators: "First-mover obesity franchise" refers to Wegovy being the first modern GLP-1 obesity drug commercialized at scale (FDA-approved 2021); "SELECT CV outcomes evidence" refers to the SELECT cardiovascular outcomes trial (published in NEJM, showing Wegovy reduces CV event risk) — Tier-1 peer-reviewed evidence and a key differentiator versus weight-only competitors; "global manufacturing scale" refers to large capacity investments (Denmark, US, France) — critical given 2023–2024 supply shortages. The three points span time (first-mover), science (clinical evidence), and supply (manufacturing) — non-redundant dimensions.

⚠ 攻击点 / ATTACK
